00189     // Compare two strings
00190     PUGI__FN bool strequal(const char_t* src, const char_t* dst)
00191     {
00192         assert(src && dst);
00193 
00194     #ifdef PUGIXML_WCHAR_MODE
00195         return wcscmp(src, dst) == 0;
00196     #else
00197         return strcmp(src, dst) == 0;
00198     #endif
00199     }
00200 
00201     // Compare lhs with [rhs_begin, rhs_end)
00202     PUGI__FN bool strequalrange(const char_t* lhs, const char_t* rhs, size_t count)
00203     {
00204         for (size_t i = 0; i < count; ++i)
00205             if (lhs[i] != rhs[i])
00206                 return false;
00207     
00208         return lhs[count] == 0;
00209     }

00211     // Get length of wide string, even if CRT lacks wide character support
00212     PUGI__FN size_t strlength_wide(const wchar_t* s)

00215

00217         return wcslen(s);
00218     #else
00219         const wchar_t* end = s;
00220         while (*end) end++;
00221         return static_cast<size_t>(end - s);
00222     #endif

00263     static const size_t xml_memory_page_size =
00264     #ifdef PUGIXML_MEMORY_PAGE_SIZE
00265         PUGIXML_MEMORY_PAGE_SIZE

00271     static const uintptr_t xml_memory_page_alignment = 64;
00272     static const uintptr_t xml_memory_page_pointer_mask = ~(xml_memory_page_alignment - 1);
00273     static const uintptr_t xml_memory_page_contents_shared_mask = 32;
00274     static const uintptr_t xml_memory_page_name_allocated_mask = 16;
00275     static const uintptr_t xml_memory_page_value_allocated_mask = 8;
00276     static const uintptr_t xml_memory_page_type_mask = 7;

00278     static const uintptr_t xml_memory_page_value_allocated_or_shared_mask = xml_memory_page_value_allocated_mask | xml_memory_page_contents_shared_mask;

00284     struct xml_memory_page
00285     {
00286         static xml_memory_page* construct(void* memory)
00287         {
00288             xml_memory_page* result = static_cast<xml_memory_page*>(memory);
00289 
00290             result->allocator = 0;
00291             result->prev = 0;
00292             result->next = 0;
00293             result->busy_size = 0;
00294             result->freed_size = 0;
00295 
00296             return result;
00297         }
00298 
00299         xml_allocator* allocator;
00300 
00301         xml_memory_page* prev;
00302         xml_memory_page* next;
00303 
00304         size_t busy_size;
00305         size_t freed_size;
00306     };

00308     struct xml_memory_string_header
00309     {
00310         uint16_t page_offset; // offset from page->data
00311         uint16_t full_size; // 0 if string occupies whole page
00312     };
00313 
00314     struct xml_allocator
00315     {
00316         xml_allocator(xml_memory_page* root): _root(root), _busy_size(root->busy_size)
00317         {
00318         }
00319 
00320         xml_memory_page* allocate_page(size_t data_size)
00321         {
00322             size_t size = sizeof(xml_memory_page) + data_size;
00323 
00324             // allocate block with some alignment, leaving memory for worst-case padding
00325             void* memory = xml_memory::allocate(size + xml_memory_page_alignment);
00326             if (!memory) return 0;
00327 
00328             // align to next page boundary (note: this guarantees at least 1 usable byte before the page)
00329             char* page_memory = reinterpret_cast<char*>((reinterpret_cast<uintptr_t>(memory) + xml_memory_page_alignment) & ~(xml_memory_page_alignment - 1));
00330 
00331             // prepare page structure
00332             xml_memory_page* page = xml_memory_page::construct(page_memory);
00333             assert(page);
00334 
00335             page->allocator = _root->allocator;
00336 
00337             // record the offset for freeing the memory block
00338             assert(page_memory > memory && page_memory - static_cast<char*>(memory) <= 127);
00339             page_memory[-1] = static_cast<char>(page_memory - static_cast<char*>(memory));
00340 
00341             return page;
00342         }
00343 
00344         static void deallocate_page(xml_memory_page* page)
00345         {
00346             char* page_memory = reinterpret_cast<char*>(page);
00347 
00348             xml_memory::deallocate(page_memory - page_memory[-1]);
00349         }
00350 
00351         void* allocate_memory_oob(size_t size, xml_memory_page*& out_page);
00352 
00353         void* allocate_memory(size_t size, xml_memory_page*& out_page)
00354         {
00355             if (_busy_size + size > xml_memory_page_size) return allocate_memory_oob(size, out_page);
00356 
00357             void* buf = reinterpret_cast<char*>(_root) + sizeof(xml_memory_page) + _busy_size;
00358 
00359             _busy_size += size;
00360 
00361             out_page = _root;
00362 
00363             return buf;
00364         }
00365 
00366         void deallocate_memory(void* ptr, size_t size, xml_memory_page* page)
00367         {
00368             if (page == _root) page->busy_size = _busy_size;
00369 
00370             assert(ptr >= reinterpret_cast<char*>(page) + sizeof(xml_memory_page) && ptr < reinterpret_cast<char*>(page) + sizeof(xml_memory_page) + page->busy_size);
00371             (void)!ptr;
00372 
00373             page->freed_size += size;
00374             assert(page->freed_size <= page->busy_size);
00375 
00376             if (page->freed_size == page->busy_size)
00377             {
00378                 if (page->next == 0)
00379                 {
00380                     assert(_root == page);
00381 
00382                     // top page freed, just reset sizes
00383                     page->busy_size = page->freed_size = 0;
00384                     _busy_size = 0;
00385                 }
00386                 else
00387                 {
00388                     assert(_root != page);
00389                     assert(page->prev);
00390 
00391                     // remove from the list
00392                     page->prev->next = page->next;
00393                     page->next->prev = page->prev;
00394 
00395                     // deallocate
00396                     deallocate_page(page);
00397                 }
00398             }
00399         }
00400 
00401         char_t* allocate_string(size_t length)
00402         {
00403             static const size_t max_encoded_offset = (1 << 16) * sizeof(void*);
00404 
00405             PUGI__STATIC_ASSERT(xml_memory_page_size <= max_encoded_offset);
00406 
00407             // allocate memory for string and header block
00408             size_t size = sizeof(xml_memory_string_header) + length * sizeof(char_t);
00409             
00410             // round size up to pointer alignment boundary
00411             size_t full_size = (size + (sizeof(void*) - 1)) & ~(sizeof(void*) - 1);
00412 
00413             xml_memory_page* page;
00414             xml_memory_string_header* header = static_cast<xml_memory_string_header*>(allocate_memory(full_size, page));
00415 
00416             if (!header) return 0;
00417 
00418             // setup header
00419             ptrdiff_t page_offset = reinterpret_cast<char*>(header) - reinterpret_cast<char*>(page) - sizeof(xml_memory_page);
00420 
00421             assert(page_offset % sizeof(void*) == 0);
00422             assert(page_offset >= 0 && static_cast<size_t>(page_offset) < max_encoded_offset);
00423             header->page_offset = static_cast<uint16_t>(static_cast<size_t>(page_offset) / sizeof(void*));
00424 
00425             // full_size == 0 for large strings that occupy the whole page
00426             assert(full_size % sizeof(void*) == 0);
00427             assert(full_size < max_encoded_offset || (page->busy_size == full_size && page_offset == 0));
00428             header->full_size = static_cast<uint16_t>(full_size < max_encoded_offset ? full_size / sizeof(void*) : 0);
00429 
00430             // round-trip through void* to avoid 'cast increases required alignment of target type' warning
00431             // header is guaranteed a pointer-sized alignment, which should be enough for char_t
00432             return static_cast<char_t*>(static_cast<void*>(header + 1));
00433         }
00434 
00435         void deallocate_string(char_t* string)
00436         {
00437             // this function casts pointers through void* to avoid 'cast increases required alignment of target type' warnings
00438             // we're guaranteed the proper (pointer-sized) alignment on the input string if it was allocated via allocate_string
00439 
00440             // get header
00441             xml_memory_string_header* header = static_cast<xml_memory_string_header*>(static_cast<void*>(string)) - 1;
00442             assert(header);
00443 
00444             // deallocate
00445             size_t page_offset = sizeof(xml_memory_page) + header->page_offset * sizeof(void*);
00446             xml_memory_page* page = reinterpret_cast<xml_memory_page*>(static_cast<void*>(reinterpret_cast<char*>(header) - page_offset));
00447 
00448             // if full_size == 0 then this string occupies the whole page
00449             size_t full_size = header->full_size == 0 ? page->busy_size : header->full_size * sizeof(void*);
00450 
00451             deallocate_memory(header, full_size, page);
00452         }
00453 
00454         xml_memory_page* _root;
00455         size_t _busy_size;
00456     };
00457 
00458     PUGI__FN_NO_INLINE void* xml_allocator::allocate_memory_oob(size_t size, xml_memory_page*& out_page)
00459     {
00460         const size_t large_allocation_threshold = xml_memory_page_size / 4;
00461 
00462         xml_memory_page* page = allocate_page(size <= large_allocation_threshold ? xml_memory_page_size : size);
00463         out_page = page;
00464 
00465         if (!page) return 0;
00466 
00467         if (size <= large_allocation_threshold)
00468         {
00469             _root->busy_size = _busy_size;
00470 
00471             // insert page at the end of linked list
00472             page->prev = _root;
00473             _root->next = page;
00474             _root = page;
00475 
00476             _busy_size = size;
00477         }
00478         else
00479         {
00480             // insert page before the end of linked list, so that it is deleted as soon as possible
00481             // the last page is not deleted even if it's empty (see deallocate_memory)
00482             assert(_root->prev);
00483 
00484             page->prev = _root->prev;
00485             page->next = _root;
00486 
00487             _root->prev->next = page;
00488             _root->prev = page;
00489         }
00490 
00491         // allocate inside page
00492         page->busy_size = size;
00493 
00494         return reinterpret_cast<char*>(page) + sizeof(xml_memory_page);
00495     }
00496 PUGI__NS_END

00593     inline void destroy_attribute(xml_attribute_struct* a, xml_allocator& alloc)
00594     {
00595         uintptr_t header = a->header;
00596 
00597         if (header & impl::xml_memory_page_name_allocated_mask) alloc.deallocate_string(a->name);
00598         if (header & impl::xml_memory_page_value_allocated_mask) alloc.deallocate_string(a->value);
00599 
00600         alloc.deallocate_memory(a, sizeof(xml_attribute_struct), reinterpret_cast<xml_memory_page*>(header & xml_memory_page_pointer_mask));
00601     }
00602 
00603     inline void destroy_node(xml_node_struct* n, xml_allocator& alloc)
00604     {
00605         uintptr_t header = n->header;
00606 
00607         if (header & impl::xml_memory_page_name_allocated_mask) alloc.deallocate_string(n->name);
00608         if (header & impl::xml_memory_page_value_allocated_mask) alloc.deallocate_string(n->value);
00609 
00610         for (xml_attribute_struct* attr = n->first_attribute; attr; )
00611         {
00612             xml_attribute_struct* next = attr->next_attribute;
00613 
00614             destroy_attribute(attr, alloc);
00615 
00616             attr = next;
00617         }
00618 
00619         for (xml_node_struct* child = n->first_child; child; )
00620         {
00621             xml_node_struct* next = child->next_sibling;
00622 
00623             destroy_node(child, alloc);
00624 
00625             child = next;
00626         }
00627 
00628         alloc.deallocate_memory(n, sizeof(xml_node_struct), reinterpret_cast<xml_memory_page*>(header & xml_memory_page_pointer_mask));
00629     }
00630 
00631     inline void append_node(xml_node_struct* child, xml_node_struct* node)
00632     {
00633         child->parent = node;
00634 
00635         xml_node_struct* head = node->first_child;
00636 
00637         if (head)
00638         {
00639             xml_node_struct* tail = head->prev_sibling_c;
00640 
00641             tail->next_sibling = child;
00642             child->prev_sibling_c = tail;
00643             head->prev_sibling_c = child;
00644         }
00645         else
00646         {
00647             node->first_child = child;
00648             child->prev_sibling_c = child;
00649         }
00650     }
00651 
00652     inline void prepend_node(xml_node_struct* child, xml_node_struct* node)
00653     {
00654         child->parent = node;
00655 
00656         xml_node_struct* head = node->first_child;
00657 
00658         if (head)
00659         {
00660             child->prev_sibling_c = head->prev_sibling_c;
00661             head->prev_sibling_c = child;
00662         }
00663         else
00664             child->prev_sibling_c = child;
00665 
00666         child->next_sibling = head;
00667         node->first_child = child;
00668     }
00669 
00670     inline void insert_node_after(xml_node_struct* child, xml_node_struct* node)
00671     {
00672         xml_node_struct* parent = node->parent;
00673 
00674         child->parent = parent;
00675 
00676         if (node->next_sibling)
00677             node->next_sibling->prev_sibling_c = child;
00678         else
00679             parent->first_child->prev_sibling_c = child;
00680 
00681         child->next_sibling = node->next_sibling;
00682         child->prev_sibling_c = node;
00683 
00684         node->next_sibling = child;
00685     }
00686 
00687     inline void insert_node_before(xml_node_struct* child, xml_node_struct* node)
00688     {
00689         xml_node_struct* parent = node->parent;
00690 
00691         child->parent = parent;
00692 
00693         if (node->prev_sibling_c->next_sibling)
00694             node->prev_sibling_c->next_sibling = child;
00695         else
00696             parent->first_child = child;
00697 
00698         child->prev_sibling_c = node->prev_sibling_c;
00699         child->next_sibling = node;
00700 
00701         node->prev_sibling_c = child;
00702     }
00703 
00704     inline void remove_node(xml_node_struct* node)
00705     {
00706         xml_node_struct* parent = node->parent;
00707 
00708         if (node->next_sibling)
00709             node->next_sibling->prev_sibling_c = node->prev_sibling_c;
00710         else
00711             parent->first_child->prev_sibling_c = node->prev_sibling_c;
00712 
00713         if (node->prev_sibling_c->next_sibling)
00714             node->prev_sibling_c->next_sibling = node->next_sibling;
00715         else
00716             parent->first_child = node->next_sibling;
00717 
00718         node->parent = 0;
00719         node->prev_sibling_c = 0;
00720         node->next_sibling = 0;
00721     }
00722 
00723     inline void append_attribute(xml_attribute_struct* attr, xml_node_struct* node)
00724     {
00725         xml_attribute_struct* head = node->first_attribute;
00726 
00727         if (head)
00728         {
00729             xml_attribute_struct* tail = head->prev_attribute_c;
00730 
00731             tail->next_attribute = attr;
00732             attr->prev_attribute_c = tail;
00733             head->prev_attribute_c = attr;
00734         }
00735         else
00736         {
00737             node->first_attribute = attr;
00738             attr->prev_attribute_c = attr;
00739         }
00740     }
00741 
00742     inline void prepend_attribute(xml_attribute_struct* attr, xml_node_struct* node)
00743     {
00744         xml_attribute_struct* head = node->first_attribute;
00745 
00746         if (head)
00747         {
00748             attr->prev_attribute_c = head->prev_attribute_c;
00749             head->prev_attribute_c = attr;
00750         }
00751         else
00752             attr->prev_attribute_c = attr;
00753 
00754         attr->next_attribute = head;
00755         node->first_attribute = attr;
00756     }
00757 
00758     inline void insert_attribute_after(xml_attribute_struct* attr, xml_attribute_struct* place, xml_node_struct* node)
00759     {
00760         if (place->next_attribute)
00761             place->next_attribute->prev_attribute_c = attr;
00762         else
00763             node->first_attribute->prev_attribute_c = attr;
00764 
00765         attr->next_attribute = place->next_attribute;
00766         attr->prev_attribute_c = place;
00767         place->next_attribute = attr;
00768     }
00769 
00770     inline void insert_attribute_before(xml_attribute_struct* attr, xml_attribute_struct* place, xml_node_struct* node)
00771     {
00772         if (place->prev_attribute_c->next_attribute)
00773             place->prev_attribute_c->next_attribute = attr;
00774         else
00775             node->first_attribute = attr;
00776 
00777         attr->prev_attribute_c = place->prev_attribute_c;
00778         attr->next_attribute = place;
00779         place->prev_attribute_c = attr;
00780     }
00781 
00782     inline void remove_attribute(xml_attribute_struct* attr, xml_node_struct* node)
00783     {
00784         if (attr->next_attribute)
00785             attr->next_attribute->prev_attribute_c = attr->prev_attribute_c;
00786         else
00787             node->first_attribute->prev_attribute_c = attr->prev_attribute_c;
00788 
00789         if (attr->prev_attribute_c->next_attribute)
00790             attr->prev_attribute_c->next_attribute = attr->next_attribute;
00791         else
00792             node->first_attribute = attr->next_attribute;
00793 
00794         attr->prev_attribute_c = 0;
00795         attr->next_attribute = 0;
00796     }
00797 
00798     PUGI__FN_NO_INLINE xml_node_struct* append_new_node(xml_node_struct* node, xml_allocator& alloc, xml_node_type type = node_element)
00799     {
00800         xml_node_struct* child = allocate_node(alloc, type);
00801         if (!child) return 0;
00802 
00803         append_node(child, node);
00804 
00805         return child;
00806     }
00807 
00808     PUGI__FN_NO_INLINE xml_attribute_struct* append_new_attribute(xml_node_struct* node, xml_allocator& alloc)
00809     {
00810         xml_attribute_struct* attr = allocate_attribute(alloc);
00811         if (!attr) return 0;
00812 
00813         append_attribute(attr, node);
00814 
00815         return attr;
00816     }

00832 // Unicode utilities
00833 PUGI__NS_BEGIN
00834     inline uint16_t endian_swap(uint16_t value)
00835     {
00836         return static_cast<uint16_t>(((value & 0xff) << 8) | (value >> 8));
00837     }
00838 
00839     inline uint32_t endian_swap(uint32_t value)
00840     {
00841         return ((value & 0xff) << 24) | ((value & 0xff00) << 8) | ((value & 0xff0000) >> 8) | (value >> 24);
00842     }
00843 
00844     struct utf8_counter
00845     {
00846         typedef size_t value_type;
00847 
00848         static value_type low(value_type result, uint32_t ch)
00849         {
00850             // U+0000..U+007F
00851             if (ch < 0x80) return result + 1;
00852             // U+0080..U+07FF
00853             else if (ch < 0x800) return result + 2;
00854             // U+0800..U+FFFF
00855             else return result + 3;
00856         }
00857 
00858         static value_type high(value_type result, uint32_t)
00859         {
00860             // U+10000..U+10FFFF
00861             return result + 4;
00862         }
00863     };
00864 
00865     struct utf8_writer
00866     {
00867         typedef uint8_t* value_type;
00868 
00869         static value_type low(value_type result, uint32_t ch)
00870         {
00871             // U+0000..U+007F
00872             if (ch < 0x80)
00873             {
00874                 *result = static_cast<uint8_t>(ch);
00875                 return result + 1;
00876             }
00877             // U+0080..U+07FF
00878             else if (ch < 0x800)
00879             {
00880                 result[0] = static_cast<uint8_t>(0xC0 | (ch >> 6));
00881                 result[1] = static_cast<uint8_t>(0x80 | (ch & 0x3F));
00882                 return result + 2;
00883             }
00884             // U+0800..U+FFFF
00885             else
00886             {
00887                 result[0] = static_cast<uint8_t>(0xE0 | (ch >> 12));
00888                 result[1] = static_cast<uint8_t>(0x80 | ((ch >> 6) & 0x3F));
00889                 result[2] = static_cast<uint8_t>(0x80 | (ch & 0x3F));
00890                 return result + 3;
00891             }
00892         }
00893 
00894         static value_type high(value_type result, uint32_t ch)
00895         {
00896             // U+10000..U+10FFFF
00897             result[0] = static_cast<uint8_t>(0xF0 | (ch >> 18));
00898             result[1] = static_cast<uint8_t>(0x80 | ((ch >> 12) & 0x3F));
00899             result[2] = static_cast<uint8_t>(0x80 | ((ch >> 6) & 0x3F));
00900             result[3] = static_cast<uint8_t>(0x80 | (ch & 0x3F));
00901             return result + 4;
00902         }
00903 
00904         static value_type any(value_type result, uint32_t ch)
00905         {
00906             return (ch < 0x10000) ? low(result, ch) : high(result, ch);
00907         }
00908     };
00909 
00910     struct utf16_counter
00911     {
00912         typedef size_t value_type;
00913 
00914         static value_type low(value_type result, uint32_t)
00915         {
00916             return result + 1;
00917         }
00918 
00919         static value_type high(value_type result, uint32_t)
00920         {
00921             return result + 2;
00922         }
00923     };
00924 
00925     struct utf16_writer
00926     {
00927         typedef uint16_t* value_type;
00928 
00929         static value_type low(value_type result, uint32_t ch)
00930         {
00931             *result = static_cast<uint16_t>(ch);
00932 
00933             return result + 1;
00934         }
00935 
00936         static value_type high(value_type result, uint32_t ch)
00937         {
00938             uint32_t msh = static_cast<uint32_t>(ch - 0x10000) >> 10;
00939             uint32_t lsh = static_cast<uint32_t>(ch - 0x10000) & 0x3ff;
00940 
00941             result[0] = static_cast<uint16_t>(0xD800 + msh);
00942             result[1] = static_cast<uint16_t>(0xDC00 + lsh);
00943 
00944             return result + 2;
00945         }
00946 
00947         static value_type any(value_type result, uint32_t ch)
00948         {
00949             return (ch < 0x10000) ? low(result, ch) : high(result, ch);
00950         }
00951     };
00952

00958         {
00959             return result + 1;
00960         }
00961 
00962         static value_type high(value_type result, uint32_t)
00963         {
00964             return result + 1;
00965         }

00974             *result = ch;
00975 
00976             return result + 1;

00981             *result = ch;
00982

00990             return result + 1;

00994     struct latin1_writer
00995     {
00996         typedef uint8_t* value_type;
00997 
00998         static value_type low(value_type result, uint32_t ch)
00999         {
01000             *result = static_cast<uint8_t>(ch > 255 ? '?' : ch);
01001 
01002             return result + 1;
01003         }
01004 
01005         static value_type high(value_type result, uint32_t ch)
01006         {
01007             (void)ch;
01008 
01009             *result = '?';
01010 
01011             return result + 1;
01012         }
01013     };

01021         typedef utf16_writer writer;
01022     };

01033 
01034     template <typename Traits, typename opt_swap = opt_false> struct utf_decoder
01035     {
01036         static inline typename Traits::value_type decode_utf8_block(const uint8_t* data, size_t size, typename Traits::value_type result)
01037         {
01038             const uint8_t utf8_byte_mask = 0x3f;
01039 
01040             while (size)
01041             {
01042                 uint8_t lead = *data;
01043 
01044                 // 0xxxxxxx -> U+0000..U+007F
01045                 if (lead < 0x80)
01046                 {
01047                     result = Traits::low(result, lead);
01048                     data += 1;
01049                     size -= 1;
01050 
01051                     // process aligned single-byte (ascii) blocks
01052                     if ((reinterpret_cast<uintptr_t>(data) & 3) == 0)
01053                     {
01054                         // round-trip through void* to silence 'cast increases required alignment of target type' warnings
01055                         while (size >= 4 && (*static_cast<const uint32_t*>(static_cast<const void*>(data)) & 0x80808080) == 0)
01056                         {
01057                             result = Traits::low(result, data[0]);
01058                             result = Traits::low(result, data[1]);
01059                             result = Traits::low(result, data[2]);
01060                             result = Traits::low(result, data[3]);
01061                             data += 4;
01062                             size -= 4;
01063                         }
01064                     }
01065                 }
01066                 // 110xxxxx -> U+0080..U+07FF
01067                 else if (static_cast<unsigned int>(lead - 0xC0) < 0x20 && size >= 2 && (data[1] & 0xc0) == 0x80)
01068                 {
01069                     result = Traits::low(result, ((lead & ~0xC0) << 6) | (data[1] & utf8_byte_mask));
01070                     data += 2;
01071                     size -= 2;
01072                 }
01073                 // 1110xxxx -> U+0800-U+FFFF
01074                 else if (static_cast<unsigned int>(lead - 0xE0) < 0x10 && size >= 3 && (data[1] & 0xc0) == 0x80 && (data[2] & 0xc0) == 0x80)
01075                 {
01076                     result = Traits::low(result, ((lead & ~0xE0) << 12) | ((data[1] & utf8_byte_mask) << 6) | (data[2] & utf8_byte_mask));
01077                     data += 3;
01078                     size -= 3;
01079                 }
01080                 // 11110xxx -> U+10000..U+10FFFF
01081                 else if (static_cast<unsigned int>(lead - 0xF0) < 0x08 && size >= 4 && (data[1] & 0xc0) == 0x80 && (data[2] & 0xc0) == 0x80 && (data[3] & 0xc0) == 0x80)
01082                 {
01083                     result = Traits::high(result, ((lead & ~0xF0) << 18) | ((data[1] & utf8_byte_mask) << 12) | ((data[2] & utf8_byte_mask) << 6) | (data[3] & utf8_byte_mask));
01084                     data += 4;
01085                     size -= 4;
01086                 }
01087                 // 10xxxxxx or 11111xxx -> invalid
01088                 else
01089                 {
01090                     data += 1;
01091                     size -= 1;
01092                 }
01093             }
01094 
01095             return result;
01096         }
01097 
01098         static inline typename Traits::value_type decode_utf16_block(const uint16_t* data, size_t size, typename Traits::value_type result)
01099         {
01100             const uint16_t* end = data + size;
01101 
01102             while (data < end)
01103             {
01104                 unsigned int lead = opt_swap::value ? endian_swap(*data) : *data;
01105 
01106                 // U+0000..U+D7FF
01107                 if (lead < 0xD800)
01108                 {
01109                     result = Traits::low(result, lead);
01110                     data += 1;
01111                 }
01112                 // U+E000..U+FFFF
01113                 else if (static_cast<unsigned int>(lead - 0xE000) < 0x2000)
01114                 {
01115                     result = Traits::low(result, lead);
01116                     data += 1;
01117                 }
01118                 // surrogate pair lead
01119                 else if (static_cast<unsigned int>(lead - 0xD800) < 0x400 && data + 1 < end)
01120                 {
01121                     uint16_t next = opt_swap::value ? endian_swap(data[1]) : data[1];
01122 
01123                     if (static_cast<unsigned int>(next - 0xDC00) < 0x400)
01124                     {
01125                         result = Traits::high(result, 0x10000 + ((lead & 0x3ff) << 10) + (next & 0x3ff));
01126                         data += 2;
01127                     }
01128                     else
01129                     {
01130                         data += 1;
01131                     }
01132                 }
01133                 else
01134                 {
01135                     data += 1;
01136                 }
01137             }
01138 
01139             return result;
01140         }
01141 
01142         static inline typename Traits::value_type decode_utf32_block(const uint32_t* data, size_t size, typename Traits::value_type result)
01143         {
01144             const uint32_t* end = data + size;
01145 
01146             while (data < end)
01147             {
01148                 uint32_t lead = opt_swap::value ? endian_swap(*data) : *data;
01149 
01150                 // U+0000..U+FFFF
01151                 if (lead < 0x10000)
01152                 {
01153                     result = Traits::low(result, lead);
01154                     data += 1;
01155                 }
01156                 // U+10000..U+10FFFF
01157                 else
01158                 {
01159                     result = Traits::high(result, lead);
01160                     data += 1;
01161                 }
01162             }
01163 
01164             return result;
01165         }
01166 
01167         static inline typename Traits::value_type decode_latin1_block(const uint8_t* data, size_t size, typename Traits::value_type result)
01168         {
01169             for (size_t i = 0; i < size; ++i)
01170             {
01171                 result = Traits::low(result, data[i]);
01172             }
01173 
01174             return result;
01175         }
01176 
01177         static inline typename Traits::value_type decode_wchar_block_impl(const uint16_t* data, size_t size, typename Traits::value_type result)
01178         {
01179             return decode_utf16_block(data, size, result);
01180         }
01181 
01182         static inline typename Traits::value_type decode_wchar_block_impl(const uint32_t* data, size_t size, typename Traits::value_type result)
01183         {
01184             return decode_utf32_block(data, size, result);
01185         }
01186 
01187         static inline typename Traits::value_type decode_wchar_block(const wchar_t* data, size_t size, typename Traits::value_type result)
01188         {
01189             return decode_wchar_block_impl(reinterpret_cast<const wchar_selector<sizeof(wchar_t)>::type*>(data), size, result);
01190         }
01191     };
01192 
01193     template <typename T> PUGI__FN void convert_utf_endian_swap(T* result, const T* data, size_t length)
01194     {
01195         for (size_t i = 0; i < length; ++i) result[i] = endian_swap(data[i]);
01196     }
01197 
01198 #ifdef PUGIXML_WCHAR_MODE
01199     PUGI__FN void convert_wchar_endian_swap(wchar_t* result, const wchar_t* data, size_t length)
01200     {
01201         for (size_t i = 0; i < length; ++i) result[i] = static_cast<wchar_t>(endian_swap(static_cast<wchar_selector<sizeof(wchar_t)>::type>(data[i])));
01202     }
01203 #endif
01204 PUGI__NS_END

01250     {
01251         3,  3,  3,  3,  3,  3,  3,  3,     3,  0,  2,  3,  3,  2,  3,  3,     // 0-15
01252         3,  3,  3,  3,  3,  3,  3,  3,     3,  3,  3,  3,  3,  3,  3,  3,     // 16-31
01253         0,  0,  2,  0,  0,  0,  3,  0,     0,  0,  0,  0,  0, 16, 16,  0,     // 32-47
01254         24, 24, 24, 24, 24, 24, 24, 24,    24, 24, 0,  0,  3,  0,  3,  0,     // 48-63
01255 
01256         0,  20, 20, 20, 20, 20, 20, 20,    20, 20, 20, 20, 20, 20, 20, 20,    // 64-79
01257         20, 20, 20, 20, 20, 20, 20, 20,    20, 20, 20, 0,  0,  0,  0,  20,    // 80-95
01258         0,  20, 20, 20, 20, 20, 20, 20,    20, 20, 20, 20, 20, 20, 20, 20,    // 96-111
01259         20, 20, 20, 20, 20, 20, 20, 20,    20, 20, 20, 0,  0,  0,  0,  0,     // 112-127
01260 
01261         20, 20, 20, 20, 20, 20, 20, 20,    20, 20, 20, 20, 20, 20, 20, 20,    // 128+
01262         20, 20, 20, 20, 20, 20, 20, 20,    20, 20, 20, 20, 20, 20, 20, 20,
01263         20, 20, 20, 20, 20, 20, 20, 20,    20, 20, 20, 20, 20, 20, 20, 20,
01264         20, 20, 20, 20, 20, 20, 20, 20,    20, 20, 20, 20, 20, 20, 20, 20,
01265         20, 20, 20, 20, 20, 20, 20, 20,    20, 20, 20, 20, 20, 20, 20, 20,
01266         20, 20, 20, 20, 20, 20, 20, 20,    20, 20, 20, 20, 20, 20, 20, 20,
01267         20, 20, 20, 20, 20, 20, 20, 20,    20, 20, 20, 20, 20, 20, 20, 20,
01268         20, 20, 20, 20, 20, 20, 20, 20,    20, 20, 20, 20, 20, 20, 20, 20
01269     };
01270     
01271 #ifdef PUGIXML_WCHAR_MODE
01272     #define PUGI__IS_CHARTYPE_IMPL(c, ct, table) ((static_cast<unsigned int>(c) < 128 ? table[static_cast<unsigned int>(c)] : table[128]) & (ct))
01273 #else
01274     #define PUGI__IS_CHARTYPE_IMPL(c, ct, table) (table[static_cast<unsigned char>(c)] & (ct))
01275 #endif
01276 
01277     #define PUGI__IS_CHARTYPE(c, ct) PUGI__IS_CHARTYPE_IMPL(c, ct, chartype_table)
01278     #define PUGI__IS_CHARTYPEX(c, ct) PUGI__IS_CHARTYPE_IMPL(c, ct, chartypex_table)
01279 
01280     PUGI__FN bool is_little_endian()
01281     {
01282         unsigned int ui = 1;
01283 
01284         return *reinterpret_cast<unsigned char*>(&ui) == 1;
01285     }
01286 
01287     PUGI__FN xml_encoding get_wchar_encoding()
01288     {
01289         PUGI__STATIC_ASSERT(sizeof(wchar_t) == 2 || sizeof(wchar_t) == 4);
01290 
01291         if (sizeof(wchar_t) == 2)
01292             return is_little_endian() ? encoding_utf16_le : encoding_utf16_be;
01293         else 
01294             return is_little_endian() ? encoding_utf32_le : encoding_utf32_be;
01295     }
01296 
01297     PUGI__FN xml_encoding guess_buffer_encoding(uint8_t d0, uint8_t d1, uint8_t d2, uint8_t d3)
01298     {
01299         // look for BOM in first few bytes
01300         if (d0 == 0 && d1 == 0 && d2 == 0xfe && d3 == 0xff) return encoding_utf32_be;
01301         if (d0 == 0xff && d1 == 0xfe && d2 == 0 && d3 == 0) return encoding_utf32_le;
01302         if (d0 == 0xfe && d1 == 0xff) return encoding_utf16_be;
01303         if (d0 == 0xff && d1 == 0xfe) return encoding_utf16_le;
01304         if (d0 == 0xef && d1 == 0xbb && d2 == 0xbf) return encoding_utf8;
01305 
01306         // look for <, <? or <?xm in various encodings
01307         if (d0 == 0 && d1 == 0 && d2 == 0 && d3 == 0x3c) return encoding_utf32_be;
01308         if (d0 == 0x3c && d1 == 0 && d2 == 0 && d3 == 0) return encoding_utf32_le;
01309         if (d0 == 0 && d1 == 0x3c && d2 == 0 && d3 == 0x3f) return encoding_utf16_be;
01310         if (d0 == 0x3c && d1 == 0 && d2 == 0x3f && d3 == 0) return encoding_utf16_le;
01311         if (d0 == 0x3c && d1 == 0x3f && d2 == 0x78 && d3 == 0x6d) return encoding_utf8;
01312 
01313         // look for utf16 < followed by node name (this may fail, but is better than utf8 since it's zero terminated so early)
01314         if (d0 == 0 && d1 == 0x3c) return encoding_utf16_be;
01315         if (d0 == 0x3c && d1 == 0) return encoding_utf16_le;
01316 
01317         // no known BOM detected, assume utf8
01318         return encoding_utf8;
01319     }
01320 
01321     PUGI__FN xml_encoding get_buffer_encoding(xml_encoding encoding, const void* contents, size_t size)
01322     {
01323         // replace wchar encoding with utf implementation
01324         if (encoding == encoding_wchar) return get_wchar_encoding();
01325 
01326         // replace utf16 encoding with utf16 with specific endianness
01327         if (encoding == encoding_utf16) return is_little_endian() ? encoding_utf16_le : encoding_utf16_be;
01328 
01329         // replace utf32 encoding with utf32 with specific endianness
01330         if (encoding == encoding_utf32) return is_little_endian() ? encoding_utf32_le : encoding_utf32_be;
01331 
01332         // only do autodetection if no explicit encoding is requested
01333         if (encoding != encoding_auto) return encoding;
01334 
01335         // skip encoding autodetection if input buffer is too small
01336         if (size < 4) return encoding_utf8;
01337 
01338         // try to guess encoding (based on XML specification, Appendix F.1)
01339         const uint8_t* data = static_cast<const uint8_t*>(contents);
01340 
01341         PUGI__DMC_VOLATILE uint8_t d0 = data[0], d1 = data[1], d2 = data[2], d3 = data[3];
01342 
01343         return guess_buffer_encoding(d0, d1, d2, d3);
01344     }
01345 
01346     PUGI__FN bool get_mutable_buffer(char_t*& out_buffer, size_t& out_length, const void* contents, size_t size, bool is_mutable)
01347     {
01348         size_t length = size / sizeof(char_t);
01349 
01350         if (is_mutable)
01351         {
01352             out_buffer = static_cast<char_t*>(const_cast<void*>(contents));
01353             out_length = length;
01354         }
01355         else
01356         {
01357             char_t* buffer = static_cast<char_t*>(xml_memory::allocate((length + 1) * sizeof(char_t)));
01358             if (!buffer) return false;
01359 
01360             if (contents)
01361                 memcpy(buffer, contents, length * sizeof(char_t));
01362             else
01363                 assert(length == 0);
01364 
01365             buffer[length] = 0;
01366 
01367             out_buffer = buffer;
01368             out_length = length + 1;
01369         }
01370 
01371         return true;
01372     }
01373 
01374 #ifdef PUGIXML_WCHAR_MODE
01375     PUGI__FN bool need_endian_swap_utf(xml_encoding le, xml_encoding re)
01376     {
01377         return (le == encoding_utf16_be && re == encoding_utf16_le) || (le == encoding_utf16_le && re == encoding_utf16_be) ||
01378                (le == encoding_utf32_be && re == encoding_utf32_le) || (le == encoding_utf32_le && re == encoding_utf32_be);
01379     }
01380 
01381     PUGI__FN bool convert_buffer_endian_swap(char_t*& out_buffer, size_t& out_length, const void* contents, size_t size, bool is_mutable)
01382     {
01383         const char_t* data = static_cast<const char_t*>(contents);
01384         size_t length = size / sizeof(char_t);
01385 
01386         if (is_mutable)
01387         {
01388             char_t* buffer = const_cast<char_t*>(data);
01389 
01390             convert_wchar_endian_swap(buffer, data, length);
01391 
01392             out_buffer = buffer;
01393             out_length = length;
01394         }
01395         else
01396         {
01397             char_t* buffer = static_cast<char_t*>(xml_memory::allocate((length + 1) * sizeof(char_t)));
01398             if (!buffer) return false;
01399 
01400             convert_wchar_endian_swap(buffer, data, length);
01401             buffer[length] = 0;
01402 
01403             out_buffer = buffer;
01404             out_length = length + 1;
01405         }
01406 
01407         return true;
01408     }
01409 
01410     PUGI__FN bool convert_buffer_utf8(char_t*& out_buffer, size_t& out_length, const void* contents, size_t size)
01411     {
01412         const uint8_t* data = static_cast<const uint8_t*>(contents);
01413         size_t data_length = size;
01414 
01415         // first pass: get length in wchar_t units
01416         size_t length = utf_decoder<wchar_counter>::decode_utf8_block(data, data_length, 0);
01417 
01418         // allocate buffer of suitable length
01419         char_t* buffer = static_cast<char_t*>(xml_memory::allocate((length + 1) * sizeof(char_t)));
01420         if (!buffer) return false;
01421 
01422         // second pass: convert utf8 input to wchar_t
01423         wchar_writer::value_type obegin = reinterpret_cast<wchar_writer::value_type>(buffer);
01424         wchar_writer::value_type oend = utf_decoder<wchar_writer>::decode_utf8_block(data, data_length, obegin);
01425 
01426         assert(oend == obegin + length);
01427         *oend = 0;
01428 
01429         out_buffer = buffer;
01430         out_length = length + 1;
01431 
01432         return true;
01433     }
01434 
01435     template <typename opt_swap> PUGI__FN bool convert_buffer_utf16(char_t*& out_buffer, size_t& out_length, const void* contents, size_t size, opt_swap)
01436     {
01437         const uint16_t* data = static_cast<const uint16_t*>(contents);
01438         size_t data_length = size / sizeof(uint16_t);
01439 
01440         // first pass: get length in wchar_t units
01441         size_t length = utf_decoder<wchar_counter, opt_swap>::decode_utf16_block(data, data_length, 0);
01442 
01443         // allocate buffer of suitable length
01444         char_t* buffer = static_cast<char_t*>(xml_memory::allocate((length + 1) * sizeof(char_t)));
01445         if (!buffer) return false;
01446 
01447         // second pass: convert utf16 input to wchar_t
01448         wchar_writer::value_type obegin = reinterpret_cast<wchar_writer::value_type>(buffer);
01449         wchar_writer::value_type oend = utf_decoder<wchar_writer, opt_swap>::decode_utf16_block(data, data_length, obegin);
01450 
01451         assert(oend == obegin + length);
01452         *oend = 0;
01453 
01454         out_buffer = buffer;
01455         out_length = length + 1;
01456 
01457         return true;
01458     }

01485     PUGI__FN bool convert_buffer_latin1(char_t*& out_buffer, size_t& out_length, const void* contents, size_t size)

01498         wchar_writer::value_type obegin = reinterpret_cast<wchar_writer::value_type>(buffer);

01500

01509 
01510     PUGI__FN bool convert_buffer(char_t*& out_buffer, size_t& out_length, xml_encoding encoding, const void* contents, size_t size, bool is_mutable)
01511     {
01512         // get native encoding
01513         xml_encoding wchar_encoding = get_wchar_encoding();
01514 
01515         // fast path: no conversion required
01516         if (encoding == wchar_encoding) return get_mutable_buffer(out_buffer, out_length, contents, size, is_mutable);
01517 
01518         // only endian-swapping is required
01519         if (need_endian_swap_utf(encoding, wchar_encoding)) return convert_buffer_endian_swap(out_buffer, out_length, contents, size, is_mutable);
01520 
01521         // source encoding is utf8
01522         if (encoding == encoding_utf8) return convert_buffer_utf8(out_buffer, out_length, contents, size);
01523 
01524         // source encoding is utf16
01525         if (encoding == encoding_utf16_be || encoding == encoding_utf16_le)
01526         {
01527             xml_encoding native_encoding = is_little_endian() ? encoding_utf16_le : encoding_utf16_be;
01528 
01529             return (native_encoding == encoding) ?
01530                 convert_buffer_utf16(out_buffer, out_length, contents, size, opt_false()) :
01531                 convert_buffer_utf16(out_buffer, out_length, contents, size, opt_true());
01532         }
01533 
01534         // source encoding is utf32
01535         if (encoding == encoding_utf32_be || encoding == encoding_utf32_le)
01536         {
01537             xml_encoding native_encoding = is_little_endian() ? encoding_utf32_le : encoding_utf32_be;
01538 
01539             return (native_encoding == encoding) ?
01540                 convert_buffer_utf32(out_buffer, out_length, contents, size, opt_false()) :
01541                 convert_buffer_utf32(out_buffer, out_length, contents, size, opt_true());
01542         }
01543 
01544         // source encoding is latin1
01545         if (encoding == encoding_latin1) return convert_buffer_latin1(out_buffer, out_length, contents, size);
01546 
01547         assert(!"Invalid encoding");
01548         return false;
01549     }
01550 #else
01551     template <typename opt_swap> PUGI__FN bool convert_buffer_utf16(char_t*& out_buffer, size_t& out_length, const void* contents, size_t size, opt_swap)
01552     {
01553         const uint16_t* data = static_cast<const uint16_t*>(contents);
01554         size_t data_length = size / sizeof(uint16_t);
01555 
01556         // first pass: get length in utf8 units
01557         size_t length = utf_decoder<utf8_counter, opt_swap>::decode_utf16_block(data, data_length, 0);
01558 
01559         // allocate buffer of suitable length
01560         char_t* buffer = static_cast<char_t*>(xml_memory::allocate((length + 1) * sizeof(char_t)));
01561         if (!buffer) return false;
01562 
01563         // second pass: convert utf16 input to utf8
01564         uint8_t* obegin = reinterpret_cast<uint8_t*>(buffer);
01565         uint8_t* oend = utf_decoder<utf8_writer, opt_swap>::decode_utf16_block(data, data_length, obegin);
01566 
01567         assert(oend == obegin + length);
01568         *oend = 0;
01569 
01570         out_buffer = buffer;
01571         out_length = length + 1;
01572 
01573         return true;
01574     }
01575 
01576     template <typename opt_swap> PUGI__FN bool convert_buffer_utf32(char_t*& out_buffer, size_t& out_length, const void* contents, size_t size, opt_swap)
01577     {
01578         const uint32_t* data = static_cast<const uint32_t*>(contents);
01579         size_t data_length = size / sizeof(uint32_t);
01580 
01581         // first pass: get length in utf8 units
01582         size_t length = utf_decoder<utf8_counter, opt_swap>::decode_utf32_block(data, data_length, 0);
01583 
01584         // allocate buffer of suitable length
01585         char_t* buffer = static_cast<char_t*>(xml_memory::allocate((length + 1) * sizeof(char_t)));
01586         if (!buffer) return false;
01587 
01588         // second pass: convert utf32 input to utf8
01589         uint8_t* obegin = reinterpret_cast<uint8_t*>(buffer);
01590         uint8_t* oend = utf_decoder<utf8_writer, opt_swap>::decode_utf32_block(data, data_length, obegin);
01591 
01592         assert(oend == obegin + length);
01593         *oend = 0;
01594 
01595         out_buffer = buffer;
01596         out_length = length + 1;
01597 
01598         return true;
01599     }

01601     PUGI__FN size_t get_latin1_7bit_prefix_length(const uint8_t* data, size_t size)
01602     {
01603         for (size_t i = 0; i < size; ++i)
01604             if (data[i] > 127)
01605                 return i;
01606 
01607         return size;
01608     }
01609 
01610     PUGI__FN bool convert_buffer_latin1(char_t*& out_buffer, size_t& out_length, const void* contents, size_t size, bool is_mutable)
01611     {
01612         const uint8_t* data = static_cast<const uint8_t*>(contents);
01613         size_t data_length = size;
01614 
01615         // get size of prefix that does not need utf8 conversion
01616         size_t prefix_length = get_latin1_7bit_prefix_length(data, data_length);
01617         assert(prefix_length <= data_length);
01618 
01619         const uint8_t* postfix = data + prefix_length;
01620         size_t postfix_length = data_length - prefix_length;
01621 
01622         // if no conversion is needed, just return the original buffer
01623         if (postfix_length == 0) return get_mutable_buffer(out_buffer, out_length, contents, size, is_mutable);
01624 
01625         // first pass: get length in utf8 units
01626         size_t length = prefix_length + utf_decoder<utf8_counter>::decode_latin1_block(postfix, postfix_length, 0);
01627 
01628         // allocate buffer of suitable length
01629         char_t* buffer = static_cast<char_t*>(xml_memory::allocate((length + 1) * sizeof(char_t)));
01630         if (!buffer) return false;
01631 
01632         // second pass: convert latin1 input to utf8
01633         memcpy(buffer, data, prefix_length);
01634 
01635         uint8_t* obegin = reinterpret_cast<uint8_t*>(buffer);
01636         uint8_t* oend = utf_decoder<utf8_writer>::decode_latin1_block(postfix, postfix_length, obegin + prefix_length);
01637 
01638         assert(oend == obegin + length);
01639         *oend = 0;
01640 
01641         out_buffer = buffer;
01642         out_length = length + 1;
01643 
01644         return true;
01645     }
01646 
01647     PUGI__FN bool convert_buffer(char_t*& out_buffer, size_t& out_length, xml_encoding encoding, const void* contents, size_t size, bool is_mutable)
01648     {
01649         // fast path: no conversion required
01650         if (encoding == encoding_utf8) return get_mutable_buffer(out_buffer, out_length, contents, size, is_mutable);
01651 
01652         // source encoding is utf16
01653         if (encoding == encoding_utf16_be || encoding == encoding_utf16_le)
01654         {
01655             xml_encoding native_encoding = is_little_endian() ? encoding_utf16_le : encoding_utf16_be;
01656 
01657             return (native_encoding == encoding) ?
01658                 convert_buffer_utf16(out_buffer, out_length, contents, size, opt_false()) :
01659                 convert_buffer_utf16(out_buffer, out_length, contents, size, opt_true());
01660         }
01661 
01662         // source encoding is utf32
01663         if (encoding == encoding_utf32_be || encoding == encoding_utf32_le)
01664         {
01665             xml_encoding native_encoding = is_little_endian() ? encoding_utf32_le : encoding_utf32_be;
01666 
01667             return (native_encoding == encoding) ?
01668                 convert_buffer_utf32(out_buffer, out_length, contents, size, opt_false()) :
01669                 convert_buffer_utf32(out_buffer, out_length, contents, size, opt_true());
01670         }
01671 
01672         // source encoding is latin1
01673         if (encoding == encoding_latin1) return convert_buffer_latin1(out_buffer, out_length, contents, size, is_mutable);
01674 
01675         assert(!"Invalid encoding");
01676         return false;
01677     }
01678 #endif
01679 
01680     PUGI__FN size_t as_utf8_begin(const wchar_t* str, size_t length)
01681     {
01682         // get length in utf8 characters
01683         return utf_decoder<utf8_counter>::decode_wchar_block(str, length, 0);
01684     }
01685 
01686     PUGI__FN void as_utf8_end(char* buffer, size_t size, const wchar_t* str, size_t length)
01687     {
01688         // convert to utf8
01689         uint8_t* begin = reinterpret_cast<uint8_t*>(buffer);
01690         uint8_t* end = utf_decoder<utf8_writer>::decode_wchar_block(str, length, begin);
01691     
01692         assert(begin + size == end);
01693         (void)!end;
01694 
01695         // zero-terminate
01696         buffer[size] = 0;
01697     }
01698     
01699 #ifndef PUGIXML_NO_STL
01700     PUGI__FN std::string as_utf8_impl(const wchar_t* str, size_t length)
01701     {
01702         // first pass: get length in utf8 characters
01703         size_t size = as_utf8_begin(str, length);
01704 
01705         // allocate resulting string
01706         std::string result;
01707         result.resize(size);
01708 
01709         // second pass: convert to utf8
01710         if (size > 0) as_utf8_end(&result[0], size, str, length);
01711 
01712         return result;
01713     }
01714 
01715     PUGI__FN std::basic_string<wchar_t> as_wide_impl(const char* str, size_t size)
01716     {
01717         const uint8_t* data = reinterpret_cast<const uint8_t*>(str);
01718 
01719         // first pass: get length in wchar_t units
01720         size_t length = utf_decoder<wchar_counter>::decode_utf8_block(data, size, 0);
01721 
01722         // allocate resulting string
01723         std::basic_string<wchar_t> result;
01724         result.resize(length);
01725 
01726         // second pass: convert to wchar_t
01727         if (length > 0)
01728         {
01729             wchar_writer::value_type begin = reinterpret_cast<wchar_writer::value_type>(&result[0]);
01730             wchar_writer::value_type end = utf_decoder<wchar_writer>::decode_utf8_block(data, size, begin);
01731 
01732             assert(begin + length == end);
01733             (void)!end;
01734         }
01735 
01736         return result;
01737     }
01738 #endif
01739 
01740     inline bool strcpy_insitu_allow(size_t length, uintptr_t header, uintptr_t header_mask, char_t* target)
01741     {
01742         // never reuse shared memory
01743         if (header & xml_memory_page_contents_shared_mask) return false;
01744 
01745         size_t target_length = strlength(target);
01746 
01747         // always reuse document buffer memory if possible
01748         if ((header & header_mask) == 0) return target_length >= length;
01749 
01750         // reuse heap memory if waste is not too great
01751         const size_t reuse_threshold = 32;
01752 
01753         return target_length >= length && (target_length < reuse_threshold || target_length - length < target_length / 2);
01754     }
01755 
01756     PUGI__FN bool strcpy_insitu(char_t*& dest, uintptr_t& header, uintptr_t header_mask, const char_t* source)
01757     {
01758         assert(header);
01759 
01760         size_t source_length = strlength(source);
01761 
01762         if (source_length == 0)
01763         {
01764             // empty string and null pointer are equivalent, so just deallocate old memory
01765             xml_allocator* alloc = reinterpret_cast<xml_memory_page*>(header & xml_memory_page_pointer_mask)->allocator;
01766 
01767             if (header & header_mask) alloc->deallocate_string(dest);
01768             
01769             // mark the string as not allocated
01770             dest = 0;
01771             header &= ~header_mask;
01772 
01773             return true;
01774         }
01775         else if (dest && strcpy_insitu_allow(source_length, header, header_mask, dest))
01776         {
01777             // we can reuse old buffer, so just copy the new data (including zero terminator)
01778             memcpy(dest, source, (source_length + 1) * sizeof(char_t));
01779             
01780             return true;
01781         }
01782         else
01783         {
01784             xml_allocator* alloc = reinterpret_cast<xml_memory_page*>(header & xml_memory_page_pointer_mask)->allocator;
01785 
01786             // allocate new buffer
01787             char_t* buf = alloc->allocate_string(source_length + 1);
01788             if (!buf) return false;
01789 
01790             // copy the string (including zero terminator)
01791             memcpy(buf, source, (source_length + 1) * sizeof(char_t));
01792 
01793             // deallocate old buffer (*after* the above to protect against overlapping memory and/or allocation failures)
01794             if (header & header_mask) alloc->deallocate_string(dest);
01795             
01796             // the string is now allocated, so set the flag
01797             dest = buf;
01798             header |= header_mask;
01799 
01800             return true;
01801         }
01802     }
01803 
01804     struct gap
01805     {
01806         char_t* end;
01807         size_t size;
01808             
01809         gap(): end(0), size(0)
01810         {
01811         }
01812             
01813         // Push new gap, move s count bytes further (skipping the gap).
01814         // Collapse previous gap.
01815         void push(char_t*& s, size_t count)
01816         {
01817             if (end) // there was a gap already; collapse it
01818             {
01819                 // Move [old_gap_end, new_gap_start) to [old_gap_start, ...)
01820                 assert(s >= end);
01821                 memmove(end - size, end, reinterpret_cast<char*>(s) - reinterpret_cast<char*>(end));
01822             }
01823                 
01824             s += count; // end of current gap
01825                 
01826             // "merge" two gaps
01827             end = s;
01828             size += count;
01829         }
01830             
01831         // Collapse all gaps, return past-the-end pointer
01832         char_t* flush(char_t* s)
01833         {
01834             if (end)
01835             {
01836                 // Move [old_gap_end, current_pos) to [old_gap_start, ...)
01837                 assert(s >= end);
01838                 memmove(end - size, end, reinterpret_cast<char*>(s) - reinterpret_cast<char*>(end));
01839 
01840                 return s - size;
01841             }
01842             else return s;
01843         }
01844     };
01845     
01846     PUGI__FN char_t* strconv_escape(char_t* s, gap& g)
01847     {
01848         char_t* stre = s + 1;
01849 
01850         switch (*stre)
01851         {
01852             case '#':   // &#...
01853             {
01854                 unsigned int ucsc = 0;
01855 
01856                 if (stre[1] == 'x') // &#x... (hex code)
01857                 {
01858                     stre += 2;
01859 
01860                     char_t ch = *stre;
01861 
01862                     if (ch == ';') return stre;
01863 
01864                     for (;;)
01865                     {
01866                         if (static_cast<unsigned int>(ch - '0') <= 9)
01867                             ucsc = 16 * ucsc + (ch - '0');
01868                         else if (static_cast<unsigned int>((ch | ' ') - 'a') <= 5)
01869                             ucsc = 16 * ucsc + ((ch | ' ') - 'a' + 10);
01870                         else if (ch == ';')
01871                             break;
01872                         else // cancel
01873                             return stre;
01874 
01875                         ch = *++stre;
01876                     }
01877                     
01878                     ++stre;
01879                 }
01880                 else    // &#... (dec code)
01881                 {
01882                     char_t ch = *++stre;
01883 
01884                     if (ch == ';') return stre;
01885 
01886                     for (;;)
01887                     {
01888                         if (static_cast<unsigned int>(static_cast<unsigned int>(ch) - '0') <= 9)
01889                             ucsc = 10 * ucsc + (ch - '0');
01890                         else if (ch == ';')
01891                             break;
01892                         else // cancel
01893                             return stre;
01894 
01895                         ch = *++stre;
01896                     }
01897                     
01898                     ++stre;
01899                 }
01900 
01901             #ifdef PUGIXML_WCHAR_MODE
01902                 s = reinterpret_cast<char_t*>(wchar_writer::any(reinterpret_cast<wchar_writer::value_type>(s), ucsc));
01903             #else
01904                 s = reinterpret_cast<char_t*>(utf8_writer::any(reinterpret_cast<uint8_t*>(s), ucsc));
01905             #endif
01906                     
01907                 g.push(s, stre - s);
01908                 return stre;
01909             }
01910 
01911             case 'a':   // &a
01912             {
01913                 ++stre;
01914 
01915                 if (*stre == 'm') // &am
01916                 {
01917                     if (*++stre == 'p' && *++stre == ';') // &amp;
01918                     {
01919                         *s++ = '&';
01920                         ++stre;
01921                             
01922                         g.push(s, stre - s);
01923                         return stre;
01924                     }
01925                 }
01926                 else if (*stre == 'p') // &ap
01927                 {
01928                     if (*++stre == 'o' && *++stre == 's' && *++stre == ';') // &apos;
01929                     {
01930                         *s++ = '\'';
01931                         ++stre;
01932 
01933                         g.push(s, stre - s);
01934                         return stre;
01935                     }
01936                 }
01937                 break;
01938             }
01939 
01940             case 'g': // &g
01941             {
01942                 if (*++stre == 't' && *++stre == ';') // &gt;
01943                 {
01944                     *s++ = '>';
01945                     ++stre;
01946                     
01947                     g.push(s, stre - s);
01948                     return stre;
01949                 }
01950                 break;
01951             }
01952 
01953             case 'l': // &l
01954             {
01955                 if (*++stre == 't' && *++stre == ';') // &lt;
01956                 {
01957                     *s++ = '<';
01958                     ++stre;
01959                         
01960                     g.push(s, stre - s);
01961                     return stre;
01962                 }
01963                 break;
01964             }
01965 
01966             case 'q': // &q
01967             {
01968                 if (*++stre == 'u' && *++stre == 'o' && *++stre == 't' && *++stre == ';') // &quot;
01969                 {
01970                     *s++ = '"';
01971                     ++stre;
01972                     
01973                     g.push(s, stre - s);
01974                     return stre;
01975                 }
01976                 break;
01977             }
01978 
01979             default:
01980                 break;
01981         }
01982         
01983         return stre;
01984     }
01985 
01986     // Parser utilities
01987     #define PUGI__ENDSWITH(c, e)        ((c) == (e) || ((c) == 0 && endch == (e)))
01988     #define PUGI__SKIPWS()              { while (PUGI__IS_CHARTYPE(*s, ct_space)) ++s; }
01989     #define PUGI__OPTSET(OPT)           ( optmsk & (OPT) )
01990     #define PUGI__PUSHNODE(TYPE)        { cursor = append_new_node(cursor, alloc, TYPE); if (!cursor) PUGI__THROW_ERROR(status_out_of_memory, s); }
01991     #define PUGI__POPNODE()             { cursor = cursor->parent; }
01992     #define PUGI__SCANFOR(X)            { while (*s != 0 && !(X)) ++s; }
01993     #define PUGI__SCANWHILE(X)          { while (X) ++s; }
01994     #define PUGI__SCANWHILE_UNROLL(X)   { for (;;) { char_t ss = s[0]; if (PUGI__UNLIKELY(!(X))) { break; } ss = s[1]; if (PUGI__UNLIKELY(!(X))) { s += 1; break; } ss = s[2]; if (PUGI__UNLIKELY(!(X))) { s += 2; break; } ss = s[3]; if (PUGI__UNLIKELY(!(X))) { s += 3; break; } s += 4; } }
01995     #define PUGI__ENDSEG()              { ch = *s; *s = 0; ++s; }
01996     #define PUGI__THROW_ERROR(err, m)   return error_offset = m, error_status = err, static_cast<char_t*>(0)
01997     #define PUGI__CHECK_ERROR(err, m)   { if (*s == 0) PUGI__THROW_ERROR(err, m); }
01998 
01999     PUGI__FN char_t* strconv_comment(char_t* s, char_t endch)
02000     {
02001         gap g;
02002         
02003         while (true)
02004         {
02005             PUGI__SCANWHILE_UNROLL(!PUGI__IS_CHARTYPE(ss, ct_parse_comment));
02006         
02007             if (*s == '\r') // Either a single 0x0d or 0x0d 0x0a pair
02008             {
02009                 *s++ = '\n'; // replace first one with 0x0a
02010                 
02011                 if (*s == '\n') g.push(s, 1);
02012             }
02013             else if (s[0] == '-' && s[1] == '-' && PUGI__ENDSWITH(s[2], '>')) // comment ends here
02014             {
02015                 *g.flush(s) = 0;
02016                 
02017                 return s + (s[2] == '>' ? 3 : 2);
02018             }
02019             else if (*s == 0)
02020             {
02021                 return 0;
02022             }
02023             else ++s;
02024         }
02025     }
02026 
02027     PUGI__FN char_t* strconv_cdata(char_t* s, char_t endch)
02028     {
02029         gap g;
02030             
02031         while (true)
02032         {
02033             PUGI__SCANWHILE_UNROLL(!PUGI__IS_CHARTYPE(ss, ct_parse_cdata));
02034             
02035             if (*s == '\r') // Either a single 0x0d or 0x0d 0x0a pair
02036             {
02037                 *s++ = '\n'; // replace first one with 0x0a
02038                 
02039                 if (*s == '\n') g.push(s, 1);
02040             }
02041             else if (s[0] == ']' && s[1] == ']' && PUGI__ENDSWITH(s[2], '>')) // CDATA ends here
02042             {
02043                 *g.flush(s) = 0;
02044                 
02045                 return s + 1;
02046             }
02047             else if (*s == 0)
02048             {
02049                 return 0;
02050             }
02051             else ++s;
02052         }
02053     }
02054     
02055     typedef char_t* (*strconv_pcdata_t)(char_t*);
02056         
02057     template <typename opt_trim, typename opt_eol, typename opt_escape> struct strconv_pcdata_impl
02058     {
02059         static char_t* parse(char_t* s)
02060         {
02061             gap g;
02062 
02063             char_t* begin = s;
02064 
02065             while (true)
02066             {
02067                 PUGI__SCANWHILE_UNROLL(!PUGI__IS_CHARTYPE(ss, ct_parse_pcdata));
02068 
02069                 if (*s == '<') // PCDATA ends here
02070                 {
02071                     char_t* end = g.flush(s);
02072 
02073                     if (opt_trim::value)
02074                         while (end > begin && PUGI__IS_CHARTYPE(end[-1], ct_space))
02075                             --end;
02076 
02077                     *end = 0;
02078                     
02079                     return s + 1;
02080                 }
02081                 else if (opt_eol::value && *s == '\r') // Either a single 0x0d or 0x0d 0x0a pair
02082                 {
02083                     *s++ = '\n'; // replace first one with 0x0a
02084                     
02085                     if (*s == '\n') g.push(s, 1);
02086                 }
02087                 else if (opt_escape::value && *s == '&')
02088                 {
02089                     s = strconv_escape(s, g);
02090                 }
02091                 else if (*s == 0)
02092                 {
02093                     char_t* end = g.flush(s);
02094 
02095                     if (opt_trim::value)
02096                         while (end > begin && PUGI__IS_CHARTYPE(end[-1], ct_space))
02097                             --end;
02098 
02099                     *end = 0;
02100 
02101                     return s;
02102                 }
02103                 else ++s;
02104             }
02105         }
02106     };
02107     
02108     PUGI__FN strconv_pcdata_t get_strconv_pcdata(unsigned int optmask)
02109     {
02110         PUGI__STATIC_ASSERT(parse_escapes == 0x10 && parse_eol == 0x20 && parse_trim_pcdata == 0x0800);
02111 
02112         switch (((optmask >> 4) & 3) | ((optmask >> 9) & 4)) // get bitmask for flags (eol escapes trim)
02113         {
02114         case 0: return strconv_pcdata_impl<opt_false, opt_false, opt_false>::parse;
02115         case 1: return strconv_pcdata_impl<opt_false, opt_false, opt_true>::parse;
02116         case 2: return strconv_pcdata_impl<opt_false, opt_true, opt_false>::parse;
02117         case 3: return strconv_pcdata_impl<opt_false, opt_true, opt_true>::parse;
02118         case 4: return strconv_pcdata_impl<opt_true, opt_false, opt_false>::parse;
02119         case 5: return strconv_pcdata_impl<opt_true, opt_false, opt_true>::parse;
02120         case 6: return strconv_pcdata_impl<opt_true, opt_true, opt_false>::parse;
02121         case 7: return strconv_pcdata_impl<opt_true, opt_true, opt_true>::parse;
02122         default: assert(false); return 0; // should not get here
02123         }
02124     }
02125 
02126     typedef char_t* (*strconv_attribute_t)(char_t*, char_t);
02127     
02128     template <typename opt_escape> struct strconv_attribute_impl
02129     {
02130         static char_t* parse_wnorm(char_t* s, char_t end_quote)
02131         {
02132             gap g;
02133 
02134             // trim leading whitespaces
02135             if (PUGI__IS_CHARTYPE(*s, ct_space))
02136             {
02137                 char_t* str = s;
02138                 
02139                 do ++str;
02140                 while (PUGI__IS_CHARTYPE(*str, ct_space));
02141                 
02142                 g.push(s, str - s);
02143             }
02144 
02145             while (true)
02146             {
02147                 PUGI__SCANWHILE_UNROLL(!PUGI__IS_CHARTYPE(ss, ct_parse_attr_ws | ct_space));
02148                 
02149                 if (*s == end_quote)
02150                 {
02151                     char_t* str = g.flush(s);
02152                     
02153                     do *str-- = 0;
02154                     while (PUGI__IS_CHARTYPE(*str, ct_space));
02155                 
02156                     return s + 1;
02157                 }
02158                 else if (PUGI__IS_CHARTYPE(*s, ct_space))
02159                 {
02160                     *s++ = ' ';
02161         
02162                     if (PUGI__IS_CHARTYPE(*s, ct_space))
02163                     {
02164                         char_t* str = s + 1;
02165                         while (PUGI__IS_CHARTYPE(*str, ct_space)) ++str;
02166                         
02167                         g.push(s, str - s);
02168                     }
02169                 }
02170                 else if (opt_escape::value && *s == '&')
02171                 {
02172                     s = strconv_escape(s, g);
02173                 }
02174                 else if (!*s)
02175                 {
02176                     return 0;
02177                 }
02178                 else ++s;
02179             }
02180         }
02181 
02182         static char_t* parse_wconv(char_t* s, char_t end_quote)
02183         {
02184             gap g;
02185 
02186             while (true)
02187             {
02188                 PUGI__SCANWHILE_UNROLL(!PUGI__IS_CHARTYPE(ss, ct_parse_attr_ws));
02189                 
02190                 if (*s == end_quote)
02191                 {
02192                     *g.flush(s) = 0;
02193                 
02194                     return s + 1;
02195                 }
02196                 else if (PUGI__IS_CHARTYPE(*s, ct_space))
02197                 {
02198                     if (*s == '\r')
02199                     {
02200                         *s++ = ' ';
02201                 
02202                         if (*s == '\n') g.push(s, 1);
02203                     }
02204                     else *s++ = ' ';
02205                 }
02206                 else if (opt_escape::value && *s == '&')
02207                 {
02208                     s = strconv_escape(s, g);
02209                 }
02210                 else if (!*s)
02211                 {
02212                     return 0;
02213                 }
02214                 else ++s;
02215             }
02216         }
02217 
02218         static char_t* parse_eol(char_t* s, char_t end_quote)
02219         {
02220             gap g;
02221 
02222             while (true)
02223             {
02224                 PUGI__SCANWHILE_UNROLL(!PUGI__IS_CHARTYPE(ss, ct_parse_attr));
02225                 
02226                 if (*s == end_quote)
02227                 {
02228                     *g.flush(s) = 0;
02229                 
02230                     return s + 1;
02231                 }
02232                 else if (*s == '\r')
02233                 {
02234                     *s++ = '\n';
02235                     
02236                     if (*s == '\n') g.push(s, 1);
02237                 }
02238                 else if (opt_escape::value && *s == '&')
02239                 {
02240                     s = strconv_escape(s, g);
02241                 }
02242                 else if (!*s)
02243                 {
02244                     return 0;
02245                 }
02246                 else ++s;
02247             }
02248         }
02249 
02250         static char_t* parse_simple(char_t* s, char_t end_quote)
02251         {
02252             gap g;
02253 
02254             while (true)
02255             {
02256                 PUGI__SCANWHILE_UNROLL(!PUGI__IS_CHARTYPE(ss, ct_parse_attr));
02257                 
02258                 if (*s == end_quote)
02259                 {
02260                     *g.flush(s) = 0;
02261                 
02262                     return s + 1;
02263                 }
02264                 else if (opt_escape::value && *s == '&')
02265                 {
02266                     s = strconv_escape(s, g);
02267                 }
02268                 else if (!*s)
02269                 {
02270                     return 0;
02271                 }
02272                 else ++s;
02273             }
02274         }
02275     };

02277     PUGI__FN strconv_attribute_t get_strconv_attribute(unsigned int optmask)
02278     {
02279         PUGI__STATIC_ASSERT(parse_escapes == 0x10 && parse_eol == 0x20 && parse_wconv_attribute == 0x40 && parse_wnorm_attribute == 0x80);
02280         
02281         switch ((optmask >> 4) & 15) // get bitmask for flags (wconv wnorm eol escapes)
02282         {
02283         case 0:  return strconv_attribute_impl<opt_false>::parse_simple;
02284         case 1:  return strconv_attribute_impl<opt_true>::parse_simple;
02285         case 2:  return strconv_attribute_impl<opt_false>::parse_eol;
02286         case 3:  return strconv_attribute_impl<opt_true>::parse_eol;
02287         case 4:  return strconv_attribute_impl<opt_false>::parse_wconv;
02288         case 5:  return strconv_attribute_impl<opt_true>::parse_wconv;
02289         case 6:  return strconv_attribute_impl<opt_false>::parse_wconv;
02290         case 7:  return strconv_attribute_impl<opt_true>::parse_wconv;
02291         case 8:  return strconv_attribute_impl<opt_false>::parse_wnorm;
02292         case 9:  return strconv_attribute_impl<opt_true>::parse_wnorm;
02293         case 10: return strconv_attribute_impl<opt_false>::parse_wnorm;
02294         case 11: return strconv_attribute_impl<opt_true>::parse_wnorm;
02295         case 12: return strconv_attribute_impl<opt_false>::parse_wnorm;
02296         case 13: return strconv_attribute_impl<opt_true>::parse_wnorm;
02297         case 14: return strconv_attribute_impl<opt_false>::parse_wnorm;
02298         case 15: return strconv_attribute_impl<opt_true>::parse_wnorm;
02299         default: assert(false); return 0; // should not get here
02300         }
02301     }
