02311 
02312     struct xml_parser
02313     {
02314         xml_allocator alloc;
02315         char_t* error_offset;
02316         xml_parse_status error_status;
02317         
02318         xml_parser(const xml_allocator& alloc_): alloc(alloc_), error_offset(0), error_status(status_ok)
02319         {
02320         }
02321 
02322         // DOCTYPE consists of nested sections of the following possible types:
02323         // <!-- ... -->, <? ... ?>, "...", '...'
02324         // <![...]]>
02325         // <!...>
02326         // First group can not contain nested groups
02327         // Second group can contain nested groups of the same type
02328         // Third group can contain all other groups
02329         char_t* parse_doctype_primitive(char_t* s)
02330         {
02331             if (*s == '"' || *s == '\'')
02332             {
02333                 // quoted string
02334                 char_t ch = *s++;
02335                 PUGI__SCANFOR(*s == ch);
02336                 if (!*s) PUGI__THROW_ERROR(status_bad_doctype, s);
02337 
02338                 s++;
02339             }
02340             else if (s[0] == '<' && s[1] == '?')
02341             {
02342                 // <? ... ?>
02343                 s += 2;
02344                 PUGI__SCANFOR(s[0] == '?' && s[1] == '>'); // no need for ENDSWITH because ?> can't terminate proper doctype
02345                 if (!*s) PUGI__THROW_ERROR(status_bad_doctype, s);
02346 
02347                 s += 2;
02348             }
02349             else if (s[0] == '<' && s[1] == '!' && s[2] == '-' && s[3] == '-')
02350             {
02351                 s += 4;
02352                 PUGI__SCANFOR(s[0] == '-' && s[1] == '-' && s[2] == '>'); // no need for ENDSWITH because --> can't terminate proper doctype
02353                 if (!*s) PUGI__THROW_ERROR(status_bad_doctype, s);
02354 
02355                 s += 3;
02356             }
02357             else PUGI__THROW_ERROR(status_bad_doctype, s);
02358 
02359             return s;
02360         }
02361 
02362         char_t* parse_doctype_ignore(char_t* s)
02363         {
02364             size_t depth = 0;
02365 
02366             assert(s[0] == '<' && s[1] == '!' && s[2] == '[');
02367             s += 3;
02368 
02369             while (*s)
02370             {
02371                 if (s[0] == '<' && s[1] == '!' && s[2] == '[')
02372                 {
02373                     // nested ignore section
02374                     s += 3;
02375                     depth++;
02376                 }
02377                 else if (s[0] == ']' && s[1] == ']' && s[2] == '>')
02378                 {
02379                     // ignore section end
02380                     s += 3;
02381 
02382                     if (depth == 0)
02383                         return s;
02384 
02385                     depth--;
02386                 }
02387                 else s++;
02388             }
02389 
02390             PUGI__THROW_ERROR(status_bad_doctype, s);
02391         }
02392 
02393         char_t* parse_doctype_group(char_t* s, char_t endch)
02394         {
02395             size_t depth = 0;
02396 
02397             assert((s[0] == '<' || s[0] == 0) && s[1] == '!');
02398             s += 2;
02399 
02400             while (*s)
02401             {
02402                 if (s[0] == '<' && s[1] == '!' && s[2] != '-')
02403                 {
02404                     if (s[2] == '[')
02405                     {
02406                         // ignore
02407                         s = parse_doctype_ignore(s);
02408                         if (!s) return s;
02409                     }
02410                     else
02411                     {
02412                         // some control group
02413                         s += 2;
02414                         depth++;
02415                     }
02416                 }
02417                 else if (s[0] == '<' || s[0] == '"' || s[0] == '\'')
02418                 {
02419                     // unknown tag (forbidden), or some primitive group
02420                     s = parse_doctype_primitive(s);
02421                     if (!s) return s;
02422                 }
02423                 else if (*s == '>')
02424                 {
02425                     if (depth == 0)
02426                         return s;
02427 
02428                     depth--;
02429                     s++;
02430                 }
02431                 else s++;
02432             }
02433 
02434             if (depth != 0 || endch != '>') PUGI__THROW_ERROR(status_bad_doctype, s);
02435 
02436             return s;
02437         }
02438 
02439         char_t* parse_exclamation(char_t* s, xml_node_struct* cursor, unsigned int optmsk, char_t endch)
02440         {
02441             // parse node contents, starting with exclamation mark
02442             ++s;
02443 
02444             if (*s == '-') // '<!-...'
02445             {
02446                 ++s;
02447 
02448                 if (*s == '-') // '<!--...'
02449                 {
02450                     ++s;
02451 
02452                     if (PUGI__OPTSET(parse_comments))
02453                     {
02454                         PUGI__PUSHNODE(node_comment); // Append a new node on the tree.
02455                         cursor->value = s; // Save the offset.
02456                     }
02457 
02458                     if (PUGI__OPTSET(parse_eol) && PUGI__OPTSET(parse_comments))
02459                     {
02460                         s = strconv_comment(s, endch);
02461 
02462                         if (!s) PUGI__THROW_ERROR(status_bad_comment, cursor->value);
02463                     }
02464                     else
02465                     {
02466                         // Scan for terminating '-->'.
02467                         PUGI__SCANFOR(s[0] == '-' && s[1] == '-' && PUGI__ENDSWITH(s[2], '>'));
02468                         PUGI__CHECK_ERROR(status_bad_comment, s);
02469 
02470                         if (PUGI__OPTSET(parse_comments))
02471                             *s = 0; // Zero-terminate this segment at the first terminating '-'.
02472 
02473                         s += (s[2] == '>' ? 3 : 2); // Step over the '\0->'.
02474                     }
02475                 }
02476                 else PUGI__THROW_ERROR(status_bad_comment, s);
02477             }
02478             else if (*s == '[')
02479             {
02480                 // '<![CDATA[...'
02481                 if (*++s=='C' && *++s=='D' && *++s=='A' && *++s=='T' && *++s=='A' && *++s == '[')
02482                 {
02483                     ++s;
02484 
02485                     if (PUGI__OPTSET(parse_cdata))
02486                     {
02487                         PUGI__PUSHNODE(node_cdata); // Append a new node on the tree.
02488                         cursor->value = s; // Save the offset.
02489 
02490                         if (PUGI__OPTSET(parse_eol))
02491                         {
02492                             s = strconv_cdata(s, endch);
02493 
02494                             if (!s) PUGI__THROW_ERROR(status_bad_cdata, cursor->value);
02495                         }
02496                         else
02497                         {
02498                             // Scan for terminating ']]>'.
02499                             PUGI__SCANFOR(s[0] == ']' && s[1] == ']' && PUGI__ENDSWITH(s[2], '>'));
02500                             PUGI__CHECK_ERROR(status_bad_cdata, s);
02501 
02502                             *s++ = 0; // Zero-terminate this segment.
02503                         }
02504                     }
02505                     else // Flagged for discard, but we still have to scan for the terminator.
02506                     {
02507                         // Scan for terminating ']]>'.
02508                         PUGI__SCANFOR(s[0] == ']' && s[1] == ']' && PUGI__ENDSWITH(s[2], '>'));
02509                         PUGI__CHECK_ERROR(status_bad_cdata, s);
02510 
02511                         ++s;
02512                     }
02513 
02514                     s += (s[1] == '>' ? 2 : 1); // Step over the last ']>'.
02515                 }
02516                 else PUGI__THROW_ERROR(status_bad_cdata, s);
02517             }
02518             else if (s[0] == 'D' && s[1] == 'O' && s[2] == 'C' && s[3] == 'T' && s[4] == 'Y' && s[5] == 'P' && PUGI__ENDSWITH(s[6], 'E'))
02519             {
02520                 s -= 2;
02521 
02522                 if (cursor->parent) PUGI__THROW_ERROR(status_bad_doctype, s);
02523 
02524                 char_t* mark = s + 9;
02525 
02526                 s = parse_doctype_group(s, endch);
02527                 if (!s) return s;
02528 
02529                 assert((*s == 0 && endch == '>') || *s == '>');
02530                 if (*s) *s++ = 0;
02531 
02532                 if (PUGI__OPTSET(parse_doctype))
02533                 {
02534                     while (PUGI__IS_CHARTYPE(*mark, ct_space)) ++mark;
02535 
02536                     PUGI__PUSHNODE(node_doctype);
02537 
02538                     cursor->value = mark;
02539                 }
02540             }
02541             else if (*s == 0 && endch == '-') PUGI__THROW_ERROR(status_bad_comment, s);
02542             else if (*s == 0 && endch == '[') PUGI__THROW_ERROR(status_bad_cdata, s);
02543             else PUGI__THROW_ERROR(status_unrecognized_tag, s);
02544 
02545             return s;
02546         }
02547 
02548         char_t* parse_question(char_t* s, xml_node_struct*& ref_cursor, unsigned int optmsk, char_t endch)
02549         {
02550             // load into registers
02551             xml_node_struct* cursor = ref_cursor;
02552             char_t ch = 0;
02553 
02554             // parse node contents, starting with question mark
02555             ++s;
02556 
02557             // read PI target
02558             char_t* target = s;
02559 
02560             if (!PUGI__IS_CHARTYPE(*s, ct_start_symbol)) PUGI__THROW_ERROR(status_bad_pi, s);
02561 
02562             PUGI__SCANWHILE(PUGI__IS_CHARTYPE(*s, ct_symbol));
02563             PUGI__CHECK_ERROR(status_bad_pi, s);
02564 
02565             // determine node type; stricmp / strcasecmp is not portable
02566             bool declaration = (target[0] | ' ') == 'x' && (target[1] | ' ') == 'm' && (target[2] | ' ') == 'l' && target + 3 == s;
02567 
02568             if (declaration ? PUGI__OPTSET(parse_declaration) : PUGI__OPTSET(parse_pi))
02569             {
02570                 if (declaration)
02571                 {
02572                     // disallow non top-level declarations
02573                     if (cursor->parent) PUGI__THROW_ERROR(status_bad_pi, s);
02574 
02575                     PUGI__PUSHNODE(node_declaration);
02576                 }
02577                 else
02578                 {
02579                     PUGI__PUSHNODE(node_pi);
02580                 }
02581 
02582                 cursor->name = target;
02583 
02584                 PUGI__ENDSEG();
02585 
02586                 // parse value/attributes
02587                 if (ch == '?')
02588                 {
02589                     // empty node
02590                     if (!PUGI__ENDSWITH(*s, '>')) PUGI__THROW_ERROR(status_bad_pi, s);
02591                     s += (*s == '>');
02592 
02593                     PUGI__POPNODE();
02594                 }
02595                 else if (PUGI__IS_CHARTYPE(ch, ct_space))
02596                 {
02597                     PUGI__SKIPWS();
02598 
02599                     // scan for tag end
02600                     char_t* value = s;
02601 
02602                     PUGI__SCANFOR(s[0] == '?' && PUGI__ENDSWITH(s[1], '>'));
02603                     PUGI__CHECK_ERROR(status_bad_pi, s);
02604 
02605                     if (declaration)
02606                     {
02607                         // replace ending ? with / so that 'element' terminates properly
02608                         *s = '/';
02609 
02610                         // we exit from this function with cursor at node_declaration, which is a signal to parse() to go to LOC_ATTRIBUTES
02611                         s = value;
02612                     }
02613                     else
02614                     {
02615                         // store value and step over >
02616                         cursor->value = value;
02617                         PUGI__POPNODE();
02618 
02619                         PUGI__ENDSEG();
02620 
02621                         s += (*s == '>');
02622                     }
02623                 }
02624                 else PUGI__THROW_ERROR(status_bad_pi, s);
02625             }
02626             else
02627             {
02628                 // scan for tag end
02629                 PUGI__SCANFOR(s[0] == '?' && PUGI__ENDSWITH(s[1], '>'));
02630                 PUGI__CHECK_ERROR(status_bad_pi, s);
02631 
02632                 s += (s[1] == '>' ? 2 : 1);
02633             }
02634 
02635             // store from registers
02636             ref_cursor = cursor;
02637 
02638             return s;
02639         }
02640 
02641         char_t* parse_tree(char_t* s, xml_node_struct* root, unsigned int optmsk, char_t endch)
02642         {
02643             strconv_attribute_t strconv_attribute = get_strconv_attribute(optmsk);
02644             strconv_pcdata_t strconv_pcdata = get_strconv_pcdata(optmsk);
02645             
02646             char_t ch = 0;
02647             xml_node_struct* cursor = root;
02648             char_t* mark = s;
02649 
02650             while (*s != 0)
02651             {
02652                 if (*s == '<')
02653                 {
02654                     ++s;
02655 
02656                 LOC_TAG:
02657                     if (PUGI__IS_CHARTYPE(*s, ct_start_symbol)) // '<#...'
02658                     {
02659                         PUGI__PUSHNODE(node_element); // Append a new node to the tree.
02660 
02661                         cursor->name = s;
02662 
02663                         PUGI__SCANWHILE_UNROLL(PUGI__IS_CHARTYPE(ss, ct_symbol)); // Scan for a terminator.
02664                         PUGI__ENDSEG(); // Save char in 'ch', terminate & step over.
02665 
02666                         if (ch == '>')
02667                         {
02668                             // end of tag
02669                         }
02670                         else if (PUGI__IS_CHARTYPE(ch, ct_space))
02671                         {
02672                         LOC_ATTRIBUTES:
02673                             while (true)
02674                             {
02675                                 PUGI__SKIPWS(); // Eat any whitespace.
02676                         
02677                                 if (PUGI__IS_CHARTYPE(*s, ct_start_symbol)) // <... #...
02678                                 {
02679                                     xml_attribute_struct* a = append_new_attribute(cursor, alloc); // Make space for this attribute.
02680                                     if (!a) PUGI__THROW_ERROR(status_out_of_memory, s);
02681 
02682                                     a->name = s; // Save the offset.
02683 
02684                                     PUGI__SCANWHILE_UNROLL(PUGI__IS_CHARTYPE(ss, ct_symbol)); // Scan for a terminator.
02685                                     PUGI__ENDSEG(); // Save char in 'ch', terminate & step over.
02686 
02687                                     if (PUGI__IS_CHARTYPE(ch, ct_space))
02688                                     {
02689                                         PUGI__SKIPWS(); // Eat any whitespace.
02690 
02691                                         ch = *s;
02692                                         ++s;
02693                                     }
02694                                     
02695                                     if (ch == '=') // '<... #=...'
02696                                     {
02697                                         PUGI__SKIPWS(); // Eat any whitespace.
02698 
02699                                         if (*s == '"' || *s == '\'') // '<... #="...'
02700                                         {
02701                                             ch = *s; // Save quote char to avoid breaking on "''" -or- '""'.
02702                                             ++s; // Step over the quote.
02703                                             a->value = s; // Save the offset.
02704 
02705                                             s = strconv_attribute(s, ch);
02706                                         
02707                                             if (!s) PUGI__THROW_ERROR(status_bad_attribute, a->value);
02708 
02709                                             // After this line the loop continues from the start;
02710                                             // Whitespaces, / and > are ok, symbols and EOF are wrong,
02711                                             // everything else will be detected
02712                                             if (PUGI__IS_CHARTYPE(*s, ct_start_symbol)) PUGI__THROW_ERROR(status_bad_attribute, s);
02713                                         }
02714                                         else PUGI__THROW_ERROR(status_bad_attribute, s);
02715                                     }
02716                                     else PUGI__THROW_ERROR(status_bad_attribute, s);
02717                                 }
02718                                 else if (*s == '/')
02719                                 {
02720                                     ++s;
02721                                     
02722                                     if (*s == '>')
02723                                     {
02724                                         PUGI__POPNODE();
02725                                         s++;
02726                                         break;
02727                                     }
02728                                     else if (*s == 0 && endch == '>')
02729                                     {
02730                                         PUGI__POPNODE();
02731                                         break;
02732                                     }
02733                                     else PUGI__THROW_ERROR(status_bad_start_element, s);
02734                                 }
02735                                 else if (*s == '>')
02736                                 {
02737                                     ++s;
02738 
02739                                     break;
02740                                 }
02741                                 else if (*s == 0 && endch == '>')
02742                                 {
02743                                     break;
02744                                 }
02745                                 else PUGI__THROW_ERROR(status_bad_start_element, s);
02746                             }
02747 
02748                             // !!!
02749                         }
02750                         else if (ch == '/') // '<#.../'
02751                         {
02752                             if (!PUGI__ENDSWITH(*s, '>')) PUGI__THROW_ERROR(status_bad_start_element, s);
02753 
02754                             PUGI__POPNODE(); // Pop.
02755 
02756                             s += (*s == '>');
02757                         }
02758                         else if (ch == 0)
02759                         {
02760                             // we stepped over null terminator, backtrack & handle closing tag
02761                             --s;
02762                             
02763                             if (endch != '>') PUGI__THROW_ERROR(status_bad_start_element, s);
02764                         }
02765                         else PUGI__THROW_ERROR(status_bad_start_element, s);
02766                     }
02767                     else if (*s == '/')
02768                     {
02769                         ++s;
02770 
02771                         char_t* name = cursor->name;
02772                         if (!name) PUGI__THROW_ERROR(status_end_element_mismatch, s);
02773                         
02774                         while (PUGI__IS_CHARTYPE(*s, ct_symbol))
02775                         {
02776                             if (*s++ != *name++) PUGI__THROW_ERROR(status_end_element_mismatch, s);
02777                         }
02778 
02779                         if (*name)
02780                         {
02781                             if (*s == 0 && name[0] == endch && name[1] == 0) PUGI__THROW_ERROR(status_bad_end_element, s);
02782                             else PUGI__THROW_ERROR(status_end_element_mismatch, s);
02783                         }
02784                             
02785                         PUGI__POPNODE(); // Pop.
02786 
02787                         PUGI__SKIPWS();
02788 
02789                         if (*s == 0)
02790                         {
02791                             if (endch != '>') PUGI__THROW_ERROR(status_bad_end_element, s);
02792                         }
02793                         else
02794                         {
02795                             if (*s != '>') PUGI__THROW_ERROR(status_bad_end_element, s);
02796                             ++s;
02797                         }
02798                     }
02799                     else if (*s == '?') // '<?...'
02800                     {
02801                         s = parse_question(s, cursor, optmsk, endch);
02802                         if (!s) return s;
02803 
02804                         assert(cursor);
02805                         if (PUGI__NODETYPE(cursor) == node_declaration) goto LOC_ATTRIBUTES;
02806                     }
02807                     else if (*s == '!') // '<!...'
02808                     {
02809                         s = parse_exclamation(s, cursor, optmsk, endch);
02810                         if (!s) return s;
02811                     }
02812                     else if (*s == 0 && endch == '?') PUGI__THROW_ERROR(status_bad_pi, s);
02813                     else PUGI__THROW_ERROR(status_unrecognized_tag, s);
02814                 }
02815                 else
02816                 {
02817                     mark = s; // Save this offset while searching for a terminator.
02818 
02819                     PUGI__SKIPWS(); // Eat whitespace if no genuine PCDATA here.
02820 
02821                     if (*s == '<' || !*s)
02822                     {
02823                         // We skipped some whitespace characters because otherwise we would take the tag branch instead of PCDATA one
02824                         assert(mark != s);
02825 
02826                         if (!PUGI__OPTSET(parse_ws_pcdata | parse_ws_pcdata_single) || PUGI__OPTSET(parse_trim_pcdata))
02827                         {
02828                             continue;
02829                         }
02830                         else if (PUGI__OPTSET(parse_ws_pcdata_single))
02831                         {
02832                             if (s[0] != '<' || s[1] != '/' || cursor->first_child) continue;
02833                         }
02834                     }
02835 
02836                     if (!PUGI__OPTSET(parse_trim_pcdata))
02837                         s = mark;
02838                             
02839                     if (cursor->parent || PUGI__OPTSET(parse_fragment))
02840                     {
02841                         PUGI__PUSHNODE(node_pcdata); // Append a new node on the tree.
02842                         cursor->value = s; // Save the offset.
02843 
02844                         s = strconv_pcdata(s);
02845                                 
02846                         PUGI__POPNODE(); // Pop since this is a standalone.
02847                         
02848                         if (!*s) break;
02849                     }
02850                     else
02851                     {
02852                         PUGI__SCANFOR(*s == '<'); // '...<'
02853                         if (!*s) break;
02854                         
02855                         ++s;
02856                     }
02857 
02858                     // We're after '<'
02859                     goto LOC_TAG;
02860                 }
02861             }
02862 
02863             // check that last tag is closed
02864             if (cursor != root) PUGI__THROW_ERROR(status_end_element_mismatch, s);
02865 
02866             return s;
02867         }
02868 
02869     #ifdef PUGIXML_WCHAR_MODE
02870         static char_t* parse_skip_bom(char_t* s)
02871         {
02872             unsigned int bom = 0xfeff;
02873             return (s[0] == static_cast<wchar_t>(bom)) ? s + 1 : s;
02874         }
02875     #else
02876         static char_t* parse_skip_bom(char_t* s)
02877         {
02878             return (s[0] == '\xef' && s[1] == '\xbb' && s[2] == '\xbf') ? s + 3 : s;
02879         }
02880     #endif
02881 
02882         static bool has_element_node_siblings(xml_node_struct* node)
02883         {
02884             while (node)
02885             {
02886                 if (PUGI__NODETYPE(node) == node_element) return true;
02887 
02888                 node = node->next_sibling;
02889             }
02890 
02891             return false;
02892         }
02893 
02894         static xml_parse_result parse(char_t* buffer, size_t length, xml_document_struct* xmldoc, xml_node_struct* root, unsigned int optmsk)
02895         {
02896             // allocator object is a part of document object
02897             xml_allocator& alloc_ = *static_cast<xml_allocator*>(xmldoc);
02898 
02899             // early-out for empty documents
02900             if (length == 0)
02901                 return make_parse_result(PUGI__OPTSET(parse_fragment) ? status_ok : status_no_document_element);
02902 
02903             // get last child of the root before parsing
02904             xml_node_struct* last_root_child = root->first_child ? root->first_child->prev_sibling_c : 0;
02905     
02906             // create parser on stack
02907             xml_parser parser(alloc_);
02908 
02909             // save last character and make buffer zero-terminated (speeds up parsing)
02910             char_t endch = buffer[length - 1];
02911             buffer[length - 1] = 0;
02912             
02913             // skip BOM to make sure it does not end up as part of parse output
02914             char_t* buffer_data = parse_skip_bom(buffer);
02915 
02916             // perform actual parsing
02917             parser.parse_tree(buffer_data, root, optmsk, endch);
02918 
02919             // update allocator state
02920             alloc_ = parser.alloc;
02921 
02922             xml_parse_result result = make_parse_result(parser.error_status, parser.error_offset ? parser.error_offset - buffer : 0);
02923             assert(result.offset >= 0 && static_cast<size_t>(result.offset) <= length);
02924 
02925             if (result)
02926             {
02927                 // since we removed last character, we have to handle the only possible false positive (stray <)
02928                 if (endch == '<')
02929                     return make_parse_result(status_unrecognized_tag, length - 1);
02930 
02931                 // check if there are any element nodes parsed
02932                 xml_node_struct* first_root_child_parsed = last_root_child ? last_root_child->next_sibling : root->first_child;
02933 
02934                 if (!PUGI__OPTSET(parse_fragment) && !has_element_node_siblings(first_root_child_parsed))
02935                     return make_parse_result(status_no_document_element, length - 1);
02936             }
02937             else
02938             {
02939                 // roll back offset if it occurs on a null terminator in the source buffer
02940                 if (result.offset > 0 && static_cast<size_t>(result.offset) == length - 1 && endch == 0)
02941                     result.offset--;
02942             }
02943 
02944             return result;
02945         }
02946     };
02947 
02948     // Output facilities
02949     PUGI__FN xml_encoding get_write_native_encoding()
02950     {
02951     #ifdef PUGIXML_WCHAR_MODE
02952         return get_wchar_encoding();
02953     #else
02954         return encoding_utf8;
02955     #endif
02956     }
02957 
02958     PUGI__FN xml_encoding get_write_encoding(xml_encoding encoding)
02959     {
02960         // replace wchar encoding with utf implementation
02961         if (encoding == encoding_wchar) return get_wchar_encoding();
02962 
02963         // replace utf16 encoding with utf16 with specific endianness
02964         if (encoding == encoding_utf16) return is_little_endian() ? encoding_utf16_le : encoding_utf16_be;
02965 
02966         // replace utf32 encoding with utf32 with specific endianness
02967         if (encoding == encoding_utf32) return is_little_endian() ? encoding_utf32_le : encoding_utf32_be;
02968 
02969         // only do autodetection if no explicit encoding is requested
02970         if (encoding != encoding_auto) return encoding;
02971 
02972         // assume utf8 encoding
02973         return encoding_utf8;
02974     }
02975 
02976 #ifdef PUGIXML_WCHAR_MODE
02977     PUGI__FN size_t get_valid_length(const char_t* data, size_t length)
02978     {
02979         if (length < 1) return 0;
02980 
02981         // discard last character if it's the lead of a surrogate pair 
02982         return (sizeof(wchar_t) == 2 && static_cast<unsigned int>(static_cast<uint16_t>(data[length - 1]) - 0xD800) < 0x400) ? length - 1 : length;
02983     }
02984 
02985     PUGI__FN size_t convert_buffer_output(char_t* r_char, uint8_t* r_u8, uint16_t* r_u16, uint32_t* r_u32, const char_t* data, size_t length, xml_encoding encoding)
02986     {
02987         // only endian-swapping is required
02988         if (need_endian_swap_utf(encoding, get_wchar_encoding()))
02989         {
02990             convert_wchar_endian_swap(r_char, data, length);
02991 
02992             return length * sizeof(char_t);
02993         }
02994     
02995         // convert to utf8
02996         if (encoding == encoding_utf8)
02997         {
02998             uint8_t* dest = r_u8;
02999             uint8_t* end = utf_decoder<utf8_writer>::decode_wchar_block(data, length, dest);
03000 
03001             return static_cast<size_t>(end - dest);
03002         }
03003 
03004         // convert to utf16
03005         if (encoding == encoding_utf16_be || encoding == encoding_utf16_le)
03006         {
03007             uint16_t* dest = r_u16;
03008 
03009             // convert to native utf16
03010             uint16_t* end = utf_decoder<utf16_writer>::decode_wchar_block(data, length, dest);
03011 
03012             // swap if necessary
03013             xml_encoding native_encoding = is_little_endian() ? encoding_utf16_le : encoding_utf16_be;
03014 
03015             if (native_encoding != encoding) convert_utf_endian_swap(dest, dest, static_cast<size_t>(end - dest));
03016 
03017             return static_cast<size_t>(end - dest) * sizeof(uint16_t);
03018         }
03019 
03020         // convert to utf32
03021         if (encoding == encoding_utf32_be || encoding == encoding_utf32_le)
03022         {
03023             uint32_t* dest = r_u32;
03024 
03025             // convert to native utf32
03026             uint32_t* end = utf_decoder<utf32_writer>::decode_wchar_block(data, length, dest);
03027 
03028             // swap if necessary
03029             xml_encoding native_encoding = is_little_endian() ? encoding_utf32_le : encoding_utf32_be;
03030 
03031             if (native_encoding != encoding) convert_utf_endian_swap(dest, dest, static_cast<size_t>(end - dest));
03032 
03033             return static_cast<size_t>(end - dest) * sizeof(uint32_t);
03034         }
03035 
03036         // convert to latin1
03037         if (encoding == encoding_latin1)
03038         {
03039             uint8_t* dest = r_u8;
03040             uint8_t* end = utf_decoder<latin1_writer>::decode_wchar_block(data, length, dest);
03041 
03042             return static_cast<size_t>(end - dest);
03043         }
03044 
03045         assert(!"Invalid encoding");
03046         return 0;
03047     }
03048 #else
03049     PUGI__FN size_t get_valid_length(const char_t* data, size_t length)
03050     {
03051         if (length < 5) return 0;
03052 
03053         for (size_t i = 1; i <= 4; ++i)
03054         {
03055             uint8_t ch = static_cast<uint8_t>(data[length - i]);
03056 
03057             // either a standalone character or a leading one
03058             if ((ch & 0xc0) != 0x80) return length - i;
03059         }
03060 
03061         // there are four non-leading characters at the end, sequence tail is broken so might as well process the whole chunk
03062         return length;
03063     }
03064 
03065     PUGI__FN size_t convert_buffer_output(char_t* /* r_char */, uint8_t* r_u8, uint16_t* r_u16, uint32_t* r_u32, const char_t* data, size_t length, xml_encoding encoding)
03066     {
03067         if (encoding == encoding_utf16_be || encoding == encoding_utf16_le)
03068         {
03069             uint16_t* dest = r_u16;
03070 
03071             // convert to native utf16
03072             uint16_t* end = utf_decoder<utf16_writer>::decode_utf8_block(reinterpret_cast<const uint8_t*>(data), length, dest);
03073 
03074             // swap if necessary
03075             xml_encoding native_encoding = is_little_endian() ? encoding_utf16_le : encoding_utf16_be;
03076 
03077             if (native_encoding != encoding) convert_utf_endian_swap(dest, dest, static_cast<size_t>(end - dest));
03078 
03079             return static_cast<size_t>(end - dest) * sizeof(uint16_t);
03080         }
03081 
03082         if (encoding == encoding_utf32_be || encoding == encoding_utf32_le)
03083         {
03084             uint32_t* dest = r_u32;
03085 
03086             // convert to native utf32
03087             uint32_t* end = utf_decoder<utf32_writer>::decode_utf8_block(reinterpret_cast<const uint8_t*>(data), length, dest);
03088 
03089             // swap if necessary
03090             xml_encoding native_encoding = is_little_endian() ? encoding_utf32_le : encoding_utf32_be;
03091 
03092             if (native_encoding != encoding) convert_utf_endian_swap(dest, dest, static_cast<size_t>(end - dest));
03093 
03094             return static_cast<size_t>(end - dest) * sizeof(uint32_t);
03095         }
03096 
03097         if (encoding == encoding_latin1)
03098         {
03099             uint8_t* dest = r_u8;
03100             uint8_t* end = utf_decoder<latin1_writer>::decode_utf8_block(reinterpret_cast<const uint8_t*>(data), length, dest);
03101 
03102             return static_cast<size_t>(end - dest);
03103         }
03104 
03105         assert(!"Invalid encoding");
03106         return 0;
03107     }
03108 #endif
03109 
03110     class xml_buffered_writer
03111     {
03112         xml_buffered_writer(const xml_buffered_writer&);
03113         xml_buffered_writer& operator=(const xml_buffered_writer&);
03114 
03115     public:
03116         xml_buffered_writer(xml_writer& writer_, xml_encoding user_encoding): writer(writer_), bufsize(0), encoding(get_write_encoding(user_encoding))
03117         {
03118             PUGI__STATIC_ASSERT(bufcapacity >= 8);
03119         }
03120 
03121         ~xml_buffered_writer()
03122         {
03123             flush();
03124         }
03125 
03126         size_t flush()
03127         {
03128             flush(buffer, bufsize);
03129             bufsize = 0;
03130             return 0;
03131         }
03132 
03133         void flush(const char_t* data, size_t size)
03134         {
03135             if (size == 0) return;
03136 
03137             // fast path, just write data
03138             if (encoding == get_write_native_encoding())
03139                 writer.write(data, size * sizeof(char_t));
03140             else
03141             {
03142                 // convert chunk
03143                 size_t result = convert_buffer_output(scratch.data_char, scratch.data_u8, scratch.data_u16, scratch.data_u32, data, size, encoding);
03144                 assert(result <= sizeof(scratch));
03145 
03146                 // write data
03147                 writer.write(scratch.data_u8, result);
03148             }
03149         }
03150 
03151         void write_direct(const char_t* data, size_t length)
03152         {
03153             // flush the remaining buffer contents
03154             flush();
03155 
03156             // handle large chunks
03157             if (length > bufcapacity)
03158             {
03159                 if (encoding == get_write_native_encoding())
03160                 {
03161                     // fast path, can just write data chunk
03162                     writer.write(data, length * sizeof(char_t));
03163                     return;
03164                 }
03165 
03166                 // need to convert in suitable chunks
03167                 while (length > bufcapacity)
03168                 {
03169                     // get chunk size by selecting such number of characters that are guaranteed to fit into scratch buffer
03170                     // and form a complete codepoint sequence (i.e. discard start of last codepoint if necessary)
03171                     size_t chunk_size = get_valid_length(data, bufcapacity);
03172                     assert(chunk_size);
03173 
03174                     // convert chunk and write
03175                     flush(data, chunk_size);
03176 
03177                     // iterate
03178                     data += chunk_size;
03179                     length -= chunk_size;
03180                 }
03181 
03182                 // small tail is copied below
03183                 bufsize = 0;
03184             }
03185 
03186             memcpy(buffer + bufsize, data, length * sizeof(char_t));
03187             bufsize += length;
03188         }
03189 
03190         void write_buffer(const char_t* data, size_t length)
03191         {
03192             size_t offset = bufsize;
03193 
03194             if (offset + length <= bufcapacity)
03195             {
03196                 memcpy(buffer + offset, data, length * sizeof(char_t));
03197                 bufsize = offset + length;
03198             }
03199             else
03200             {
03201                 write_direct(data, length);
03202             }
03203         }
03204 
03205         void write_string(const char_t* data)
03206         {
03207             // write the part of the string that fits in the buffer
03208             size_t offset = bufsize;
03209 
03210             while (*data && offset < bufcapacity)
03211                 buffer[offset++] = *data++;
03212 
03213             // write the rest
03214             if (offset < bufcapacity)
03215             {
03216                 bufsize = offset;
03217             }
03218             else
03219             {
03220                 // backtrack a bit if we have split the codepoint
03221                 size_t length = offset - bufsize;
03222                 size_t extra = length - get_valid_length(data - length, length);
03223 
03224                 bufsize = offset - extra;
03225 
03226                 write_direct(data - extra, strlength(data) + extra);
03227             }
03228         }
03229 
03230         void write(char_t d0)
03231         {
03232             size_t offset = bufsize;
03233             if (offset > bufcapacity - 1) offset = flush();
03234 
03235             buffer[offset + 0] = d0;
03236             bufsize = offset + 1;
03237         }
03238 
03239         void write(char_t d0, char_t d1)
03240         {
03241             size_t offset = bufsize;
03242             if (offset > bufcapacity - 2) offset = flush();
03243 
03244             buffer[offset + 0] = d0;
03245             buffer[offset + 1] = d1;
03246             bufsize = offset + 2;
03247         }
03248 
03249         void write(char_t d0, char_t d1, char_t d2)
03250         {
03251             size_t offset = bufsize;
03252             if (offset > bufcapacity - 3) offset = flush();
03253 
03254             buffer[offset + 0] = d0;
03255             buffer[offset + 1] = d1;
03256             buffer[offset + 2] = d2;
03257             bufsize = offset + 3;
03258         }
03259 
03260         void write(char_t d0, char_t d1, char_t d2, char_t d3)
03261         {
03262             size_t offset = bufsize;
03263             if (offset > bufcapacity - 4) offset = flush();
03264 
03265             buffer[offset + 0] = d0;
03266             buffer[offset + 1] = d1;
03267             buffer[offset + 2] = d2;
03268             buffer[offset + 3] = d3;
03269             bufsize = offset + 4;
03270         }
03271 
03272         void write(char_t d0, char_t d1, char_t d2, char_t d3, char_t d4)
03273         {
03274             size_t offset = bufsize;
03275             if (offset > bufcapacity - 5) offset = flush();
03276 
03277             buffer[offset + 0] = d0;
03278             buffer[offset + 1] = d1;
03279             buffer[offset + 2] = d2;
03280             buffer[offset + 3] = d3;
03281             buffer[offset + 4] = d4;
03282             bufsize = offset + 5;
03283         }
03284 
03285         void write(char_t d0, char_t d1, char_t d2, char_t d3, char_t d4, char_t d5)
03286         {
03287             size_t offset = bufsize;
03288             if (offset > bufcapacity - 6) offset = flush();
03289 
03290             buffer[offset + 0] = d0;
03291             buffer[offset + 1] = d1;
03292             buffer[offset + 2] = d2;
03293             buffer[offset + 3] = d3;
03294             buffer[offset + 4] = d4;
03295             buffer[offset + 5] = d5;
03296             bufsize = offset + 6;
03297         }
03298 
03299         // utf8 maximum expansion: x4 (-> utf32)
03300         // utf16 maximum expansion: x2 (-> utf32)
03301         // utf32 maximum expansion: x1
03302         enum
03303         {
03304             bufcapacitybytes =
03305             #ifdef PUGIXML_MEMORY_OUTPUT_STACK
03306                 PUGIXML_MEMORY_OUTPUT_STACK
03307             #else
03308                 10240
03309             #endif
03310             ,
03311             bufcapacity = bufcapacitybytes / (sizeof(char_t) + 4)
03312         };
03313 
03314         char_t buffer[bufcapacity];
03315 
03316         union
03317         {
03318             uint8_t data_u8[4 * bufcapacity];
03319             uint16_t data_u16[2 * bufcapacity];
03320             uint32_t data_u32[bufcapacity];
03321             char_t data_char[bufcapacity];
03322         } scratch;
03323 
03324         xml_writer& writer;
03325         size_t bufsize;
03326         xml_encoding encoding;
03327     };
03328 
03329     PUGI__FN void text_output_escaped(xml_buffered_writer& writer, const char_t* s, chartypex_t type)
03330     {
03331         while (*s)
03332         {
03333             const char_t* prev = s;
03334             
03335             // While *s is a usual symbol
03336             PUGI__SCANWHILE_UNROLL(!PUGI__IS_CHARTYPEX(ss, type));
03337         
03338             writer.write_buffer(prev, static_cast<size_t>(s - prev));
03339 
03340             switch (*s)
03341             {
03342                 case 0: break;
03343                 case '&':
03344                     writer.write('&', 'a', 'm', 'p', ';');
03345                     ++s;
03346                     break;
03347                 case '<':
03348                     writer.write('&', 'l', 't', ';');
03349                     ++s;
03350                     break;
03351                 case '>':
03352                     writer.write('&', 'g', 't', ';');
03353                     ++s;
03354                     break;
03355                 case '"':
03356                     writer.write('&', 'q', 'u', 'o', 't', ';');
03357                     ++s;
03358                     break;
03359                 default: // s is not a usual symbol
03360                 {
03361                     unsigned int ch = static_cast<unsigned int>(*s++);
03362                     assert(ch < 32);
03363 
03364                     writer.write('&', '#', static_cast<char_t>((ch / 10) + '0'), static_cast<char_t>((ch % 10) + '0'), ';');
03365                 }
03366             }
03367         }
03368     }
03369 
03370     PUGI__FN void text_output(xml_buffered_writer& writer, const char_t* s, chartypex_t type, unsigned int flags)
03371     {
03372         if (flags & format_no_escapes)
03373             writer.write_string(s);
03374         else
03375             text_output_escaped(writer, s, type);
03376     }
03377 
03378     PUGI__FN void text_output_cdata(xml_buffered_writer& writer, const char_t* s)
03379     {
03380         do
03381         {
03382             writer.write('<', '!', '[', 'C', 'D');
03383             writer.write('A', 'T', 'A', '[');
03384 
03385             const char_t* prev = s;
03386 
03387             // look for ]]> sequence - we can't output it as is since it terminates CDATA
03388             while (*s && !(s[0] == ']' && s[1] == ']' && s[2] == '>')) ++s;
03389 
03390             // skip ]] if we stopped at ]]>, > will go to the next CDATA section
03391             if (*s) s += 2;
03392 
03393             writer.write_buffer(prev, static_cast<size_t>(s - prev));
03394 
03395             writer.write(']', ']', '>');
03396         }
03397         while (*s);
03398     }
03399 
03400     PUGI__FN void text_output_indent(xml_buffered_writer& writer, const char_t* indent, size_t indent_length, unsigned int depth)
03401     {
03402         switch (indent_length)
03403         {
03404         case 1:
03405         {
03406             for (unsigned int i = 0; i < depth; ++i)
03407                 writer.write(indent[0]);
03408             break;
03409         }
03410 
03411         case 2:
03412         {
03413             for (unsigned int i = 0; i < depth; ++i)
03414                 writer.write(indent[0], indent[1]);
03415             break;
03416         }
03417 
03418         case 3:
03419         {
03420             for (unsigned int i = 0; i < depth; ++i)
03421                 writer.write(indent[0], indent[1], indent[2]);
03422             break;
03423         }
03424 
03425         case 4:
03426         {
03427             for (unsigned int i = 0; i < depth; ++i)
03428                 writer.write(indent[0], indent[1], indent[2], indent[3]);
03429             break;
03430         }
03431 
03432         default:
03433         {
03434             for (unsigned int i = 0; i < depth; ++i)
03435                 writer.write_buffer(indent, indent_length);
03436         }
03437         }
03438     }
03439 
03440     PUGI__FN void node_output_comment(xml_buffered_writer& writer, const char_t* s)
03441     {
03442         writer.write('<', '!', '-', '-');
03443 
03444         while (*s)
03445         {
03446             const char_t* prev = s;
03447 
03448             // look for -\0 or -- sequence - we can't output it since -- is illegal in comment body
03449             while (*s && !(s[0] == '-' && (s[1] == '-' || s[1] == 0))) ++s;
03450 
03451             writer.write_buffer(prev, static_cast<size_t>(s - prev));
03452 
03453             if (*s)
03454             {
03455                 assert(*s == '-');
03456 
03457                 writer.write('-', ' ');
03458                 ++s;
03459             }
03460         }
03461 
03462         writer.write('-', '-', '>');
03463     }
03464 
03465     PUGI__FN void node_output_pi_value(xml_buffered_writer& writer, const char_t* s)
03466     {
03467         while (*s)
03468         {
03469             const char_t* prev = s;
03470 
03471             // look for ?> sequence - we can't output it since ?> terminates PI
03472             while (*s && !(s[0] == '?' && s[1] == '>')) ++s;
03473 
03474             writer.write_buffer(prev, static_cast<size_t>(s - prev));
03475 
03476             if (*s)
03477             {
03478                 assert(s[0] == '?' && s[1] == '>');
03479 
03480                 writer.write('?', ' ', '>');
03481                 s += 2;
03482             }
03483         }
03484     }
03485 
03486     PUGI__FN void node_output_attributes(xml_buffered_writer& writer, xml_node_struct* node, unsigned int flags)
03487     {
03488         const char_t* default_name = PUGIXML_TEXT(":anonymous");
03489 
03490         for (xml_attribute_struct* a = node->first_attribute; a; a = a->next_attribute)
03491         {
03492             writer.write(' ');
03493             writer.write_string(a->name ? a->name : default_name);
03494             writer.write('=', '"');
03495 
03496             if (a->value)
03497                 text_output(writer, a->value, ctx_special_attr, flags);
03498 
03499             writer.write('"');
03500         }
03501     }
03502 
03503     PUGI__FN bool node_output_start(xml_buffered_writer& writer, xml_node_struct* node, unsigned int flags)
03504     {
03505         const char_t* default_name = PUGIXML_TEXT(":anonymous");
03506         const char_t* name = node->name ? node->name : default_name;
03507 
03508         writer.write('<');
03509         writer.write_string(name);
03510 
03511         if (node->first_attribute)
03512             node_output_attributes(writer, node, flags);
03513 
03514         if (!node->first_child)
03515         {
03516             writer.write(' ', '/', '>');
03517 
03518             return false;
03519         }
03520         else
03521         {
03522             writer.write('>');
03523 
03524             return true;
03525         }
03526     }
03527 
03528     PUGI__FN void node_output_end(xml_buffered_writer& writer, xml_node_struct* node)
03529     {
03530         const char_t* default_name = PUGIXML_TEXT(":anonymous");
03531         const char_t* name = node->name ? node->name : default_name;
03532 
03533         writer.write('<', '/');
03534         writer.write_string(name);
03535         writer.write('>');
03536     }
03537 
03538     PUGI__FN void node_output_simple(xml_buffered_writer& writer, xml_node_struct* node, unsigned int flags)
03539     {
03540         const char_t* default_name = PUGIXML_TEXT(":anonymous");
03541 
03542         switch (PUGI__NODETYPE(node))
03543         {
03544             case node_pcdata:
03545                 text_output(writer, node->value ? node->value : PUGIXML_TEXT(""), ctx_special_pcdata, flags);
03546                 break;
03547 
03548             case node_cdata:
03549                 text_output_cdata(writer, node->value ? node->value : PUGIXML_TEXT(""));
03550                 break;
03551 
03552             case node_comment:
03553                 node_output_comment(writer, node->value ? node->value : PUGIXML_TEXT(""));
03554                 break;
03555 
03556             case node_pi:
03557                 writer.write('<', '?');
03558                 writer.write_string(node->name ? node->name : default_name);
03559 
03560                 if (node->value)
03561                 {
03562                     writer.write(' ');
03563                     node_output_pi_value(writer, node->value);
03564                 }
03565 
03566                 writer.write('?', '>');
03567                 break;
03568 
03569             case node_declaration:
03570                 writer.write('<', '?');
03571                 writer.write_string(node->name ? node->name : default_name);
03572                 node_output_attributes(writer, node, flags);
03573                 writer.write('?', '>');
03574                 break;
03575 
03576             case node_doctype:
03577                 writer.write('<', '!', 'D', 'O', 'C');
03578                 writer.write('T', 'Y', 'P', 'E');
03579 
03580                 if (node->value)
03581                 {
03582                     writer.write(' ');
03583                     writer.write_string(node->value);
03584                 }
03585 
03586                 writer.write('>');
03587                 break;
03588 
03589             default:
03590                 assert(!"Invalid node type");
03591         }
03592     }
03593 
03594     enum indent_flags_t
03595     {
03596         indent_newline = 1,
03597         indent_indent = 2
03598     };
03599 
03600     PUGI__FN void node_output(xml_buffered_writer& writer, xml_node_struct* root, const char_t* indent, unsigned int flags, unsigned int depth)
03601     {
03602         size_t indent_length = ((flags & (format_indent | format_raw)) == format_indent) ? strlength(indent) : 0;
03603         unsigned int indent_flags = indent_indent;
03604 
03605         xml_node_struct* node = root;
03606 
03607         do
03608         {
03609             assert(node);
03610 
03611             // begin writing current node
03612             if (PUGI__NODETYPE(node) == node_pcdata || PUGI__NODETYPE(node) == node_cdata)
03613             {
03614                 node_output_simple(writer, node, flags);
03615 
03616                 indent_flags = 0;
03617             }
03618             else
03619             {
03620                 if ((indent_flags & indent_newline) && (flags & format_raw) == 0)
03621                     writer.write('\n');
03622 
03623                 if ((indent_flags & indent_indent) && indent_length)
03624                     text_output_indent(writer, indent, indent_length, depth);
03625 
03626                 if (PUGI__NODETYPE(node) == node_element)
03627                 {
03628                     indent_flags = indent_newline | indent_indent;
03629 
03630                     if (node_output_start(writer, node, flags))
03631                     {
03632                         node = node->first_child;
03633                         depth++;
03634                         continue;
03635                     }
03636                 }
03637                 else if (PUGI__NODETYPE(node) == node_document)
03638                 {
03639                     indent_flags = indent_indent;
03640 
03641                     if (node->first_child)
03642                     {
03643                         node = node->first_child;
03644                         continue;
03645                     }
03646                 }
03647                 else
03648                 {
03649                     node_output_simple(writer, node, flags);
03650 
03651                     indent_flags = indent_newline | indent_indent;
03652                 }
03653             }
03654 
03655             // continue to the next node
03656             while (node != root)
03657             {
03658                 if (node->next_sibling)
03659                 {
03660                     node = node->next_sibling;
03661                     break;
03662                 }
03663 
03664                 node = node->parent;
03665 
03666                 // write closing node
03667                 if (PUGI__NODETYPE(node) == node_element)
03668                 {
03669                     depth--;
03670 
03671                     if ((indent_flags & indent_newline) && (flags & format_raw) == 0)
03672                         writer.write('\n');
03673 
03674                     if ((indent_flags & indent_indent) && indent_length)
03675                         text_output_indent(writer, indent, indent_length, depth);
03676 
03677                     node_output_end(writer, node);
03678 
03679                     indent_flags = indent_newline | indent_indent;
03680                 }
03681             }
03682         }
03683         while (node != root);
03684 
03685         if ((indent_flags & indent_newline) && (flags & format_raw) == 0)
03686             writer.write('\n');
03687     }
03688 
03689     PUGI__FN bool has_declaration(xml_node_struct* node)
03690     {
03691         for (xml_node_struct* child = node->first_child; child; child = child->next_sibling)
03692         {
03693             xml_node_type type = PUGI__NODETYPE(child);
03694 
03695             if (type == node_declaration) return true;
03696             if (type == node_element) return false;
03697         }
03698 
03699         return false;
03700     }
03701 
03702     PUGI__FN bool is_attribute_of(xml_attribute_struct* attr, xml_node_struct* node)
03703     {
03704         for (xml_attribute_struct* a = node->first_attribute; a; a = a->next_attribute)
03705             if (a == attr)
03706                 return true;
03707 
03708         return false;
03709     }
03710 
03711     PUGI__FN bool allow_insert_attribute(xml_node_type parent)
03712     {
03713         return parent == node_element || parent == node_declaration;
03714     }
03715 
03716     PUGI__FN bool allow_insert_child(xml_node_type parent, xml_node_type child)
03717     {
03718         if (parent != node_document && parent != node_element) return false;
03719         if (child == node_document || child == node_null) return false;
03720         if (parent != node_document && (child == node_declaration || child == node_doctype)) return false;
03721 
03722         return true;
03723     }
03724 
03725     PUGI__FN bool allow_move(xml_node parent, xml_node child)
03726     {
03727         // check that child can be a child of parent
03728         if (!allow_insert_child(parent.type(), child.type()))
03729             return false;
03730 
03731         // check that node is not moved between documents
03732         if (parent.root() != child.root())
03733             return false;
03734 
03735         // check that new parent is not in the child subtree
03736         xml_node cur = parent;
03737 
03738         while (cur)
03739         {
03740             if (cur == child)
03741                 return false;
03742 
03743             cur = cur.parent();
03744         }
03745 
03746         return true;
03747     }
03748 
03749     PUGI__FN void node_copy_string(char_t*& dest, uintptr_t& header, uintptr_t header_mask, char_t* source, uintptr_t& source_header, xml_allocator* alloc)
03750     {
03751         assert(!dest && (header & header_mask) == 0);
03752 
03753         if (source)
03754         {
03755             if (alloc && (source_header & header_mask) == 0)
03756             {
03757                 dest = source;
03758 
03759                 // since strcpy_insitu can reuse document buffer memory we need to mark both source and dest as shared
03760                 header |= xml_memory_page_contents_shared_mask;
03761                 source_header |= xml_memory_page_contents_shared_mask;
03762             }
03763             else
03764                 strcpy_insitu(dest, header, header_mask, source);
03765         }
03766     }
03767 
03768     PUGI__FN void node_copy_contents(xml_node_struct* dn, xml_node_struct* sn, xml_allocator* shared_alloc)
03769     {
03770         node_copy_string(dn->name, dn->header, xml_memory_page_name_allocated_mask, sn->name, sn->header, shared_alloc);
03771         node_copy_string(dn->value, dn->header, xml_memory_page_value_allocated_mask, sn->value, sn->header, shared_alloc);
03772 
03773         for (xml_attribute_struct* sa = sn->first_attribute; sa; sa = sa->next_attribute)
03774         {
03775             xml_attribute_struct* da = append_new_attribute(dn, get_allocator(dn));
03776 
03777             if (da)
03778             {
03779                 node_copy_string(da->name, da->header, xml_memory_page_name_allocated_mask, sa->name, sa->header, shared_alloc);
03780                 node_copy_string(da->value, da->header, xml_memory_page_value_allocated_mask, sa->value, sa->header, shared_alloc);
03781             }
03782         }
03783     }
03784 
03785     PUGI__FN void node_copy_tree(xml_node_struct* dn, xml_node_struct* sn)
03786     {
03787         xml_allocator& alloc = get_allocator(dn);
03788         xml_allocator* shared_alloc = (&alloc == &get_allocator(sn)) ? &alloc : 0;
03789 
03790         node_copy_contents(dn, sn, shared_alloc);
03791 
03792         xml_node_struct* dit = dn;
03793         xml_node_struct* sit = sn->first_child;
03794 
03795         while (sit && sit != sn)
03796         {
03797             if (sit != dn)
03798             {
03799                 xml_node_struct* copy = append_new_node(dit, alloc, PUGI__NODETYPE(sit));
03800 
03801                 if (copy)
03802                 {
03803                     node_copy_contents(copy, sit, shared_alloc);
03804 
03805                     if (sit->first_child)
03806                     {
03807                         dit = copy;
03808                         sit = sit->first_child;
03809                         continue;
03810                     }
03811                 }
03812             }
03813 
03814             // continue to the next node
03815             do
03816             {
03817                 if (sit->next_sibling)
03818                 {
03819                     sit = sit->next_sibling;
03820                     break;
03821                 }
03822 
03823                 sit = sit->parent;
03824                 dit = dit->parent;
03825             }
03826             while (sit != sn);
03827         }
03828     }
03829 
03830     inline bool is_text_node(xml_node_struct* node)
03831     {
03832         xml_node_type type = PUGI__NODETYPE(node);
03833 
03834         return type == node_pcdata || type == node_cdata;
03835     }

03837     // get value with conversion functions
03838     PUGI__FN int get_integer_base(const char_t* value)
03839     {
03840         const char_t* s = value;
03841 
03842         while (PUGI__IS_CHARTYPE(*s, ct_space))
03843             s++;
03844 
03845         if (*s == '-')
03846             s++;
03847 
03848         return (s[0] == '0' && (s[1] == 'x' || s[1] == 'X')) ? 16 : 10;
03849     }
03850 
03851     PUGI__FN int get_value_int(const char_t* value, int def)
03852     {
03853         if (!value) return def;
03854 
03855         int base = get_integer_base(value);
03856 
03857     #ifdef PUGIXML_WCHAR_MODE
03858         return static_cast<int>(wcstol(value, 0, base));
03859     #else
03860         return static_cast<int>(strtol(value, 0, base));
03861     #endif
03862     }

03899     PUGI__FN bool get_value_bool(const char_t* value, bool def)
03900     {
03901         if (!value) return def;
03902 
03903         // only look at first char
03904         char_t first = *value;
03905 
03906         // 1*, t* (true), T* (True), y* (yes), Y* (YES)
03907         return (first == '1' || first == 't' || first == 'T' || first == 'y' || first == 'Y');
03908     }

04021 
04022     // we need to get length of entire file to load it in memory; the only (relatively) sane way to do it is via seek/tell trick
04023     PUGI__FN xml_parse_status get_file_size(FILE* file, size_t& out_result)
04024     {
04025     #if defined(PUGI__MSVC_CRT_VERSION) && PUGI__MSVC_CRT_VERSION >= 1400 && !defined(_WIN32_WCE)
04026         // there are 64-bit versions of fseek/ftell, let's use them
04027         typedef __int64 length_type;
04028 
04029         _fseeki64(file, 0, SEEK_END);
04030         length_type length = _ftelli64(file);
04031         _fseeki64(file, 0, SEEK_SET);
04032     #elif defined(__MINGW32__) && !defined(__NO_MINGW_LFS) && (!defined(__STRICT_ANSI__) || defined(__MINGW64_VERSION_MAJOR))
04033         // there are 64-bit versions of fseek/ftell, let's use them
04034         typedef off64_t length_type;
04035 
04036         fseeko64(file, 0, SEEK_END);
04037         length_type length = ftello64(file);
04038         fseeko64(file, 0, SEEK_SET);
04039     #else
04040         // if this is a 32-bit OS, long is enough; if this is a unix system, long is 64-bit, which is enough; otherwise we can't do anything anyway.
04041         typedef long length_type;
04042 
04043         fseek(file, 0, SEEK_END);
04044         length_type length = ftell(file);
04045         fseek(file, 0, SEEK_SET);
04046     #endif
04047 
04048         // check for I/O errors
04049         if (length < 0) return status_io_error;
04050         
04051         // check for overflow
04052         size_t result = static_cast<size_t>(length);
04053 
04054         if (static_cast<length_type>(result) != length) return status_out_of_memory;
04055 
04056         // finalize
04057         out_result = result;
04058 
04059         return status_ok;
04060     }
04061 
04062     PUGI__FN size_t zero_terminate_buffer(void* buffer, size_t size, xml_encoding encoding) 
04063     {
04064         // We only need to zero-terminate if encoding conversion does not do it for us
04065     #ifdef PUGIXML_WCHAR_MODE
04066         xml_encoding wchar_encoding = get_wchar_encoding();
04067 
04068         if (encoding == wchar_encoding || need_endian_swap_utf(encoding, wchar_encoding))
04069         {
04070             size_t length = size / sizeof(char_t);
04071 
04072             static_cast<char_t*>(buffer)[length] = 0;
04073             return (length + 1) * sizeof(char_t);
04074         }
04075     #else
04076         if (encoding == encoding_utf8)
04077         {
04078             static_cast<char*>(buffer)[size] = 0;
04079             return size + 1;
04080         }
04081     #endif
04082 
04083         return size;
04084     }
04085 
04086     PUGI__FN xml_parse_result load_file_impl(xml_document& doc, FILE* file, unsigned int options, xml_encoding encoding)
04087     {
04088         if (!file) return make_parse_result(status_file_not_found);
04089 
04090         // get file size (can result in I/O errors)
04091         size_t size = 0;
04092         xml_parse_status size_status = get_file_size(file, size);
04093 
04094         if (size_status != status_ok)
04095         {
04096             fclose(file);
04097             return make_parse_result(size_status);
04098         }
04099         
04100         size_t max_suffix_size = sizeof(char_t);
04101 
04102         // allocate buffer for the whole file
04103         char* contents = static_cast<char*>(xml_memory::allocate(size + max_suffix_size));
04104 
04105         if (!contents)
04106         {
04107             fclose(file);
04108             return make_parse_result(status_out_of_memory);
04109         }
04110 
04111         // read file in memory
04112         size_t read_size = fread(contents, 1, size, file);
04113         fclose(file);
04114 
04115         if (read_size != size)
04116         {
04117             xml_memory::deallocate(contents);
04118             return make_parse_result(status_io_error);
04119         }
04120 
04121         xml_encoding real_encoding = get_buffer_encoding(encoding, contents, size);
04122         
04123         return doc.load_buffer_inplace_own(contents, zero_terminate_buffer(contents, size, real_encoding), options, real_encoding);
04124     }
04125 
04126 #ifndef PUGIXML_NO_STL
04127     template <typename T> struct xml_stream_chunk
04128     {
04129         static xml_stream_chunk* create()
04130         {
04131             void* memory = xml_memory::allocate(sizeof(xml_stream_chunk));
04132             
04133             return new (memory) xml_stream_chunk();
04134         }
04135 
04136         static void destroy(void* ptr)
04137         {
04138             xml_stream_chunk* chunk = static_cast<xml_stream_chunk*>(ptr);
04139 
04140             // free chunk chain
04141             while (chunk)
04142             {
04143                 xml_stream_chunk* next_ = chunk->next;
04144 
04145                 xml_memory::deallocate(chunk);
04146 
04147                 chunk = next_;
04148             }
04149         }
04150 
04151         xml_stream_chunk(): next(0), size(0)
04152         {
04153         }
04154 
04155         xml_stream_chunk* next;
04156         size_t size;
04157 
04158         T data[xml_memory_page_size / sizeof(T)];
04159     };
04160 
04161     template <typename T> PUGI__FN xml_parse_status load_stream_data_noseek(std::basic_istream<T>& stream, void** out_buffer, size_t* out_size)
04162     {
04163         buffer_holder chunks(0, xml_stream_chunk<T>::destroy);
04164 
04165         // read file to a chunk list
04166         size_t total = 0;
04167         xml_stream_chunk<T>* last = 0;
04168 
04169         while (!stream.eof())
04170         {
04171             // allocate new chunk
04172             xml_stream_chunk<T>* chunk = xml_stream_chunk<T>::create();
04173             if (!chunk) return status_out_of_memory;
04174 
04175             // append chunk to list
04176             if (last) last = last->next = chunk;
04177             else chunks.data = last = chunk;
04178 
04179             // read data to chunk
04180             stream.read(chunk->data, static_cast<std::streamsize>(sizeof(chunk->data) / sizeof(T)));
04181             chunk->size = static_cast<size_t>(stream.gcount()) * sizeof(T);
04182 
04183             // read may set failbit | eofbit in case gcount() is less than read length, so check for other I/O errors
04184             if (stream.bad() || (!stream.eof() && stream.fail())) return status_io_error;
04185 
04186             // guard against huge files (chunk size is small enough to make this overflow check work)
04187             if (total + chunk->size < total) return status_out_of_memory;
04188             total += chunk->size;
04189         }
04190 
04191         size_t max_suffix_size = sizeof(char_t);
04192 
04193         // copy chunk list to a contiguous buffer
04194         char* buffer = static_cast<char*>(xml_memory::allocate(total + max_suffix_size));
04195         if (!buffer) return status_out_of_memory;
04196 
04197         char* write = buffer;
04198 
04199         for (xml_stream_chunk<T>* chunk = static_cast<xml_stream_chunk<T>*>(chunks.data); chunk; chunk = chunk->next)
04200         {
04201             assert(write + chunk->size <= buffer + total);
04202             memcpy(write, chunk->data, chunk->size);
04203             write += chunk->size;
04204         }
04205 
04206         assert(write == buffer + total);
04207 
04208         // return buffer
04209         *out_buffer = buffer;
04210         *out_size = total;
04211 
04212         return status_ok;
04213     }
04214 
04215     template <typename T> PUGI__FN xml_parse_status load_stream_data_seek(std::basic_istream<T>& stream, void** out_buffer, size_t* out_size)
04216     {
04217         // get length of remaining data in stream
04218         typename std::basic_istream<T>::pos_type pos = stream.tellg();
04219         stream.seekg(0, std::ios::end);
04220         std::streamoff length = stream.tellg() - pos;
04221         stream.seekg(pos);
04222 
04223         if (stream.fail() || pos < 0) return status_io_error;
04224 
04225         // guard against huge files
04226         size_t read_length = static_cast<size_t>(length);
04227 
04228         if (static_cast<std::streamsize>(read_length) != length || length < 0) return status_out_of_memory;
04229 
04230         size_t max_suffix_size = sizeof(char_t);
04231 
04232         // read stream data into memory (guard against stream exceptions with buffer holder)
04233         buffer_holder buffer(xml_memory::allocate(read_length * sizeof(T) + max_suffix_size), xml_memory::deallocate);
04234         if (!buffer.data) return status_out_of_memory;
04235 
04236         stream.read(static_cast<T*>(buffer.data), static_cast<std::streamsize>(read_length));
04237 
04238         // read may set failbit | eofbit in case gcount() is less than read_length (i.e. line ending conversion), so check for other I/O errors
04239         if (stream.bad() || (!stream.eof() && stream.fail())) return status_io_error;
04240 
04241         // return buffer
04242         size_t actual_length = static_cast<size_t>(stream.gcount());
04243         assert(actual_length <= read_length);
04244         
04245         *out_buffer = buffer.release();
04246         *out_size = actual_length * sizeof(T);
04247 
04248         return status_ok;
04249     }
04250 
04251     template <typename T> PUGI__FN xml_parse_result load_stream_impl(xml_document& doc, std::basic_istream<T>& stream, unsigned int options, xml_encoding encoding)
04252     {
04253         void* buffer = 0;
04254         size_t size = 0;
04255         xml_parse_status status = status_ok;
04256 
04257         // if stream has an error bit set, bail out (otherwise tellg() can fail and we'll clear error bits)
04258         if (stream.fail()) return make_parse_result(status_io_error);
04259 
04260         // load stream to memory (using seek-based implementation if possible, since it's faster and takes less memory)
04261         if (stream.tellg() < 0)
04262         {
04263             stream.clear(); // clear error flags that could be set by a failing tellg
04264             status = load_stream_data_noseek(stream, &buffer, &size);
04265         }
04266         else
04267             status = load_stream_data_seek(stream, &buffer, &size);
04268 
04269         if (status != status_ok) return make_parse_result(status);
04270 
04271         xml_encoding real_encoding = get_buffer_encoding(encoding, buffer, size);
04272         
04273         return doc.load_buffer_inplace_own(buffer, zero_terminate_buffer(buffer, size, real_encoding), options, real_encoding);
04274     }
04275 #endif
04276 
04277 #if defined(PUGI__MSVC_CRT_VERSION) || defined(__BORLANDC__) || (defined(__MINGW32__) && (!defined(__STRICT_ANSI__) || defined(__MINGW64_VERSION_MAJOR)))
04278     PUGI__FN FILE* open_file_wide(const wchar_t* path, const wchar_t* mode)
04279     {
04280         return _wfopen(path, mode);
04281     }
04282 #else
04283     PUGI__FN char* convert_path_heap(const wchar_t* str)
04284     {
04285         assert(str);
04286 
04287         // first pass: get length in utf8 characters
04288         size_t length = strlength_wide(str);
04289         size_t size = as_utf8_begin(str, length);
04290 
04291         // allocate resulting string
04292         char* result = static_cast<char*>(xml_memory::allocate(size + 1));
04293         if (!result) return 0;
04294 
04295         // second pass: convert to utf8
04296         as_utf8_end(result, size, str, length);
04297 
04298         return result;
04299     }
04300 
04301     PUGI__FN FILE* open_file_wide(const wchar_t* path, const wchar_t* mode)
04302     {
04303         // there is no standard function to open wide paths, so our best bet is to try utf8 path
04304         char* path_utf8 = convert_path_heap(path);
04305         if (!path_utf8) return 0;
04306 
04307         // convert mode to ASCII (we mirror _wfopen interface)
04308         char mode_ascii[4] = {0};
04309         for (size_t i = 0; mode[i]; ++i) mode_ascii[i] = static_cast<char>(mode[i]);
04310 
04311         // try to open the utf8 path
04312         FILE* result = fopen(path_utf8, mode_ascii);
04313 
04314         // free dummy buffer
04315         xml_memory::deallocate(path_utf8);
04316 
04317         return result;
04318     }
04319 #endif
04320 
04321     PUGI__FN bool save_file_impl(const xml_document& doc, FILE* file, const char_t* indent, unsigned int flags, xml_encoding encoding)
04322     {
04323         if (!file) return false;
04324 
04325         xml_writer_file writer(file);
04326         doc.save(writer, indent, flags, encoding);
04327 
04328         int result = ferror(file);
04329 
04330         fclose(file);
04331 
04332         return result == 0;
04333     }
04334 
04335     PUGI__FN xml_parse_result load_buffer_impl(xml_document_struct* doc, xml_node_struct* root, void* contents, size_t size, unsigned int options, xml_encoding encoding, bool is_mutable, bool own, char_t** out_buffer)
04336     {
04337         // check input buffer
04338         if (!contents && size) return make_parse_result(status_io_error);
04339 
04340         // get actual encoding
04341         xml_encoding buffer_encoding = impl::get_buffer_encoding(encoding, contents, size);
04342 
04343         // get private buffer
04344         char_t* buffer = 0;
04345         size_t length = 0;
04346 
04347         if (!impl::convert_buffer(buffer, length, buffer_encoding, contents, size, is_mutable)) return impl::make_parse_result(status_out_of_memory);
04348         
04349         // delete original buffer if we performed a conversion
04350         if (own && buffer != contents && contents) impl::xml_memory::deallocate(contents);
04351 
04352         // store buffer for offset_debug
04353         doc->buffer = buffer;
04354 
04355         // parse
04356         xml_parse_result res = impl::xml_parser::parse(buffer, length, doc, root, options);
04357 
04358         // remember encoding
04359         res.encoding = buffer_encoding;
04360 
04361         // grab onto buffer if it's our buffer, user is responsible for deallocating contents himself
04362         if (own || buffer != contents) *out_buffer = buffer;
04363 
04364         return res;
04365     }
04366 PUGI__NS_END
04367

04375     {
04376         size_t result = fwrite(data, 1, size, static_cast<FILE*>(file));
04377         (void)!result; // unfortunately we can't do proper error handling here
04378     }

04389     PUGI__FN void xml_writer_stream::write(const void* data, size_t size)
04390     {
04391         if (narrow_stream)
04392         {
04393             assert(!wide_stream);
04394             narrow_stream->write(reinterpret_cast<const char*>(data), static_cast<std::streamsize>(size));
04395         }
04396         else
04397         {
04398             assert(wide_stream);
04399             assert(size % sizeof(wchar_t) == 0);
04400 
04401             wide_stream->write(reinterpret_cast<const wchar_t*>(data), static_cast<std::streamsize>(size / sizeof(wchar_t)));
04402         }
04403     }
04404 #endif

04792     PUGI__FN xml_node xml_node::child(const char_t* name_) const
04793     {
04794         if (!_root) return xml_node();
04795 
04796         for (xml_node_struct* i = _root->first_child; i; i = i->next_sibling)
04797             if (i->name && impl::strequal(name_, i->name)) return xml_node(i);
04798 
04799         return xml_node();
04800     }
04801 
04802     PUGI__FN xml_attribute xml_node::attribute(const char_t* name_) const
04803     {
04804         if (!_root) return xml_attribute();
04805 
04806         for (xml_attribute_struct* i = _root->first_attribute; i; i = i->next_attribute)
04807             if (i->name && impl::strequal(name_, i->name))
04808                 return xml_attribute(i);
04809         
04810         return xml_attribute();
04811     }

04813     PUGI__FN xml_node xml_node::next_sibling(const char_t* name_) const
04814     {
04815         if (!_root) return xml_node();
04816         
04817         for (xml_node_struct* i = _root->next_sibling; i; i = i->next_sibling)
04818             if (i->name && impl::strequal(name_, i->name)) return xml_node(i);
04819 
04820         return xml_node();
04821     }

04833             if (i->name && impl::strequal(name_, i->name)) return xml_node(i);
04834
