04897     PUGI__FN bool xml_node::set_name(const char_t* rhs)
04898     {
04899         switch (type())
04900         {
04901         case node_pi:
04902         case node_declaration:
04903         case node_element:
04904             return impl::strcpy_insitu(_root->name, _root->header, impl::xml_memory_page_name_allocated_mask, rhs);
04905 
04906         default:
04907             return false;
04908         }
04909     }
04910         
04911     PUGI__FN bool xml_node::set_value(const char_t* rhs)
04912     {
04913         switch (type())
04914         {
04915         case node_pi:
04916         case node_cdata:
04917         case node_pcdata:
04918         case node_comment:
04919         case node_doctype:
04920             return impl::strcpy_insitu(_root->value, _root->header, impl::xml_memory_page_value_allocated_mask, rhs);
04921 
04922         default:
04923             return false;
04924         }
04925     }
04926 
04927     PUGI__FN xml_attribute xml_node::append_attribute(const char_t* name_)
04928     {
04929         if (!impl::allow_insert_attribute(type())) return xml_attribute();
04930         
04931         xml_attribute a(impl::allocate_attribute(impl::get_allocator(_root)));
04932         if (!a) return xml_attribute();
04933 
04934         impl::append_attribute(a._attr, _root);
04935 
04936         a.set_name(name_);
04937         
04938         return a;
04939     }
04940 
04941     PUGI__FN xml_attribute xml_node::prepend_attribute(const char_t* name_)
04942     {
04943         if (!impl::allow_insert_attribute(type())) return xml_attribute();
04944         
04945         xml_attribute a(impl::allocate_attribute(impl::get_allocator(_root)));
04946         if (!a) return xml_attribute();
04947 
04948         impl::prepend_attribute(a._attr, _root);
04949 
04950         a.set_name(name_);
04951 
04952         return a;
04953     }
04954 
04955     PUGI__FN xml_attribute xml_node::insert_attribute_after(const char_t* name_, const xml_attribute& attr)
04956     {
04957         if (!impl::allow_insert_attribute(type())) return xml_attribute();
04958         if (!attr || !impl::is_attribute_of(attr._attr, _root)) return xml_attribute();
04959         
04960         xml_attribute a(impl::allocate_attribute(impl::get_allocator(_root)));
04961         if (!a) return xml_attribute();
04962 
04963         impl::insert_attribute_after(a._attr, attr._attr, _root);
04964 
04965         a.set_name(name_);
04966 
04967         return a;
04968     }
04969 
04970     PUGI__FN xml_attribute xml_node::insert_attribute_before(const char_t* name_, const xml_attribute& attr)
04971     {
04972         if (!impl::allow_insert_attribute(type())) return xml_attribute();
04973         if (!attr || !impl::is_attribute_of(attr._attr, _root)) return xml_attribute();
04974         
04975         xml_attribute a(impl::allocate_attribute(impl::get_allocator(_root)));
04976         if (!a) return xml_attribute();
04977 
04978         impl::insert_attribute_before(a._attr, attr._attr, _root);
04979 
04980         a.set_name(name_);
04981 
04982         return a;
04983     }

04988

04990         result.set_value(proto.value());

04995     PUGI__FN xml_attribute xml_node::prepend_copy(const xml_attribute& proto)

04997         if (!proto) return xml_attribute();
04998

05000         result.set_value(proto.value());

05005     PUGI__FN xml_attribute xml_node::insert_copy_after(const xml_attribute& proto, const xml_attribute& attr)
05006     {
05007         if (!proto) return xml_attribute();
05008 
05009         xml_attribute result = insert_attribute_after(proto.name(), attr);
05010         result.set_value(proto.value());
05011 
05012         return result;
05013     }
05014 
05015     PUGI__FN xml_attribute xml_node::insert_copy_before(const xml_attribute& proto, const xml_attribute& attr)
05016     {
05017         if (!proto) return xml_attribute();
05018 
05019         xml_attribute result = insert_attribute_before(proto.name(), attr);
05020         result.set_value(proto.value());
05021 
05022         return result;
05023     }

05025     PUGI__FN xml_node xml_node::append_child(xml_node_type type_)
05026     {
05027         if (!impl::allow_insert_child(type(), type_)) return xml_node();
05028         
05029         xml_node n(impl::allocate_node(impl::get_allocator(_root), type_));
05030         if (!n) return xml_node();
05031 
05032         impl::append_node(n._root, _root);
05033 
05034         if (type_ == node_declaration) n.set_name(PUGIXML_TEXT("xml"));
05035 
05036         return n;
05037     }

05040     {
05041         if (!impl::allow_insert_child(type(), type_)) return xml_node();
05042         
05043         xml_node n(impl::allocate_node(impl::get_allocator(_root), type_));
05044         if (!n) return xml_node();
05045 
05046         impl::prepend_node(n._root, _root);
05047                 
05048         if (type_ == node_declaration) n.set_name(PUGIXML_TEXT("xml"));
05049 
05050         return n;
05051     }

05054     {
05055         if (!impl::allow_insert_child(type(), type_)) return xml_node();
05056         if (!node._root || node._root->parent != _root) return xml_node();
05057     
05058         xml_node n(impl::allocate_node(impl::get_allocator(_root), type_));
05059         if (!n) return xml_node();
05060 
05061         impl::insert_node_before(n._root, node._root);
05062 
05063         if (type_ == node_declaration) n.set_name(PUGIXML_TEXT("xml"));
05064 
05065         return n;

05177     PUGI__FN xml_node xml_node::append_move(const xml_node& moved)
05178     {
05179         if (!impl::allow_move(*this, moved)) return xml_node();
05180 
05181         // disable document_buffer_order optimization since moving nodes around changes document order without changing buffer pointers
05182         impl::get_document(_root).header |= impl::xml_memory_page_contents_shared_mask;
05183 
05184         impl::remove_node(moved._root);
05185         impl::append_node(moved._root, _root);
05186 
05187         return moved;
05188     }
05189 
05190     PUGI__FN xml_node xml_node::prepend_move(const xml_node& moved)
05191     {
05192         if (!impl::allow_move(*this, moved)) return xml_node();
05193 
05194         // disable document_buffer_order optimization since moving nodes around changes document order without changing buffer pointers
05195         impl::get_document(_root).header |= impl::xml_memory_page_contents_shared_mask;
05196 
05197         impl::remove_node(moved._root);
05198         impl::prepend_node(moved._root, _root);
05199 
05200         return moved;
05201     }
05202 
05203     PUGI__FN xml_node xml_node::insert_move_after(const xml_node& moved, const xml_node& node)
05204     {
05205         if (!impl::allow_move(*this, moved)) return xml_node();
05206         if (!node._root || node._root->parent != _root) return xml_node();
05207         if (moved._root == node._root) return xml_node();
05208 
05209         // disable document_buffer_order optimization since moving nodes around changes document order without changing buffer pointers
05210         impl::get_document(_root).header |= impl::xml_memory_page_contents_shared_mask;
05211 
05212         impl::remove_node(moved._root);
05213         impl::insert_node_after(moved._root, node._root);
05214 
05215         return moved;
05216     }
05217 
05218     PUGI__FN xml_node xml_node::insert_move_before(const xml_node& moved, const xml_node& node)
05219     {
05220         if (!impl::allow_move(*this, moved)) return xml_node();
05221         if (!node._root || node._root->parent != _root) return xml_node();
05222         if (moved._root == node._root) return xml_node();
05223 
05224         // disable document_buffer_order optimization since moving nodes around changes document order without changing buffer pointers
05225         impl::get_document(_root).header |= impl::xml_memory_page_contents_shared_mask;
05226 
05227         impl::remove_node(moved._root);
05228         impl::insert_node_before(moved._root, node._root);
05229 
05230         return moved;
05231     }

05238     PUGI__FN bool xml_node::remove_attribute(const xml_attribute& a)
05239     {
05240         if (!_root || !a._attr) return false;
05241         if (!impl::is_attribute_of(a._attr, _root)) return false;
05242 
05243         impl::remove_attribute(a._attr, _root);
05244         impl::destroy_attribute(a._attr, impl::get_allocator(_root));
05245 
05246         return true;
05247     }

05254     PUGI__FN bool xml_node::remove_child(const xml_node& n)
05255     {
05256         if (!_root || !n._root || n._root->parent != _root) return false;
05257 
05258         impl::remove_node(n._root);
05259         impl::destroy_node(n._root, impl::get_allocator(_root));
05260 
05261         return true;
05262     }
05263 
05264     PUGI__FN xml_parse_result xml_node::append_buffer(const void* contents, size_t size, unsigned int options, xml_encoding encoding)
05265     {
05266         // append_buffer is only valid for elements/documents
05267         if (!impl::allow_insert_child(type(), node_element)) return impl::make_parse_result(status_append_invalid_root);
05268 
05269         // get document node
05270         impl::xml_document_struct* doc = &impl::get_document(_root);
05271 
05272         // disable document_buffer_order optimization since in a document with multiple buffers comparing buffer pointers does not make sense
05273         doc->header |= impl::xml_memory_page_contents_shared_mask;
05274         
05275         // get extra buffer element (we'll store the document fragment buffer there so that we can deallocate it later)
05276         impl::xml_memory_page* page = 0;
05277         impl::xml_extra_buffer* extra = static_cast<impl::xml_extra_buffer*>(doc->allocate_memory(sizeof(impl::xml_extra_buffer), page));
05278         (void)page;
05279 
05280         if (!extra) return impl::make_parse_result(status_out_of_memory);
05281 
05282         // save name; name of the root has to be NULL before parsing - otherwise closing node mismatches will not be detected at the top level
05283         char_t* rootname = _root->name;
05284         _root->name = 0;
05285 
05286         // parse
05287         char_t* buffer = 0;
05288         xml_parse_result res = impl::load_buffer_impl(doc, _root, const_cast<void*>(contents), size, options, encoding, false, false, &buffer);
05289 
05290         // restore name
05291         _root->name = rootname;
05292 
05293         // add extra buffer to the list
05294         extra->buffer = buffer;
05295         extra->next = doc->extra_buffers;
05296         doc->extra_buffers = extra;
05297 
05298         return res;
05299     }
05300 
05301     PUGI__FN xml_node xml_node::find_child_by_attribute(const char_t* name_, const char_t* attr_name, const char_t* attr_value) const
05302     {
05303         if (!_root) return xml_node();
05304         
05305         for (xml_node_struct* i = _root->first_child; i; i = i->next_sibling)
05306             if (i->name && impl::strequal(name_, i->name))
05307             {
05308                 for (xml_attribute_struct* a = i->first_attribute; a; a = a->next_attribute)
05309                     if (a->name && impl::strequal(attr_name, a->name) && impl::strequal(attr_value, a->value ? a->value : PUGIXML_TEXT("")))
05310                         return xml_node(i);
05311             }
05312 
05313         return xml_node();
05314     }
05315 
05316     PUGI__FN xml_node xml_node::find_child_by_attribute(const char_t* attr_name, const char_t* attr_value) const
05317     {
05318         if (!_root) return xml_node();
05319         
05320         for (xml_node_struct* i = _root->first_child; i; i = i->next_sibling)
05321             for (xml_attribute_struct* a = i->first_attribute; a; a = a->next_attribute)
05322                 if (a->name && impl::strequal(attr_name, a->name) && impl::strequal(attr_value, a->value ? a->value : PUGIXML_TEXT("")))
05323                     return xml_node(i);
05324 
05325         return xml_node();
05326     }

05328 #ifndef PUGIXML_NO_STL
05329     PUGI__FN string_t xml_node::path(char_t delimiter) const
05330     {
05331         xml_node cursor = *this; // Make a copy.
05332         
05333         string_t result = cursor.name();
05334 
05335         while (cursor.parent())
05336         {
05337             cursor = cursor.parent();
05338             
05339             string_t temp = cursor.name();
05340             temp += delimiter;
05341             temp += result;
05342             result.swap(temp);
05343         }
05344 
05345         return result;
05346     }
05347 #endif
05348 
05349     PUGI__FN xml_node xml_node::first_element_by_path(const char_t* path_, char_t delimiter) const
05350     {
05351         xml_node found = *this; // Current search context.
05352 
05353         if (!_root || !path_ || !path_[0]) return found;
05354 
05355         if (path_[0] == delimiter)
05356         {
05357             // Absolute path; e.g. '/foo/bar'
05358             found = found.root();
05359             ++path_;
05360         }
05361 
05362         const char_t* path_segment = path_;
05363 
05364         while (*path_segment == delimiter) ++path_segment;
05365 
05366         const char_t* path_segment_end = path_segment;
05367 
05368         while (*path_segment_end && *path_segment_end != delimiter) ++path_segment_end;
05369 
05370         if (path_segment == path_segment_end) return found;
05371 
05372         const char_t* next_segment = path_segment_end;
05373 
05374         while (*next_segment == delimiter) ++next_segment;
05375 
05376         if (*path_segment == '.' && path_segment + 1 == path_segment_end)
05377             return found.first_element_by_path(next_segment, delimiter);
05378         else if (*path_segment == '.' && *(path_segment+1) == '.' && path_segment + 2 == path_segment_end)
05379             return found.parent().first_element_by_path(next_segment, delimiter);
05380         else
05381         {
05382             for (xml_node_struct* j = found._root->first_child; j; j = j->next_sibling)
05383             {
05384                 if (j->name && impl::strequalrange(j->name, path_segment, static_cast<size_t>(path_segment_end - path_segment)))
05385                 {
05386                     xml_node subsearch = xml_node(j).first_element_by_path(next_segment, delimiter);
05387 
05388                     if (subsearch) return subsearch;
05389                 }
05390             }
05391 
05392             return xml_node();
05393         }
05394     }
05395 
05396     PUGI__FN bool xml_node::traverse(xml_tree_walker& walker)
05397     {
05398         walker._depth = -1;
05399         
05400         xml_node arg_begin = *this;
05401         if (!walker.begin(arg_begin)) return false;
05402 
05403         xml_node cur = first_child();
05404                 
05405         if (cur)
05406         {
05407             ++walker._depth;
05408 
05409             do 
05410             {
05411                 xml_node arg_for_each = cur;
05412                 if (!walker.for_each(arg_for_each))
05413                     return false;
05414                         
05415                 if (cur.first_child())
05416                 {
05417                     ++walker._depth;
05418                     cur = cur.first_child();
05419                 }
05420                 else if (cur.next_sibling())
05421                     cur = cur.next_sibling();
05422                 else
05423                 {
05424                     // Borland C++ workaround
05425                     while (!cur.next_sibling() && cur != *this && !cur.parent().empty())
05426                     {
05427                         --walker._depth;
05428                         cur = cur.parent();
05429                     }
05430                         
05431                     if (cur != *this)
05432                         cur = cur.next_sibling();
05433                 }
05434             }
05435             while (cur && cur != *this);
05436         }
05437 
05438         assert(walker._depth == -1);
05439 
05440         xml_node arg_end = *this;
05441         return walker.end(arg_end);
05442     }
05443

05447     }

05478 
05479     PUGI__FN ptrdiff_t xml_node::offset_debug() const
05480     {
05481         if (!_root) return -1;
05482 
05483         impl::xml_document_struct& doc = impl::get_document(_root);
05484 
05485         // we can determine the offset reliably only if there is exactly once parse buffer
05486         if (!doc.buffer || doc.extra_buffers) return -1;
05487 
05488         switch (type())
05489         {
05490         case node_document:
05491             return 0;
05492 
05493         case node_element:
05494         case node_declaration:
05495         case node_pi:
05496             return _root->name && (_root->header & impl::xml_memory_page_name_allocated_or_shared_mask) == 0 ? _root->name - doc.buffer : -1;
05497 
05498         case node_pcdata:
05499         case node_cdata:
05500         case node_comment:
05501         case node_doctype:
05502             return _root->value && (_root->header & impl::xml_memory_page_value_allocated_or_shared_mask) == 0 ? _root->value - doc.buffer : -1;
05503 
05504         default:
05505             return -1;
05506         }
05507     }
05508

05531                 return node;
05532 
05533         return 0;
05534     }

05915         assert(_wrap._root);
05916         _wrap = _wrap.next_sibling(_name);
05917         return *this;
05918     }

05924         return temp;

05927     PUGI__FN const xml_named_node_iterator& xml_named_node_iterator::operator--()
05928     {
05929         if (_wrap._root)
05930             _wrap = _wrap.previous_sibling(_name);
05931         else
05932         {
05933             _wrap = _parent.last_child();
05934 
05935             if (!impl::strequal(_wrap.name(), _name))
05936                 _wrap = _wrap.previous_sibling(_name);
05937         }
05938 
05939         return *this;
05940     }

05951     }

05953     PUGI__FN xml_parse_result::operator bool() const
05954     {
05955         return status == status_ok;
05956     }
05957 
05958     PUGI__FN const char* xml_parse_result::description() const
05959     {
05960         switch (status)
05961         {
05962         case status_ok: return "No error";
05963 
05964         case status_file_not_found: return "File was not found";
05965         case status_io_error: return "Error reading from file/stream";
05966         case status_out_of_memory: return "Could not allocate memory";
05967         case status_internal_error: return "Internal error occurred";
05968 
05969         case status_unrecognized_tag: return "Could not determine tag type";
05970 
05971         case status_bad_pi: return "Error parsing document declaration/processing instruction";
05972         case status_bad_comment: return "Error parsing comment";
05973         case status_bad_cdata: return "Error parsing CDATA section";
05974         case status_bad_doctype: return "Error parsing document type declaration";
05975         case status_bad_pcdata: return "Error parsing PCDATA section";
05976         case status_bad_start_element: return "Error parsing start element tag";
05977         case status_bad_attribute: return "Error parsing element attribute";
05978         case status_bad_end_element: return "Error parsing end element tag";
05979         case status_end_element_mismatch: return "Start-end tags mismatch";
05980 
05981         case status_append_invalid_root: return "Unable to append nodes: root is not an element or document";
05982 
05983         case status_no_document_element: return "No document element found";
05984 
05985         default: return "Unknown error";
05986         }
05987     }

05999     PUGI__FN void xml_document::reset()
06000     {
06001         destroy();
06002         create();
06003     }
06004 
06005     PUGI__FN void xml_document::reset(const xml_document& proto)
06006     {
06007         reset();
06008 
06009         for (xml_node cur = proto.first_child(); cur; cur = cur.next_sibling())
06010             append_copy(cur);
06011     }
06012 
06013     PUGI__FN void xml_document::create()
06014     {
06015         assert(!_root);
06016 
06017         // initialize sentinel page
06018         PUGI__STATIC_ASSERT(sizeof(impl::xml_memory_page) + sizeof(impl::xml_document_struct) + impl::xml_memory_page_alignment - sizeof(void*) <= sizeof(_memory));
06019 
06020         // align upwards to page boundary
06021         void* page_memory = reinterpret_cast<void*>((reinterpret_cast<uintptr_t>(_memory) + (impl::xml_memory_page_alignment - 1)) & ~(impl::xml_memory_page_alignment - 1));
06022 
06023         // prepare page structure
06024         impl::xml_memory_page* page = impl::xml_memory_page::construct(page_memory);
06025         assert(page);
06026 
06027         page->busy_size = impl::xml_memory_page_size;
06028 
06029         // allocate new root
06030         _root = new (reinterpret_cast<char*>(page) + sizeof(impl::xml_memory_page)) impl::xml_document_struct(page);
06031         _root->prev_sibling_c = _root;
06032 
06033         // setup sentinel page
06034         page->allocator = static_cast<impl::xml_document_struct*>(_root);
06035 
06036         // verify the document allocation
06037         assert(reinterpret_cast<char*>(_root) + sizeof(impl::xml_document_struct) <= _memory + sizeof(_memory));
06038     }
06039 
06040     PUGI__FN void xml_document::destroy()
06041     {
06042         assert(_root);
06043 
06044         // destroy static storage
06045         if (_buffer)
06046         {
06047             impl::xml_memory::deallocate(_buffer);
06048             _buffer = 0;
06049         }
06050 
06051         // destroy extra buffers (note: no need to destroy linked list nodes, they're allocated using document allocator)
06052         for (impl::xml_extra_buffer* extra = static_cast<impl::xml_document_struct*>(_root)->extra_buffers; extra; extra = extra->next)
06053         {
06054             if (extra->buffer) impl::xml_memory::deallocate(extra->buffer);
06055         }
06056 
06057         // destroy dynamic storage, leave sentinel page (it's in static memory)
06058         impl::xml_memory_page* root_page = reinterpret_cast<impl::xml_memory_page*>(_root->header & impl::xml_memory_page_pointer_mask);
06059         assert(root_page && !root_page->prev);
06060         assert(reinterpret_cast<char*>(root_page) >= _memory && reinterpret_cast<char*>(root_page) < _memory + sizeof(_memory));
06061 
06062         for (impl::xml_memory_page* page = root_page->next; page; )
06063         {
06064             impl::xml_memory_page* next = page->next;
06065 
06066             impl::xml_allocator::deallocate_page(page);
06067 
06068             page = next;
06069         }
06070 
06071         _root = 0;
06072     }

06146     PUGI__FN void xml_document::save(xml_writer& writer, const char_t* indent, unsigned int flags, xml_encoding encoding) const
06147     {
06148         impl::xml_buffered_writer buffered_writer(writer, encoding);
06149 
06150         if ((flags & format_write_bom) && encoding != encoding_latin1)
06151         {
06152             // BOM always represents the codepoint U+FEFF, so just write it in native encoding
06153         #ifdef PUGIXML_WCHAR_MODE
06154             unsigned int bom = 0xfeff;
06155             buffered_writer.write(static_cast<wchar_t>(bom));
06156         #else
06157             buffered_writer.write('\xef', '\xbb', '\xbf');
06158         #endif
06159         }
06160 
06161         if (!(flags & format_no_declaration) && !impl::has_declaration(_root))
06162         {
06163             buffered_writer.write_string(PUGIXML_TEXT("<?xml version=\"1.0\""));
06164             if (encoding == encoding_latin1) buffered_writer.write_string(PUGIXML_TEXT(" encoding=\"ISO-8859-1\""));
06165             buffered_writer.write('?', '>');
06166             if (!(flags & format_raw)) buffered_writer.write('\n');
06167         }
06168 
06169         impl::node_output(buffered_writer, _root, indent, flags, 0);
06170     }
06171 
06172 #ifndef PUGIXML_NO_STL
06173     PUGI__FN void xml_document::save(std::basic_ostream<char, std::char_traits<char> >& stream, const char_t* indent, unsigned int flags, xml_encoding encoding) const
06174     {
06175         xml_writer_stream writer(stream);
06176 
06177         save(writer, indent, flags, encoding);
06178     }

06200     PUGI__FN xml_node xml_document::document_element() const
06201     {
06202         assert(_root);
06203 
06204         for (xml_node_struct* i = _root->first_child; i; i = i->next_sibling)
06205             if (PUGI__NODETYPE(i) == node_element)
06206                 return xml_node(i);
06207 
06208         return xml_node();
06209     }

06268     PUGI__FN std::bidirectional_iterator_tag _Iter_cat(const pugi::xml_named_node_iterator&)
06269     {

06297 // STL replacements
06298 PUGI__NS_BEGIN
06299     struct equal_to
06300     {
06301         template <typename T> bool operator()(const T& lhs, const T& rhs) const
06302         {
06303             return lhs == rhs;
06304         }
06305     };
06306 
06307     struct not_equal_to
06308     {
06309         template <typename T> bool operator()(const T& lhs, const T& rhs) const
06310         {
06311             return lhs != rhs;
06312         }
06313     };
06314 
06315     struct less
06316     {
06317         template <typename T> bool operator()(const T& lhs, const T& rhs) const
06318         {
06319             return lhs < rhs;
06320         }
06321     };
06322 
06323     struct less_equal
06324     {
06325         template <typename T> bool operator()(const T& lhs, const T& rhs) const
06326         {
06327             return lhs <= rhs;
06328         }
06329     };
06330 
06331     template <typename T> void swap(T& lhs, T& rhs)
06332     {
06333         T temp = lhs;
06334         lhs = rhs;
06335         rhs = temp;
06336     }
06337 
06338     template <typename I, typename Pred> I min_element(I begin, I end, const Pred& pred)
06339     {
06340         I result = begin;
06341 
06342         for (I it = begin + 1; it != end; ++it)
06343             if (pred(*it, *result))
06344                 result = it;
06345 
06346         return result;
06347     }
06348 
06349     template <typename I> void reverse(I begin, I end)
06350     {
06351         while (end - begin > 1) swap(*begin++, *--end);
06352     }
06353 
06354     template <typename I> I unique(I begin, I end)
06355     {
06356         // fast skip head
06357         while (end - begin > 1 && *begin != *(begin + 1)) begin++;
06358 
06359         if (begin == end) return begin;
06360 
06361         // last written element
06362         I write = begin++; 
06363 
06364         // merge unique elements
06365         while (begin != end)
06366         {
06367             if (*begin != *write)
06368                 *++write = *begin++;
06369             else
06370                 begin++;
06371         }
06372 
06373         // past-the-end (write points to live element)
06374         return write + 1;
06375     }
06376 
06377     template <typename I> void copy_backwards(I begin, I end, I target)
06378     {
06379         while (begin != end) *--target = *--end;
06380     }
06381 
06382     template <typename I, typename Pred, typename T> void insertion_sort(I begin, I end, const Pred& pred, T*)
06383     {
06384         assert(begin != end);
06385 
06386         for (I it = begin + 1; it != end; ++it)
06387         {
06388             T val = *it;
06389 
06390             if (pred(val, *begin))
06391             {
06392                 // move to front
06393                 copy_backwards(begin, it, it + 1);
06394                 *begin = val;
06395             }
06396             else
06397             {
06398                 I hole = it;
06399 
06400                 // move hole backwards
06401                 while (pred(val, *(hole - 1)))
06402                 {
06403                     *hole = *(hole - 1);
06404                     hole--;
06405                 }
06406 
06407                 // fill hole with element
06408                 *hole = val;
06409             }
06410         }
06411     }
06412 
06413     // std variant for elements with ==
06414     template <typename I, typename Pred> void partition(I begin, I middle, I end, const Pred& pred, I* out_eqbeg, I* out_eqend)
06415     {
06416         I eqbeg = middle, eqend = middle + 1;
06417 
06418         // expand equal range
06419         while (eqbeg != begin && *(eqbeg - 1) == *eqbeg) --eqbeg;
06420         while (eqend != end && *eqend == *eqbeg) ++eqend;
06421 
06422         // process outer elements
06423         I ltend = eqbeg, gtbeg = eqend;
06424 
06425         for (;;)
06426         {
06427             // find the element from the right side that belongs to the left one
06428             for (; gtbeg != end; ++gtbeg)
06429                 if (!pred(*eqbeg, *gtbeg))
06430                 {
06431                     if (*gtbeg == *eqbeg) swap(*gtbeg, *eqend++);
06432                     else break;
06433                 }
06434 
06435             // find the element from the left side that belongs to the right one
06436             for (; ltend != begin; --ltend)
06437                 if (!pred(*(ltend - 1), *eqbeg))
06438                 {
06439                     if (*eqbeg == *(ltend - 1)) swap(*(ltend - 1), *--eqbeg);
06440                     else break;
06441                 }
06442 
06443             // scanned all elements
06444             if (gtbeg == end && ltend == begin)
06445             {
06446                 *out_eqbeg = eqbeg;
06447                 *out_eqend = eqend;
06448                 return;
06449             }
06450 
06451             // make room for elements by moving equal area
06452             if (gtbeg == end)
06453             {
06454                 if (--ltend != --eqbeg) swap(*ltend, *eqbeg);
06455                 swap(*eqbeg, *--eqend);
06456             }
06457             else if (ltend == begin)
06458             {
06459                 if (eqend != gtbeg) swap(*eqbeg, *eqend);
06460                 ++eqend;
06461                 swap(*gtbeg++, *eqbeg++);
06462             }
06463             else swap(*gtbeg++, *--ltend);
06464         }
06465     }
06466 
06467     template <typename I, typename Pred> void median3(I first, I middle, I last, const Pred& pred)
06468     {
06469         if (pred(*middle, *first)) swap(*middle, *first);
06470         if (pred(*last, *middle)) swap(*last, *middle);
06471         if (pred(*middle, *first)) swap(*middle, *first);
06472     }
06473 
06474     template <typename I, typename Pred> void median(I first, I middle, I last, const Pred& pred)
06475     {
06476         if (last - first <= 40)
06477         {
06478             // median of three for small chunks
06479             median3(first, middle, last, pred);
06480         }
06481         else
06482         {
06483             // median of nine
06484             size_t step = (last - first + 1) / 8;
06485 
06486             median3(first, first + step, first + 2 * step, pred);
06487             median3(middle - step, middle, middle + step, pred);
06488             median3(last - 2 * step, last - step, last, pred);
06489             median3(first + step, middle, last - step, pred);
06490         }
06491     }
06492 
06493     template <typename I, typename Pred> void sort(I begin, I end, const Pred& pred)
06494     {
06495         // sort large chunks
06496         while (end - begin > 32)
06497         {
06498             // find median element
06499             I middle = begin + (end - begin) / 2;
06500             median(begin, middle, end - 1, pred);
06501 
06502             // partition in three chunks (< = >)
06503             I eqbeg, eqend;
06504             partition(begin, middle, end, pred, &eqbeg, &eqend);
06505 
06506             // loop on larger half
06507             if (eqbeg - begin > end - eqend)
06508             {
06509                 sort(eqend, end, pred);
06510                 end = eqbeg;
06511             }
06512             else
06513             {
06514                 sort(begin, eqbeg, pred);
06515                 begin = eqend;
06516             }
06517         }
06518 
06519         // insertion sort small chunk
06520         if (begin != end) insertion_sort(begin, end, pred, &*begin);
06521     }
06522 PUGI__NS_END
06523 
06524 // Allocator used for AST and evaluation stacks
06525 PUGI__NS_BEGIN
06526     struct xpath_memory_block
06527     {   
06528         xpath_memory_block* next;
06529         size_t capacity;
06530 
06531         char data[
06532     #ifdef PUGIXML_MEMORY_XPATH_PAGE_SIZE
06533             PUGIXML_MEMORY_XPATH_PAGE_SIZE
06534     #else
06535             4096
06536     #endif
06537         ];
06538     };
06539         
06540     class xpath_allocator
06541     {
06542         xpath_memory_block* _root;
06543         size_t _root_size;
06544 
06545     public:
06546     #ifdef PUGIXML_NO_EXCEPTIONS
06547         jmp_buf* error_handler;
06548     #endif
06549 
06550         xpath_allocator(xpath_memory_block* root, size_t root_size = 0): _root(root), _root_size(root_size)
06551         {
06552         #ifdef PUGIXML_NO_EXCEPTIONS
06553             error_handler = 0;
06554         #endif
06555         }
06556         
06557         void* allocate_nothrow(size_t size)
06558         {
06559             // align size so that we're able to store pointers in subsequent blocks
06560             size = (size + sizeof(void*) - 1) & ~(sizeof(void*) - 1);
06561 
06562             if (_root_size + size <= _root->capacity)
06563             {
06564                 void* buf = _root->data + _root_size;
06565                 _root_size += size;
06566                 return buf;
06567             }
06568             else
06569             {
06570                 // make sure we have at least 1/4th of the page free after allocation to satisfy subsequent allocation requests
06571                 size_t block_capacity_base = sizeof(_root->data);
06572                 size_t block_capacity_req = size + block_capacity_base / 4;
06573                 size_t block_capacity = (block_capacity_base > block_capacity_req) ? block_capacity_base : block_capacity_req;
06574 
06575                 size_t block_size = block_capacity + offsetof(xpath_memory_block, data);
06576 
06577                 xpath_memory_block* block = static_cast<xpath_memory_block*>(xml_memory::allocate(block_size));
06578                 if (!block) return 0;
06579                 
06580                 block->next = _root;
06581                 block->capacity = block_capacity;
06582                 
06583                 _root = block;
06584                 _root_size = size;
06585                 
06586                 return block->data;
06587             }
06588         }
06589 
06590         void* allocate(size_t size)
06591         {
06592             void* result = allocate_nothrow(size);
06593 
06594             if (!result)
06595             {
06596             #ifdef PUGIXML_NO_EXCEPTIONS
06597                 assert(error_handler);
06598                 longjmp(*error_handler, 1);
06599             #else
06600                 throw std::bad_alloc();
06601             #endif
06602             }
06603 
06604             return result;
06605         }
06606 
06607         void* reallocate(void* ptr, size_t old_size, size_t new_size)
06608         {
06609             // align size so that we're able to store pointers in subsequent blocks
06610             old_size = (old_size + sizeof(void*) - 1) & ~(sizeof(void*) - 1);
06611             new_size = (new_size + sizeof(void*) - 1) & ~(sizeof(void*) - 1);
06612 
06613             // we can only reallocate the last object
06614             assert(ptr == 0 || static_cast<char*>(ptr) + old_size == _root->data + _root_size);
06615 
06616             // adjust root size so that we have not allocated the object at all
06617             bool only_object = (_root_size == old_size);
06618 
06619             if (ptr) _root_size -= old_size;
06620 
06621             // allocate a new version (this will obviously reuse the memory if possible)
06622             void* result = allocate(new_size);
06623             assert(result);
06624 
06625             // we have a new block
06626             if (result != ptr && ptr)
06627             {
06628                 // copy old data
06629                 assert(new_size >= old_size);
06630                 memcpy(result, ptr, old_size);
06631 
06632                 // free the previous page if it had no other objects
06633                 if (only_object)
06634                 {
06635                     assert(_root->data == result);
06636                     assert(_root->next);
06637 
06638                     xpath_memory_block* next = _root->next->next;
06639 
06640                     if (next)
06641                     {
06642                         // deallocate the whole page, unless it was the first one
06643                         xml_memory::deallocate(_root->next);
06644                         _root->next = next;
06645                     }
06646                 }
06647             }
06648 
06649             return result;
06650         }
06651 
06652         void revert(const xpath_allocator& state)
06653         {
06654             // free all new pages
06655             xpath_memory_block* cur = _root;
06656 
06657             while (cur != state._root)
06658             {
06659                 xpath_memory_block* next = cur->next;
06660 
06661                 xml_memory::deallocate(cur);
06662 
06663                 cur = next;
06664             }
06665 
06666             // restore state
06667             _root = state._root;
06668             _root_size = state._root_size;
06669         }
06670 
06671         void release()
06672         {
06673             xpath_memory_block* cur = _root;
06674             assert(cur);
06675 
06676             while (cur->next)
06677             {
06678                 xpath_memory_block* next = cur->next;
06679 
06680                 xml_memory::deallocate(cur);
06681 
06682                 cur = next;
06683             }
06684         }
06685     };
06686 
06687     struct xpath_allocator_capture
06688     {
06689         xpath_allocator_capture(xpath_allocator* alloc): _target(alloc), _state(*alloc)
06690         {
06691         }
06692 
06693         ~xpath_allocator_capture()
06694         {
06695             _target->revert(_state);
06696         }
06697 
06698         xpath_allocator* _target;
06699         xpath_allocator _state;
06700     };
06701 
06702     struct xpath_stack
06703     {
06704         xpath_allocator* result;
06705         xpath_allocator* temp;
06706     };
06707 
06708     struct xpath_stack_data
06709     {
06710         xpath_memory_block blocks[2];
06711         xpath_allocator result;
06712         xpath_allocator temp;
06713         xpath_stack stack;
06714 
06715     #ifdef PUGIXML_NO_EXCEPTIONS
06716         jmp_buf error_handler;
06717     #endif
06718 
06719         xpath_stack_data(): result(blocks + 0), temp(blocks + 1)
06720         {
06721             blocks[0].next = blocks[1].next = 0;
06722             blocks[0].capacity = blocks[1].capacity = sizeof(blocks[0].data);
06723 
06724             stack.result = &result;
06725             stack.temp = &temp;
06726 
06727         #ifdef PUGIXML_NO_EXCEPTIONS
06728             result.error_handler = temp.error_handler = &error_handler;
06729         #endif
06730         }
06731 
06732         ~xpath_stack_data()
06733         {
06734             result.release();
06735             temp.release();
06736         }
06737     };
06738 PUGI__NS_END
06739 
06740 // String class
06741 PUGI__NS_BEGIN
06742     class xpath_string
06743     {
06744         const char_t* _buffer;
06745         bool _uses_heap;
06746         size_t _length_heap;
06747 
06748         static char_t* duplicate_string(const char_t* string, size_t length, xpath_allocator* alloc)
06749         {
06750             char_t* result = static_cast<char_t*>(alloc->allocate((length + 1) * sizeof(char_t)));
06751             assert(result);
06752 
06753             memcpy(result, string, length * sizeof(char_t));
06754             result[length] = 0;
06755 
06756             return result;
06757         }
06758 
06759         xpath_string(const char_t* buffer, bool uses_heap_, size_t length_heap): _buffer(buffer), _uses_heap(uses_heap_), _length_heap(length_heap)
06760         {
06761         }
06762 
06763     public:
06764         static xpath_string from_const(const char_t* str)
06765         {
06766             return xpath_string(str, false, 0);
06767         }
06768 
06769         static xpath_string from_heap_preallocated(const char_t* begin, const char_t* end)
06770         {
06771             assert(begin <= end && *end == 0);
06772 
06773             return xpath_string(begin, true, static_cast<size_t>(end - begin));
06774         }
06775 
06776         static xpath_string from_heap(const char_t* begin, const char_t* end, xpath_allocator* alloc)
06777         {
06778             assert(begin <= end);
06779 
06780             size_t length = static_cast<size_t>(end - begin);
06781 
06782             return length == 0 ? xpath_string() : xpath_string(duplicate_string(begin, length, alloc), true, length);
06783         }
06784 
06785         xpath_string(): _buffer(PUGIXML_TEXT("")), _uses_heap(false), _length_heap(0)
06786         {
06787         }
06788 
06789         void append(const xpath_string& o, xpath_allocator* alloc)
06790         {
06791             // skip empty sources
06792             if (!*o._buffer) return;
06793 
06794             // fast append for constant empty target and constant source
06795             if (!*_buffer && !_uses_heap && !o._uses_heap)
06796             {
06797                 _buffer = o._buffer;
06798             }
06799             else
06800             {
06801                 // need to make heap copy
06802                 size_t target_length = length();
06803                 size_t source_length = o.length();
06804                 size_t result_length = target_length + source_length;
06805 
06806                 // allocate new buffer
06807                 char_t* result = static_cast<char_t*>(alloc->reallocate(_uses_heap ? const_cast<char_t*>(_buffer) : 0, (target_length + 1) * sizeof(char_t), (result_length + 1) * sizeof(char_t)));
06808                 assert(result);
06809 
06810                 // append first string to the new buffer in case there was no reallocation
06811                 if (!_uses_heap) memcpy(result, _buffer, target_length * sizeof(char_t));
06812 
06813                 // append second string to the new buffer
06814                 memcpy(result + target_length, o._buffer, source_length * sizeof(char_t));
06815                 result[result_length] = 0;
06816 
06817                 // finalize
06818                 _buffer = result;
06819                 _uses_heap = true;
06820                 _length_heap = result_length;
06821             }
06822         }
06823 
06824         const char_t* c_str() const
06825         {
06826             return _buffer;
06827         }
06828 
06829         size_t length() const
06830         {
06831             return _uses_heap ? _length_heap : strlength(_buffer);
06832         }
06833         
06834         char_t* data(xpath_allocator* alloc)
06835         {
06836             // make private heap copy
06837             if (!_uses_heap)
06838             {
06839                 size_t length_ = strlength(_buffer);
06840 
06841                 _buffer = duplicate_string(_buffer, length_, alloc);
06842                 _uses_heap = true;
06843                 _length_heap = length_;
06844             }
06845 
06846             return const_cast<char_t*>(_buffer);
06847         }
06848 
06849         bool empty() const
06850         {
06851             return *_buffer == 0;
06852         }
06853 
06854         bool operator==(const xpath_string& o) const
06855         {
06856             return strequal(_buffer, o._buffer);
06857         }
06858 
06859         bool operator!=(const xpath_string& o) const
06860         {
06861             return !strequal(_buffer, o._buffer);
06862         }
06863 
06864         bool uses_heap() const
06865         {
06866             return _uses_heap;
06867         }
06868     };
06869 PUGI__NS_END
06870 
06871 PUGI__NS_BEGIN
06872     PUGI__FN bool starts_with(const char_t* string, const char_t* pattern)
06873     {
06874         while (*pattern && *string == *pattern)
06875         {
06876             string++;
06877             pattern++;
06878         }
06879 
06880         return *pattern == 0;
06881     }
06882 
06883     PUGI__FN const char_t* find_char(const char_t* s, char_t c)
06884     {
06885     #ifdef PUGIXML_WCHAR_MODE
06886         return wcschr(s, c);
06887     #else
06888         return strchr(s, c);
06889     #endif
06890     }
06891 
06892     PUGI__FN const char_t* find_substring(const char_t* s, const char_t* p)
06893     {
06894     #ifdef PUGIXML_WCHAR_MODE
06895         // MSVC6 wcsstr bug workaround (if s is empty it always returns 0)
06896         return (*p == 0) ? s : wcsstr(s, p);
06897     #else
06898         return strstr(s, p);
06899     #endif
06900     }
06901 
06902     // Converts symbol to lower case, if it is an ASCII one
06903     PUGI__FN char_t tolower_ascii(char_t ch)
06904     {
06905         return static_cast<unsigned int>(ch - 'A') < 26 ? static_cast<char_t>(ch | ' ') : ch;
06906     }
06907 
06908     PUGI__FN xpath_string string_value(const xpath_node& na, xpath_allocator* alloc)
06909     {
06910         if (na.attribute())
06911             return xpath_string::from_const(na.attribute().value());
06912         else
06913         {
06914             xml_node n = na.node();
06915 
06916             switch (n.type())
06917             {
06918             case node_pcdata:
06919             case node_cdata:
06920             case node_comment:
06921             case node_pi:
06922                 return xpath_string::from_const(n.value());
06923             
06924             case node_document:
06925             case node_element:
06926             {
06927                 xpath_string result;
06928 
06929                 xml_node cur = n.first_child();
06930                 
06931                 while (cur && cur != n)
06932                 {
06933                     if (cur.type() == node_pcdata || cur.type() == node_cdata)
06934                         result.append(xpath_string::from_const(cur.value()), alloc);
06935 
06936                     if (cur.first_child())
06937                         cur = cur.first_child();
06938                     else if (cur.next_sibling())
06939                         cur = cur.next_sibling();
06940                     else
06941                     {
06942                         while (!cur.next_sibling() && cur != n)
06943                             cur = cur.parent();
06944 
06945                         if (cur != n) cur = cur.next_sibling();
06946                     }
06947                 }
06948                 
06949                 return result;
06950             }
06951             
06952             default:
06953                 return xpath_string();
06954             }
06955         }
06956     }
06957     
06958     PUGI__FN bool node_is_before_sibling(xml_node_struct* ln, xml_node_struct* rn)
06959     {
06960         assert(ln->parent == rn->parent);
06961 
06962         // there is no common ancestor (the shared parent is null), nodes are from different documents
06963         if (!ln->parent) return ln < rn;
06964 
06965         // determine sibling order
06966         xml_node_struct* ls = ln;
06967         xml_node_struct* rs = rn;
06968 
06969         while (ls && rs)
06970         {
06971             if (ls == rn) return true;
06972             if (rs == ln) return false;
06973 
06974             ls = ls->next_sibling;
06975             rs = rs->next_sibling;
06976         }
06977 
06978         // if rn sibling chain ended ln must be before rn
06979         return !rs;
06980     }
06981     
06982     PUGI__FN bool node_is_before(xml_node_struct* ln, xml_node_struct* rn)
06983     {
06984         // find common ancestor at the same depth, if any
06985         xml_node_struct* lp = ln;
06986         xml_node_struct* rp = rn;
06987 
06988         while (lp && rp && lp->parent != rp->parent)
06989         {
06990             lp = lp->parent;
06991             rp = rp->parent;
06992         }
06993 
06994         // parents are the same!
06995         if (lp && rp) return node_is_before_sibling(lp, rp);
06996 
06997         // nodes are at different depths, need to normalize heights
06998         bool left_higher = !lp;
06999 
07000         while (lp)
07001         {
07002             lp = lp->parent;
07003             ln = ln->parent;
07004         }
07005 
07006         while (rp)
07007         {
07008             rp = rp->parent;
07009             rn = rn->parent;
07010         }
07011 
07012         // one node is the ancestor of the other
07013         if (ln == rn) return left_higher;
07014 
07015         // find common ancestor... again
07016         while (ln->parent != rn->parent)
07017         {
07018             ln = ln->parent;
07019             rn = rn->parent;
07020         }
07021 
07022         return node_is_before_sibling(ln, rn);
07023     }
07024 
07025     PUGI__FN bool node_is_ancestor(xml_node_struct* parent, xml_node_struct* node)
07026     {
07027         while (node && node != parent) node = node->parent;
07028 
07029         return parent && node == parent;
07030     }
07031 
07032     PUGI__FN const void* document_buffer_order(const xpath_node& xnode)
07033     {
07034         xml_node_struct* node = xnode.node().internal_object();
07035 
07036         if (node)
07037         {
07038             if ((get_document(node).header & xml_memory_page_contents_shared_mask) == 0)
07039             {
07040                 if (node->name && (node->header & impl::xml_memory_page_name_allocated_or_shared_mask) == 0) return node->name;
07041                 if (node->value && (node->header & impl::xml_memory_page_value_allocated_or_shared_mask) == 0) return node->value;
07042             }
07043 
07044             return 0;
07045         }
07046 
07047         xml_attribute_struct* attr = xnode.attribute().internal_object();
07048 
07049         if (attr)
07050         {
07051             if ((get_document(attr).header & xml_memory_page_contents_shared_mask) == 0)
07052             {
07053                 if ((attr->header & impl::xml_memory_page_name_allocated_or_shared_mask) == 0) return attr->name;
07054                 if ((attr->header & impl::xml_memory_page_value_allocated_or_shared_mask) == 0) return attr->value;
07055             }
07056 
07057             return 0;
07058         }
07059 
07060         return 0;
07061     }
07062     
07063     struct document_order_comparator
07064     {
07065         bool operator()(const xpath_node& lhs, const xpath_node& rhs) const
07066         {
07067             // optimized document order based check
07068             const void* lo = document_buffer_order(lhs);
07069             const void* ro = document_buffer_order(rhs);
07070 
07071             if (lo && ro) return lo < ro;
07072 
07073             // slow comparison
07074             xml_node ln = lhs.node(), rn = rhs.node();
07075 
07076             // compare attributes
07077             if (lhs.attribute() && rhs.attribute())
07078             {
07079                 // shared parent
07080                 if (lhs.parent() == rhs.parent())
07081                 {
07082                     // determine sibling order
07083                     for (xml_attribute a = lhs.attribute(); a; a = a.next_attribute())
07084                         if (a == rhs.attribute())
07085                             return true;
07086                     
07087                     return false;
07088                 }
07089                 
07090                 // compare attribute parents
07091                 ln = lhs.parent();
07092                 rn = rhs.parent();
07093             }
07094             else if (lhs.attribute())
07095             {
07096                 // attributes go after the parent element
07097                 if (lhs.parent() == rhs.node()) return false;
07098                 
07099                 ln = lhs.parent();
07100             }
07101             else if (rhs.attribute())
07102             {
07103                 // attributes go after the parent element
07104                 if (rhs.parent() == lhs.node()) return true;
07105                 
07106                 rn = rhs.parent();
07107             }
07108 
07109             if (ln == rn) return false;
07110 
07111             if (!ln || !rn) return ln < rn;
07112             
07113             return node_is_before(ln.internal_object(), rn.internal_object());
07114         }
07115     };
07116 
07117     struct duplicate_comparator
07118     {
07119         bool operator()(const xpath_node& lhs, const xpath_node& rhs) const
07120         {
07121             if (lhs.attribute()) return rhs.attribute() ? lhs.attribute() < rhs.attribute() : true;
07122             else return rhs.attribute() ? false : lhs.node() < rhs.node();
07123         }
07124     };
07125     
07126     PUGI__FN double gen_nan()
07127     {
07128     #if defined(__STDC_IEC_559__) || ((FLT_RADIX - 0 == 2) && (FLT_MAX_EXP - 0 == 128) && (FLT_MANT_DIG - 0 == 24))
07129         union { float f; uint32_t i; } u[sizeof(float) == sizeof(uint32_t) ? 1 : -1];
07130         u[0].i = 0x7fc00000;
07131         return u[0].f;
07132     #else
07133         // fallback
07134         const volatile double zero = 0.0;
07135         return zero / zero;
07136     #endif
07137     }
07138     
07139     PUGI__FN bool is_nan(double value)
07140     {
07141     #if defined(PUGI__MSVC_CRT_VERSION) || defined(__BORLANDC__)
07142         return !!_isnan(value);
07143     #elif defined(fpclassify) && defined(FP_NAN)
07144         return fpclassify(value) == FP_NAN;
07145     #else
07146         // fallback
07147         const volatile double v = value;
07148         return v != v;
07149     #endif
07150     }
07151     
07152     PUGI__FN const char_t* convert_number_to_string_special(double value)
07153     {
07154     #if defined(PUGI__MSVC_CRT_VERSION) || defined(__BORLANDC__)
07155         if (_finite(value)) return (value == 0) ? PUGIXML_TEXT("0") : 0;
07156         if (_isnan(value)) return PUGIXML_TEXT("NaN");
07157         return value > 0 ? PUGIXML_TEXT("Infinity") : PUGIXML_TEXT("-Infinity");
07158     #elif defined(fpclassify) && defined(FP_NAN) && defined(FP_INFINITE) && defined(FP_ZERO)
07159         switch (fpclassify(value))
07160         {
07161         case FP_NAN:
07162             return PUGIXML_TEXT("NaN");
07163 
07164         case FP_INFINITE:
07165             return value > 0 ? PUGIXML_TEXT("Infinity") : PUGIXML_TEXT("-Infinity");
07166 
07167         case FP_ZERO:
07168             return PUGIXML_TEXT("0");
07169 
07170         default:
07171             return 0;
07172         }
07173     #else
07174         // fallback
07175         const volatile double v = value;
07176 
07177         if (v == 0) return PUGIXML_TEXT("0");
07178         if (v != v) return PUGIXML_TEXT("NaN");
07179         if (v * 2 == v) return value > 0 ? PUGIXML_TEXT("Infinity") : PUGIXML_TEXT("-Infinity");
07180         return 0;
07181     #endif
07182     }
07183     
07184     PUGI__FN bool convert_number_to_boolean(double value)
07185     {
07186         return (value != 0 && !is_nan(value));
07187     }
07188     
07189     PUGI__FN void truncate_zeros(char* begin, char* end)
07190     {
07191         while (begin != end && end[-1] == '0') end--;
07192 
07193         *end = 0;
07194     }
07195 
07196     // gets mantissa digits in the form of 0.xxxxx with 0. implied and the exponent
07197 #if defined(PUGI__MSVC_CRT_VERSION) && PUGI__MSVC_CRT_VERSION >= 1400 && !defined(_WIN32_WCE)
07198     PUGI__FN void convert_number_to_mantissa_exponent(double value, char* buffer, size_t buffer_size, char** out_mantissa, int* out_exponent)
07199     {
07200         // get base values
07201         int sign, exponent;
07202         _ecvt_s(buffer, buffer_size, value, DBL_DIG + 1, &exponent, &sign);
07203 
07204         // truncate redundant zeros
07205         truncate_zeros(buffer, buffer + strlen(buffer));
07206 
07207         // fill results
07208         *out_mantissa = buffer;
07209         *out_exponent = exponent;
07210     }
07211 #else
07212     PUGI__FN void convert_number_to_mantissa_exponent(double value, char* buffer, size_t buffer_size, char** out_mantissa, int* out_exponent)
07213     {
07214         // get a scientific notation value with IEEE DBL_DIG decimals
07215         sprintf(buffer, "%.*e", DBL_DIG, value);
07216         assert(strlen(buffer) < buffer_size);
07217         (void)!buffer_size;
07218 
07219         // get the exponent (possibly negative)
07220         char* exponent_string = strchr(buffer, 'e');
07221         assert(exponent_string);
07222 
07223         int exponent = atoi(exponent_string + 1);
07224 
07225         // extract mantissa string: skip sign
07226         char* mantissa = buffer[0] == '-' ? buffer + 1 : buffer;
07227         assert(mantissa[0] != '0' && mantissa[1] == '.');
07228 
07229         // divide mantissa by 10 to eliminate integer part
07230         mantissa[1] = mantissa[0];
07231         mantissa++;
07232         exponent++;
07233 
07234         // remove extra mantissa digits and zero-terminate mantissa
07235         truncate_zeros(mantissa, exponent_string);
07236 
07237         // fill results
07238         *out_mantissa = mantissa;
07239         *out_exponent = exponent;
07240     }
07241 #endif
07242 
07243     PUGI__FN xpath_string convert_number_to_string(double value, xpath_allocator* alloc)
07244     {
07245         // try special number conversion
07246         const char_t* special = convert_number_to_string_special(value);
07247         if (special) return xpath_string::from_const(special);
07248 
07249         // get mantissa + exponent form
07250         char mantissa_buffer[32];
07251 
07252         char* mantissa;
07253         int exponent;
07254         convert_number_to_mantissa_exponent(value, mantissa_buffer, sizeof(mantissa_buffer), &mantissa, &exponent);
07255 
07256         // allocate a buffer of suitable length for the number
07257         size_t result_size = strlen(mantissa_buffer) + (exponent > 0 ? exponent : -exponent) + 4;
07258         char_t* result = static_cast<char_t*>(alloc->allocate(sizeof(char_t) * result_size));
07259         assert(result);
07260 
07261         // make the number!
07262         char_t* s = result;
07263 
07264         // sign
07265         if (value < 0) *s++ = '-';
07266 
07267         // integer part
07268         if (exponent <= 0)
07269         {
07270             *s++ = '0';
07271         }
07272         else
07273         {
07274             while (exponent > 0)
07275             {
07276                 assert(*mantissa == 0 || static_cast<unsigned int>(static_cast<unsigned int>(*mantissa) - '0') <= 9);
07277                 *s++ = *mantissa ? *mantissa++ : '0';
07278                 exponent--;
07279             }
07280         }
07281 
07282         // fractional part
07283         if (*mantissa)
07284         {
07285             // decimal point
07286             *s++ = '.';
07287 
07288             // extra zeroes from negative exponent
07289             while (exponent < 0)
07290             {
07291                 *s++ = '0';
07292                 exponent++;
07293             }
07294 
07295             // extra mantissa digits
07296             while (*mantissa)
07297             {
07298                 assert(static_cast<unsigned int>(*mantissa - '0') <= 9);
07299                 *s++ = *mantissa++;
07300             }
07301         }
07302 
07303         // zero-terminate
07304         assert(s < result + result_size);
07305         *s = 0;
07306 
07307         return xpath_string::from_heap_preallocated(result, s);
07308     }
07309     
07310     PUGI__FN bool check_string_to_number_format(const char_t* string)
07311     {
07312         // parse leading whitespace
07313         while (PUGI__IS_CHARTYPE(*string, ct_space)) ++string;
07314 
07315         // parse sign
07316         if (*string == '-') ++string;
07317 
07318         if (!*string) return false;
07319 
07320         // if there is no integer part, there should be a decimal part with at least one digit
07321         if (!PUGI__IS_CHARTYPEX(string[0], ctx_digit) && (string[0] != '.' || !PUGI__IS_CHARTYPEX(string[1], ctx_digit))) return false;
07322 
07323         // parse integer part
07324         while (PUGI__IS_CHARTYPEX(*string, ctx_digit)) ++string;
07325 
07326         // parse decimal part
07327         if (*string == '.')
07328         {
07329             ++string;
07330 
07331             while (PUGI__IS_CHARTYPEX(*string, ctx_digit)) ++string;
07332         }
07333 
07334         // parse trailing whitespace
07335         while (PUGI__IS_CHARTYPE(*string, ct_space)) ++string;
07336 
07337         return *string == 0;
07338     }
07339 
07340     PUGI__FN double convert_string_to_number(const char_t* string)
07341     {
07342         // check string format
07343         if (!check_string_to_number_format(string)) return gen_nan();
07344 
07345         // parse string
07346     #ifdef PUGIXML_WCHAR_MODE
07347         return wcstod(string, 0);
07348     #else
07349         return atof(string);
07350     #endif
07351     }
07352 
07353     PUGI__FN bool convert_string_to_number_scratch(char_t (&buffer)[32], const char_t* begin, const char_t* end, double* out_result)
07354     {
07355         size_t length = static_cast<size_t>(end - begin);
07356         char_t* scratch = buffer;
07357 
07358         if (length >= sizeof(buffer) / sizeof(buffer[0]))
07359         {
07360             // need to make dummy on-heap copy
07361             scratch = static_cast<char_t*>(xml_memory::allocate((length + 1) * sizeof(char_t)));
07362             if (!scratch) return false;
07363         }
07364 
07365         // copy string to zero-terminated buffer and perform conversion
07366         memcpy(scratch, begin, length * sizeof(char_t));
07367         scratch[length] = 0;
07368 
07369         *out_result = convert_string_to_number(scratch);
07370 
07371         // free dummy buffer
07372         if (scratch != buffer) xml_memory::deallocate(scratch);
07373 
07374         return true;
07375     }
07376     
07377     PUGI__FN double round_nearest(double value)
07378     {
07379         return floor(value + 0.5);
07380     }
07381 
07382     PUGI__FN double round_nearest_nzero(double value)
07383     {
07384         // same as round_nearest, but returns -0 for [-0.5, -0]
07385         // ceil is used to differentiate between +0 and -0 (we return -0 for [-0.5, -0] and +0 for +0)
07386         return (value >= -0.5 && value <= 0) ? ceil(value) : floor(value + 0.5);
07387     }

07389     PUGI__FN const char_t* qualified_name(const xpath_node& node)
07390     {
07391         return node.attribute() ? node.attribute().name() : node.node().name();
07392     }
07393     
07394     PUGI__FN const char_t* local_name(const xpath_node& node)
07395     {
07396         const char_t* name = qualified_name(node);
07397         const char_t* p = find_char(name, ':');
07398         
07399         return p ? p + 1 : name;
07400     }

07402     struct namespace_uri_predicate
07403     {
07404         const char_t* prefix;
07405         size_t prefix_length;
07406 
07407         namespace_uri_predicate(const char_t* name)
07408         {
07409             const char_t* pos = find_char(name, ':');
07410 
07411             prefix = pos ? name : 0;
07412             prefix_length = pos ? static_cast<size_t>(pos - name) : 0;
07413         }
07414 
07415         bool operator()(xml_attribute a) const
07416         {
07417             const char_t* name = a.name();
07418 
07419             if (!starts_with(name, PUGIXML_TEXT("xmlns"))) return false;
07420 
07421             return prefix ? name[5] == ':' && strequalrange(name + 6, prefix, prefix_length) : name[5] == 0;
07422         }
07423     };
07424 
07425     PUGI__FN const char_t* namespace_uri(xml_node node)
07426     {
07427         namespace_uri_predicate pred = node.name();
07428         
07429         xml_node p = node;
07430         
07431         while (p)
07432         {
07433             xml_attribute a = p.find_attribute(pred);
07434             
07435             if (a) return a.value();
07436             
07437             p = p.parent();
07438         }
07439         
07440         return PUGIXML_TEXT("");
07441     }
07442 
07443     PUGI__FN const char_t* namespace_uri(xml_attribute attr, xml_node parent)
07444     {
07445         namespace_uri_predicate pred = attr.name();
07446         
07447         // Default namespace does not apply to attributes
07448         if (!pred.prefix) return PUGIXML_TEXT("");
07449         
07450         xml_node p = parent;
07451         
07452         while (p)
07453         {
07454             xml_attribute a = p.find_attribute(pred);
07455             
07456             if (a) return a.value();
07457             
07458             p = p.parent();
07459         }
07460         
07461         return PUGIXML_TEXT("");
07462     }
07463 
07464     PUGI__FN const char_t* namespace_uri(const xpath_node& node)
07465     {
07466         return node.attribute() ? namespace_uri(node.attribute(), node.parent()) : namespace_uri(node.node());
07467     }
07468 
07469     PUGI__FN char_t* normalize_space(char_t* buffer)
07470     {
07471         char_t* write = buffer;
07472 
07473         for (char_t* it = buffer; *it; )
07474         {
07475             char_t ch = *it++;
07476 
07477             if (PUGI__IS_CHARTYPE(ch, ct_space))
07478             {
07479                 // replace whitespace sequence with single space
07480                 while (PUGI__IS_CHARTYPE(*it, ct_space)) it++;
07481 
07482                 // avoid leading spaces
07483                 if (write != buffer) *write++ = ' ';
07484             }
07485             else *write++ = ch;
07486         }
07487 
07488         // remove trailing space
07489         if (write != buffer && PUGI__IS_CHARTYPE(write[-1], ct_space)) write--;
07490 
07491         // zero-terminate
07492         *write = 0;
07493 
07494         return write;
07495     }
07496 
07497     PUGI__FN char_t* translate(char_t* buffer, const char_t* from, const char_t* to, size_t to_length)
07498     {
07499         char_t* write = buffer;
07500 
07501         while (*buffer)
07502         {
07503             PUGI__DMC_VOLATILE char_t ch = *buffer++;
07504 
07505             const char_t* pos = find_char(from, ch);
07506 
07507             if (!pos)
07508                 *write++ = ch; // do not process
07509             else if (static_cast<size_t>(pos - from) < to_length)
07510                 *write++ = to[pos - from]; // replace
07511         }
07512 
07513         // zero-terminate
07514         *write = 0;
07515 
07516         return write;
07517     }
07518 
07519     PUGI__FN unsigned char* translate_table_generate(xpath_allocator* alloc, const char_t* from, const char_t* to)
07520     {
07521         unsigned char table[128] = {0};
07522 
07523         while (*from)
07524         {
07525             unsigned int fc = static_cast<unsigned int>(*from);
07526             unsigned int tc = static_cast<unsigned int>(*to);
07527 
07528             if (fc >= 128 || tc >= 128)
07529                 return 0;
07530 
07531             // code=128 means "skip character"
07532             if (!table[fc])
07533                 table[fc] = static_cast<unsigned char>(tc ? tc : 128);
07534 
07535             from++;
07536             if (tc) to++;
07537         }
07538 
07539         for (int i = 0; i < 128; ++i)
07540             if (!table[i])
07541                 table[i] = static_cast<unsigned char>(i);
07542 
07543         void* result = alloc->allocate_nothrow(sizeof(table));
07544 
07545         if (result)
07546         {
07547             memcpy(result, table, sizeof(table));
07548         }
07549 
07550         return static_cast<unsigned char*>(result);
07551     }
07552 
07553     PUGI__FN char_t* translate_table(char_t* buffer, const unsigned char* table)
07554     {
07555         char_t* write = buffer;
07556 
07557         while (*buffer)
07558         {
07559             char_t ch = *buffer++;
07560             unsigned int index = static_cast<unsigned int>(ch);
07561 
07562             if (index < 128)
07563             {
07564                 unsigned char code = table[index];
07565 
07566                 // code=128 means "skip character" (table size is 128 so 128 can be a special value)
07567                 // this code skips these characters without extra branches
07568                 *write = static_cast<char_t>(code);
07569                 write += 1 - (code >> 7);
07570             }
07571             else
07572             {
07573                 *write++ = ch;
07574             }
07575         }
07576 
07577         // zero-terminate
07578         *write = 0;
07579 
07580         return write;
07581     }
07582

07584     {
07585         return !(starts_with(name, PUGIXML_TEXT("xmlns")) && (name[5] == 0 || name[5] == ':'));
07586     }
