07631     PUGI__FN unsigned int hash_string(const char_t* str)
07632     {
07633         // Jenkins one-at-a-time hash (http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jenkins_hash_function#one-at-a-time)
07634         unsigned int result = 0;
07635 
07636         while (*str)
07637         {
07638             result += static_cast<unsigned int>(*str++);
07639             result += result << 10;
07640             result ^= result >> 6;
07641         }
07642     
07643         result += result << 3;
07644         result ^= result >> 11;
07645         result += result << 15;
07646     
07647         return result;
07648     }
07649 
07650     template <typename T> PUGI__FN T* new_xpath_variable(const char_t* name)
07651     {
07652         size_t length = strlength(name);
07653         if (length == 0) return 0; // empty variable names are invalid
07654 
07655         // $$ we can't use offsetof(T, name) because T is non-POD, so we just allocate additional length characters
07656         void* memory = xml_memory::allocate(sizeof(T) + length * sizeof(char_t));
07657         if (!memory) return 0;
07658 
07659         T* result = new (memory) T();
07660 
07661         memcpy(result->name, name, (length + 1) * sizeof(char_t));
07662 
07663         return result;
07664     }
07665 
07666     PUGI__FN xpath_variable* new_xpath_variable(xpath_value_type type, const char_t* name)
07667     {
07668         switch (type)
07669         {
07670         case xpath_type_node_set:
07671             return new_xpath_variable<xpath_variable_node_set>(name);
07672 
07673         case xpath_type_number:
07674             return new_xpath_variable<xpath_variable_number>(name);
07675 
07676         case xpath_type_string:
07677             return new_xpath_variable<xpath_variable_string>(name);
07678 
07679         case xpath_type_boolean:
07680             return new_xpath_variable<xpath_variable_boolean>(name);
07681 
07682         default:
07683             return 0;
07684         }
07685     }
07686 
07687     template <typename T> PUGI__FN void delete_xpath_variable(T* var)
07688     {
07689         var->~T();
07690         xml_memory::deallocate(var);
07691     }
07692 
07693     PUGI__FN void delete_xpath_variable(xpath_value_type type, xpath_variable* var)
07694     {
07695         switch (type)
07696         {
07697         case xpath_type_node_set:
07698             delete_xpath_variable(static_cast<xpath_variable_node_set*>(var));
07699             break;
07700 
07701         case xpath_type_number:
07702             delete_xpath_variable(static_cast<xpath_variable_number*>(var));
07703             break;
07704 
07705         case xpath_type_string:
07706             delete_xpath_variable(static_cast<xpath_variable_string*>(var));
07707             break;
07708 
07709         case xpath_type_boolean:
07710             delete_xpath_variable(static_cast<xpath_variable_boolean*>(var));
07711             break;
07712 
07713         default:
07714             assert(!"Invalid variable type");
07715         }
07716     }
07717 
07718     PUGI__FN xpath_variable* get_variable_scratch(char_t (&buffer)[32], xpath_variable_set* set, const char_t* begin, const char_t* end)
07719     {
07720         size_t length = static_cast<size_t>(end - begin);
07721         char_t* scratch = buffer;
07722 
07723         if (length >= sizeof(buffer) / sizeof(buffer[0]))
07724         {
07725             // need to make dummy on-heap copy
07726             scratch = static_cast<char_t*>(xml_memory::allocate((length + 1) * sizeof(char_t)));
07727             if (!scratch) return 0;
07728         }
07729 
07730         // copy string to zero-terminated buffer and perform lookup
07731         memcpy(scratch, begin, length * sizeof(char_t));
07732         scratch[length] = 0;
07733 
07734         xpath_variable* result = set->get(scratch);
07735 
07736         // free dummy buffer
07737         if (scratch != buffer) xml_memory::deallocate(scratch);
07738 
07739         return result;
07740     }
07741 PUGI__NS_END
07742 
07743 // Internal node set class
07744 PUGI__NS_BEGIN
07745     PUGI__FN xpath_node_set::type_t xpath_get_order(const xpath_node* begin, const xpath_node* end)
07746     {
07747         if (end - begin < 2)
07748             return xpath_node_set::type_sorted;
07749 
07750         document_order_comparator cmp;
07751 
07752         bool first = cmp(begin[0], begin[1]);
07753 
07754         for (const xpath_node* it = begin + 1; it + 1 < end; ++it)
07755             if (cmp(it[0], it[1]) != first)
07756                 return xpath_node_set::type_unsorted;
07757 
07758         return first ? xpath_node_set::type_sorted : xpath_node_set::type_sorted_reverse;
07759     }
07760 
07761     PUGI__FN xpath_node_set::type_t xpath_sort(xpath_node* begin, xpath_node* end, xpath_node_set::type_t type, bool rev)
07762     {
07763         xpath_node_set::type_t order = rev ? xpath_node_set::type_sorted_reverse : xpath_node_set::type_sorted;
07764 
07765         if (type == xpath_node_set::type_unsorted)
07766         {
07767             xpath_node_set::type_t sorted = xpath_get_order(begin, end);
07768 
07769             if (sorted == xpath_node_set::type_unsorted)
07770             {
07771                 sort(begin, end, document_order_comparator());
07772 
07773                 type = xpath_node_set::type_sorted;
07774             }
07775             else
07776                 type = sorted;
07777         }
07778         
07779         if (type != order) reverse(begin, end);
07780             
07781         return order;
07782     }
07783 
07784     PUGI__FN xpath_node xpath_first(const xpath_node* begin, const xpath_node* end, xpath_node_set::type_t type)
07785     {
07786         if (begin == end) return xpath_node();
07787 
07788         switch (type)
07789         {
07790         case xpath_node_set::type_sorted:
07791             return *begin;
07792 
07793         case xpath_node_set::type_sorted_reverse:
07794             return *(end - 1);
07795 
07796         case xpath_node_set::type_unsorted:
07797             return *min_element(begin, end, document_order_comparator());
07798 
07799         default:
07800             assert(!"Invalid node set type");
07801             return xpath_node();
07802         }
07803     }
07804 
07805     class xpath_node_set_raw
07806     {
07807         xpath_node_set::type_t _type;
07808 
07809         xpath_node* _begin;
07810         xpath_node* _end;
07811         xpath_node* _eos;
07812 
07813     public:
07814         xpath_node_set_raw(): _type(xpath_node_set::type_unsorted), _begin(0), _end(0), _eos(0)
07815         {
07816         }
07817 
07818         xpath_node* begin() const
07819         {
07820             return _begin;
07821         }
07822 
07823         xpath_node* end() const
07824         {
07825             return _end;
07826         }
07827 
07828         bool empty() const
07829         {
07830             return _begin == _end;
07831         }
07832 
07833         size_t size() const
07834         {
07835             return static_cast<size_t>(_end - _begin);
07836         }
07837 
07838         xpath_node first() const
07839         {
07840             return xpath_first(_begin, _end, _type);
07841         }
07842 
07843         void push_back_grow(const xpath_node& node, xpath_allocator* alloc);
07844 
07845         void push_back(const xpath_node& node, xpath_allocator* alloc)
07846         {
07847             if (_end != _eos)
07848                 *_end++ = node;
07849             else
07850                 push_back_grow(node, alloc);
07851         }
07852 
07853         void append(const xpath_node* begin_, const xpath_node* end_, xpath_allocator* alloc)
07854         {
07855             if (begin_ == end_) return;
07856 
07857             size_t size_ = static_cast<size_t>(_end - _begin);
07858             size_t capacity = static_cast<size_t>(_eos - _begin);
07859             size_t count = static_cast<size_t>(end_ - begin_);
07860 
07861             if (size_ + count > capacity)
07862             {
07863                 // reallocate the old array or allocate a new one
07864                 xpath_node* data = static_cast<xpath_node*>(alloc->reallocate(_begin, capacity * sizeof(xpath_node), (size_ + count) * sizeof(xpath_node)));
07865                 assert(data);
07866 
07867                 // finalize
07868                 _begin = data;
07869                 _end = data + size_;
07870                 _eos = data + size_ + count;
07871             }
07872 
07873             memcpy(_end, begin_, count * sizeof(xpath_node));
07874             _end += count;
07875         }
07876 
07877         void sort_do()
07878         {
07879             _type = xpath_sort(_begin, _end, _type, false);
07880         }
07881 
07882         void truncate(xpath_node* pos)
07883         {
07884             assert(_begin <= pos && pos <= _end);
07885 
07886             _end = pos;
07887         }
07888 
07889         void remove_duplicates()
07890         {
07891             if (_type == xpath_node_set::type_unsorted)
07892                 sort(_begin, _end, duplicate_comparator());
07893         
07894             _end = unique(_begin, _end);
07895         }
07896 
07897         xpath_node_set::type_t type() const
07898         {
07899             return _type;
07900         }
07901 
07902         void set_type(xpath_node_set::type_t value)
07903         {
07904             _type = value;
07905         }
07906     };
07907 
07908     PUGI__FN_NO_INLINE void xpath_node_set_raw::push_back_grow(const xpath_node& node, xpath_allocator* alloc)
07909     {
07910         size_t capacity = static_cast<size_t>(_eos - _begin);
07911 
07912         // get new capacity (1.5x rule)
07913         size_t new_capacity = capacity + capacity / 2 + 1;
07914 
07915         // reallocate the old array or allocate a new one
07916         xpath_node* data = static_cast<xpath_node*>(alloc->reallocate(_begin, capacity * sizeof(xpath_node), new_capacity * sizeof(xpath_node)));
07917         assert(data);
07918 
07919         // finalize
07920         _begin = data;
07921         _end = data + capacity;
07922         _eos = data + new_capacity;
07923 
07924         // push
07925         *_end++ = node;
07926     }
07927 PUGI__NS_END
07928 
07929 PUGI__NS_BEGIN

07931     {
07932         xpath_node n;
07933         size_t position, size;
07934 
07935         xpath_context(const xpath_node& n_, size_t position_, size_t size_): n(n_), position(position_), size(size_)
07936         {
07937         }
07938     };

07940     enum lexeme_t
07941     {
07942         lex_none = 0,
07943         lex_equal,
07944         lex_not_equal,
07945         lex_less,
07946         lex_greater,
07947         lex_less_or_equal,
07948         lex_greater_or_equal,
07949         lex_plus,
07950         lex_minus,
07951         lex_multiply,
07952         lex_union,
07953         lex_var_ref,
07954         lex_open_brace,
07955         lex_close_brace,
07956         lex_quoted_string,
07957         lex_number,
07958         lex_slash,
07959         lex_double_slash,
07960         lex_open_square_brace,
07961         lex_close_square_brace,
07962         lex_string,
07963         lex_comma,
07964         lex_axis_attribute,
07965         lex_dot,
07966         lex_double_dot,
07967         lex_double_colon,
07968         lex_eof

07971     struct xpath_lexer_string
07972     {
07973         const char_t* begin;
07974         const char_t* end;
07975 
07976         xpath_lexer_string(): begin(0), end(0)
07977         {
07978         }
07979 
07980         bool operator==(const char_t* other) const
07981         {
07982             size_t length = static_cast<size_t>(end - begin);
07983 
07984             return strequalrange(other, begin, length);
07985         }

07987 
07988     class xpath_lexer
07989     {
07990         const char_t* _cur;
07991         const char_t* _cur_lexeme_pos;
07992         xpath_lexer_string _cur_lexeme_contents;
07993 
07994         lexeme_t _cur_lexeme;
07995 
07996     public:
07997         explicit xpath_lexer(const char_t* query): _cur(query)
07998         {
07999             next();
08000         }
08001         
08002         const char_t* state() const
08003         {
08004             return _cur;
08005         }
08006         
08007         void next()
08008         {
08009             const char_t* cur = _cur;
08010 
08011             while (PUGI__IS_CHARTYPE(*cur, ct_space)) ++cur;
08012 
08013             // save lexeme position for error reporting
08014             _cur_lexeme_pos = cur;
08015 
08016             switch (*cur)
08017             {
08018             case 0:
08019                 _cur_lexeme = lex_eof;
08020                 break;
08021             
08022             case '>':
08023                 if (*(cur+1) == '=')
08024                 {
08025                     cur += 2;
08026                     _cur_lexeme = lex_greater_or_equal;
08027                 }
08028                 else
08029                 {
08030                     cur += 1;
08031                     _cur_lexeme = lex_greater;
08032                 }
08033                 break;
08034 
08035             case '<':
08036                 if (*(cur+1) == '=')
08037                 {
08038                     cur += 2;
08039                     _cur_lexeme = lex_less_or_equal;
08040                 }
08041                 else
08042                 {
08043                     cur += 1;
08044                     _cur_lexeme = lex_less;
08045                 }
08046                 break;
08047 
08048             case '!':
08049                 if (*(cur+1) == '=')
08050                 {
08051                     cur += 2;
08052                     _cur_lexeme = lex_not_equal;
08053                 }
08054                 else
08055                 {
08056                     _cur_lexeme = lex_none;
08057                 }
08058                 break;
08059 
08060             case '=':
08061                 cur += 1;
08062                 _cur_lexeme = lex_equal;
08063 
08064                 break;
08065             
08066             case '+':
08067                 cur += 1;
08068                 _cur_lexeme = lex_plus;
08069 
08070                 break;
08071 
08072             case '-':
08073                 cur += 1;
08074                 _cur_lexeme = lex_minus;
08075 
08076                 break;
08077 
08078             case '*':
08079                 cur += 1;
08080                 _cur_lexeme = lex_multiply;
08081 
08082                 break;
08083 
08084             case '|':
08085                 cur += 1;
08086                 _cur_lexeme = lex_union;
08087 
08088                 break;
08089             
08090             case '$':
08091                 cur += 1;
08092 
08093                 if (PUGI__IS_CHARTYPEX(*cur, ctx_start_symbol))
08094                 {
08095                     _cur_lexeme_contents.begin = cur;
08096 
08097                     while (PUGI__IS_CHARTYPEX(*cur, ctx_symbol)) cur++;
08098 
08099                     if (cur[0] == ':' && PUGI__IS_CHARTYPEX(cur[1], ctx_symbol)) // qname
08100                     {
08101                         cur++; // :
08102 
08103                         while (PUGI__IS_CHARTYPEX(*cur, ctx_symbol)) cur++;
08104                     }
08105 
08106                     _cur_lexeme_contents.end = cur;
08107                 
08108                     _cur_lexeme = lex_var_ref;
08109                 }
08110                 else
08111                 {
08112                     _cur_lexeme = lex_none;
08113                 }
08114 
08115                 break;
08116 
08117             case '(':
08118                 cur += 1;
08119                 _cur_lexeme = lex_open_brace;
08120 
08121                 break;
08122 
08123             case ')':
08124                 cur += 1;
08125                 _cur_lexeme = lex_close_brace;
08126 
08127                 break;
08128             
08129             case '[':
08130                 cur += 1;
08131                 _cur_lexeme = lex_open_square_brace;
08132 
08133                 break;
08134 
08135             case ']':
08136                 cur += 1;
08137                 _cur_lexeme = lex_close_square_brace;
08138 
08139                 break;
08140 
08141             case ',':
08142                 cur += 1;
08143                 _cur_lexeme = lex_comma;
08144 
08145                 break;
08146 
08147             case '/':
08148                 if (*(cur+1) == '/')
08149                 {
08150                     cur += 2;
08151                     _cur_lexeme = lex_double_slash;
08152                 }
08153                 else
08154                 {
08155                     cur += 1;
08156                     _cur_lexeme = lex_slash;
08157                 }
08158                 break;
08159         
08160             case '.':
08161                 if (*(cur+1) == '.')
08162                 {
08163                     cur += 2;
08164                     _cur_lexeme = lex_double_dot;
08165                 }
08166                 else if (PUGI__IS_CHARTYPEX(*(cur+1), ctx_digit))
08167                 {
08168                     _cur_lexeme_contents.begin = cur; // .
08169 
08170                     ++cur;
08171 
08172                     while (PUGI__IS_CHARTYPEX(*cur, ctx_digit)) cur++;
08173 
08174                     _cur_lexeme_contents.end = cur;
08175                     
08176                     _cur_lexeme = lex_number;
08177                 }
08178                 else
08179                 {
08180                     cur += 1;
08181                     _cur_lexeme = lex_dot;
08182                 }
08183                 break;
08184 
08185             case '@':
08186                 cur += 1;
08187                 _cur_lexeme = lex_axis_attribute;
08188 
08189                 break;
08190 
08191             case '"':
08192             case '\'':
08193             {
08194                 char_t terminator = *cur;
08195 
08196                 ++cur;
08197 
08198                 _cur_lexeme_contents.begin = cur;
08199                 while (*cur && *cur != terminator) cur++;
08200                 _cur_lexeme_contents.end = cur;
08201                 
08202                 if (!*cur)
08203                     _cur_lexeme = lex_none;
08204                 else
08205                 {
08206                     cur += 1;
08207                     _cur_lexeme = lex_quoted_string;
08208                 }
08209 
08210                 break;
08211             }
08212 
08213             case ':':
08214                 if (*(cur+1) == ':')
08215                 {
08216                     cur += 2;
08217                     _cur_lexeme = lex_double_colon;
08218                 }
08219                 else
08220                 {
08221                     _cur_lexeme = lex_none;
08222                 }
08223                 break;
08224 
08225             default:
08226                 if (PUGI__IS_CHARTYPEX(*cur, ctx_digit))
08227                 {
08228                     _cur_lexeme_contents.begin = cur;
08229 
08230                     while (PUGI__IS_CHARTYPEX(*cur, ctx_digit)) cur++;
08231                 
08232                     if (*cur == '.')
08233                     {
08234                         cur++;
08235 
08236                         while (PUGI__IS_CHARTYPEX(*cur, ctx_digit)) cur++;
08237                     }
08238 
08239                     _cur_lexeme_contents.end = cur;
08240 
08241                     _cur_lexeme = lex_number;
08242                 }
08243                 else if (PUGI__IS_CHARTYPEX(*cur, ctx_start_symbol))
08244                 {
08245                     _cur_lexeme_contents.begin = cur;
08246 
08247                     while (PUGI__IS_CHARTYPEX(*cur, ctx_symbol)) cur++;
08248 
08249                     if (cur[0] == ':')
08250                     {
08251                         if (cur[1] == '*') // namespace test ncname:*
08252                         {
08253                             cur += 2; // :*
08254                         }
08255                         else if (PUGI__IS_CHARTYPEX(cur[1], ctx_symbol)) // namespace test qname
08256                         {
08257                             cur++; // :
08258 
08259                             while (PUGI__IS_CHARTYPEX(*cur, ctx_symbol)) cur++;
08260                         }
08261                     }
08262 
08263                     _cur_lexeme_contents.end = cur;
08264                 
08265                     _cur_lexeme = lex_string;
08266                 }
08267                 else
08268                 {
08269                     _cur_lexeme = lex_none;
08270                 }
08271             }
08272 
08273             _cur = cur;
08274         }
08275 
08276         lexeme_t current() const
08277         {
08278             return _cur_lexeme;
08279         }
08280 
08281         const char_t* current_pos() const
08282         {
08283             return _cur_lexeme_pos;
08284         }
08285 
08286         const xpath_lexer_string& contents() const
08287         {
08288             assert(_cur_lexeme == lex_var_ref || _cur_lexeme == lex_number || _cur_lexeme == lex_string || _cur_lexeme == lex_quoted_string);
08289 
08290             return _cur_lexeme_contents;
08291         }
08292     };
08293

08411     class xpath_ast_node
08412     {
08413     private:
08414         // node type
08415         char _type;
08416         char _rettype;
08417 
08418         // for ast_step
08419         char _axis;
08420 
08421         // for ast_step/ast_predicate/ast_filter
08422         char _test;
08423 
08424         // tree node structure
08425         xpath_ast_node* _left;
08426         xpath_ast_node* _right;
08427         xpath_ast_node* _next;
08428 
08429         union
08430         {
08431             // value for ast_string_constant
08432             const char_t* string;
08433             // value for ast_number_constant
08434             double number;
08435             // variable for ast_variable
08436             xpath_variable* variable;
08437             // node test for ast_step (node name/namespace/node type/pi target)
08438             const char_t* nodetest;
08439             // table for ast_opt_translate_table
08440             const unsigned char* table;
08441         } _data;
08442 
08443         xpath_ast_node(const xpath_ast_node&);
08444         xpath_ast_node& operator=(const xpath_ast_node&);
08445 
08446         template <class Comp> static bool compare_eq(xpath_ast_node* lhs, xpath_ast_node* rhs, const xpath_context& c, const xpath_stack& stack, const Comp& comp)
08447         {
08448             xpath_value_type lt = lhs->rettype(), rt = rhs->rettype();
08449 
08450             if (lt != xpath_type_node_set && rt != xpath_type_node_set)
08451             {
08452                 if (lt == xpath_type_boolean || rt == xpath_type_boolean)
08453                     return comp(lhs->eval_boolean(c, stack), rhs->eval_boolean(c, stack));
08454                 else if (lt == xpath_type_number || rt == xpath_type_number)
08455                     return comp(lhs->eval_number(c, stack), rhs->eval_number(c, stack));
08456                 else if (lt == xpath_type_string || rt == xpath_type_string)
08457                 {
08458                     xpath_allocator_capture cr(stack.result);
08459 
08460                     xpath_string ls = lhs->eval_string(c, stack);
08461                     xpath_string rs = rhs->eval_string(c, stack);
08462 
08463                     return comp(ls, rs);
08464                 }
08465             }
08466             else if (lt == xpath_type_node_set && rt == xpath_type_node_set)
08467             {
08468                 xpath_allocator_capture cr(stack.result);
08469 
08470                 xpath_node_set_raw ls = lhs->eval_node_set(c, stack, nodeset_eval_all);
08471                 xpath_node_set_raw rs = rhs->eval_node_set(c, stack, nodeset_eval_all);
08472 
08473                 for (const xpath_node* li = ls.begin(); li != ls.end(); ++li)
08474                     for (const xpath_node* ri = rs.begin(); ri != rs.end(); ++ri)
08475                     {
08476                         xpath_allocator_capture cri(stack.result);
08477 
08478                         if (comp(string_value(*li, stack.result), string_value(*ri, stack.result)))
08479                             return true;
08480                     }
08481 
08482                 return false;
08483             }
08484             else
08485             {
08486                 if (lt == xpath_type_node_set)
08487                 {
08488                     swap(lhs, rhs);
08489                     swap(lt, rt);
08490                 }
08491 
08492                 if (lt == xpath_type_boolean)
08493                     return comp(lhs->eval_boolean(c, stack), rhs->eval_boolean(c, stack));
08494                 else if (lt == xpath_type_number)
08495                 {
08496                     xpath_allocator_capture cr(stack.result);
08497 
08498                     double l = lhs->eval_number(c, stack);
08499                     xpath_node_set_raw rs = rhs->eval_node_set(c, stack, nodeset_eval_all);
08500 
08501                     for (const xpath_node* ri = rs.begin(); ri != rs.end(); ++ri)
08502                     {
08503                         xpath_allocator_capture cri(stack.result);
08504 
08505                         if (comp(l, convert_string_to_number(string_value(*ri, stack.result).c_str())))
08506                             return true;
08507                     }
08508 
08509                     return false;
08510                 }
08511                 else if (lt == xpath_type_string)
08512                 {
08513                     xpath_allocator_capture cr(stack.result);
08514 
08515                     xpath_string l = lhs->eval_string(c, stack);
08516                     xpath_node_set_raw rs = rhs->eval_node_set(c, stack, nodeset_eval_all);
08517 
08518                     for (const xpath_node* ri = rs.begin(); ri != rs.end(); ++ri)
08519                     {
08520                         xpath_allocator_capture cri(stack.result);
08521 
08522                         if (comp(l, string_value(*ri, stack.result)))
08523                             return true;
08524                     }
08525 
08526                     return false;
08527                 }
08528             }
08529 
08530             assert(!"Wrong types");
08531             return false;
08532         }
08533 
08534         static bool eval_once(xpath_node_set::type_t type, nodeset_eval_t eval)
08535         {
08536             return type == xpath_node_set::type_sorted ? eval != nodeset_eval_all : eval == nodeset_eval_any;
08537         }
08538 
08539         template <class Comp> static bool compare_rel(xpath_ast_node* lhs, xpath_ast_node* rhs, const xpath_context& c, const xpath_stack& stack, const Comp& comp)
08540         {
08541             xpath_value_type lt = lhs->rettype(), rt = rhs->rettype();
08542 
08543             if (lt != xpath_type_node_set && rt != xpath_type_node_set)
08544                 return comp(lhs->eval_number(c, stack), rhs->eval_number(c, stack));
08545             else if (lt == xpath_type_node_set && rt == xpath_type_node_set)
08546             {
08547                 xpath_allocator_capture cr(stack.result);
08548 
08549                 xpath_node_set_raw ls = lhs->eval_node_set(c, stack, nodeset_eval_all);
08550                 xpath_node_set_raw rs = rhs->eval_node_set(c, stack, nodeset_eval_all);
08551 
08552                 for (const xpath_node* li = ls.begin(); li != ls.end(); ++li)
08553                 {
08554                     xpath_allocator_capture cri(stack.result);
08555 
08556                     double l = convert_string_to_number(string_value(*li, stack.result).c_str());
08557 
08558                     for (const xpath_node* ri = rs.begin(); ri != rs.end(); ++ri)
08559                     {
08560                         xpath_allocator_capture crii(stack.result);
08561 
08562                         if (comp(l, convert_string_to_number(string_value(*ri, stack.result).c_str())))
08563                             return true;
08564                     }
08565                 }
08566 
08567                 return false;
08568             }
08569             else if (lt != xpath_type_node_set && rt == xpath_type_node_set)
08570             {
08571                 xpath_allocator_capture cr(stack.result);
08572 
08573                 double l = lhs->eval_number(c, stack);
08574                 xpath_node_set_raw rs = rhs->eval_node_set(c, stack, nodeset_eval_all);
08575 
08576                 for (const xpath_node* ri = rs.begin(); ri != rs.end(); ++ri)
08577                 {
08578                     xpath_allocator_capture cri(stack.result);
08579 
08580                     if (comp(l, convert_string_to_number(string_value(*ri, stack.result).c_str())))
08581                         return true;
08582                 }
08583 
08584                 return false;
08585             }
08586             else if (lt == xpath_type_node_set && rt != xpath_type_node_set)
08587             {
08588                 xpath_allocator_capture cr(stack.result);
08589 
08590                 xpath_node_set_raw ls = lhs->eval_node_set(c, stack, nodeset_eval_all);
08591                 double r = rhs->eval_number(c, stack);
08592 
08593                 for (const xpath_node* li = ls.begin(); li != ls.end(); ++li)
08594                 {
08595                     xpath_allocator_capture cri(stack.result);
08596 
08597                     if (comp(convert_string_to_number(string_value(*li, stack.result).c_str()), r))
08598                         return true;
08599                 }
08600 
08601                 return false;
08602             }
08603             else
08604             {
08605                 assert(!"Wrong types");
08606                 return false;
08607             }
08608         }
08609 
08610         static void apply_predicate_boolean(xpath_node_set_raw& ns, size_t first, xpath_ast_node* expr, const xpath_stack& stack, bool once)
08611         {
08612             assert(ns.size() >= first);
08613             assert(expr->rettype() != xpath_type_number);
08614 
08615             size_t i = 1;
08616             size_t size = ns.size() - first;
08617 
08618             xpath_node* last = ns.begin() + first;
08619 
08620             // remove_if... or well, sort of
08621             for (xpath_node* it = last; it != ns.end(); ++it, ++i)
08622             {
08623                 xpath_context c(*it, i, size);
08624 
08625                 if (expr->eval_boolean(c, stack))
08626                 {
08627                     *last++ = *it;
08628 
08629                     if (once) break;
08630                 }
08631             }
08632 
08633             ns.truncate(last);
08634         }
08635 
08636         static void apply_predicate_number(xpath_node_set_raw& ns, size_t first, xpath_ast_node* expr, const xpath_stack& stack, bool once)
08637         {
08638             assert(ns.size() >= first);
08639             assert(expr->rettype() == xpath_type_number);
08640 
08641             size_t i = 1;
08642             size_t size = ns.size() - first;
08643 
08644             xpath_node* last = ns.begin() + first;
08645 
08646             // remove_if... or well, sort of
08647             for (xpath_node* it = last; it != ns.end(); ++it, ++i)
08648             {
08649                 xpath_context c(*it, i, size);
08650 
08651                 if (expr->eval_number(c, stack) == i)
08652                 {
08653                     *last++ = *it;
08654 
08655                     if (once) break;
08656                 }
08657             }
08658 
08659             ns.truncate(last);
08660         }
08661 
08662         static void apply_predicate_number_const(xpath_node_set_raw& ns, size_t first, xpath_ast_node* expr, const xpath_stack& stack)
08663         {
08664             assert(ns.size() >= first);
08665             assert(expr->rettype() == xpath_type_number);
08666 
08667             size_t size = ns.size() - first;
08668 
08669             xpath_node* last = ns.begin() + first;
08670 
08671             xpath_context c(xpath_node(), 1, size);
08672 
08673             double er = expr->eval_number(c, stack);
08674 
08675             if (er >= 1.0 && er <= size)
08676             {
08677                 size_t eri = static_cast<size_t>(er);
08678 
08679                 if (er == eri)
08680                 {
08681                     xpath_node r = last[eri - 1];
08682 
08683                     *last++ = r;
08684                 }
08685             }
08686 
08687             ns.truncate(last);
08688         }
08689 
08690         void apply_predicate(xpath_node_set_raw& ns, size_t first, const xpath_stack& stack, bool once)
08691         {
08692             if (ns.size() == first) return;
08693 
08694             assert(_type == ast_filter || _type == ast_predicate);
08695 
08696             if (_test == predicate_constant || _test == predicate_constant_one)
08697                 apply_predicate_number_const(ns, first, _right, stack);
08698             else if (_right->rettype() == xpath_type_number)
08699                 apply_predicate_number(ns, first, _right, stack, once);
08700             else
08701                 apply_predicate_boolean(ns, first, _right, stack, once);
08702         }
08703 
08704         void apply_predicates(xpath_node_set_raw& ns, size_t first, const xpath_stack& stack, nodeset_eval_t eval)
08705         {
08706             if (ns.size() == first) return;
08707 
08708             bool last_once = eval_once(ns.type(), eval);
08709 
08710             for (xpath_ast_node* pred = _right; pred; pred = pred->_next)
08711                 pred->apply_predicate(ns, first, stack, !pred->_next && last_once);
08712         }
08713 
08714         bool step_push(xpath_node_set_raw& ns, xml_attribute_struct* a, xml_node_struct* parent, xpath_allocator* alloc)
08715         {
08716             assert(a);
08717 
08718             const char_t* name = a->name ? a->name : PUGIXML_TEXT("");
08719 
08720             switch (_test)
08721             {
08722             case nodetest_name:
08723                 if (strequal(name, _data.nodetest) && is_xpath_attribute(name))
08724                 {
08725                     ns.push_back(xpath_node(xml_attribute(a), xml_node(parent)), alloc);
08726                     return true;
08727                 }
08728                 break;
08729                 
08730             case nodetest_type_node:
08731             case nodetest_all:
08732                 if (is_xpath_attribute(name))
08733                 {
08734                     ns.push_back(xpath_node(xml_attribute(a), xml_node(parent)), alloc);
08735                     return true;
08736                 }
08737                 break;
08738                 
08739             case nodetest_all_in_namespace:
08740                 if (starts_with(name, _data.nodetest) && is_xpath_attribute(name))
08741                 {
08742                     ns.push_back(xpath_node(xml_attribute(a), xml_node(parent)), alloc);
08743                     return true;
08744                 }
08745                 break;
08746             
08747             default:
08748                 ;
08749             }
08750 
08751             return false;
08752         }
08753         
08754         bool step_push(xpath_node_set_raw& ns, xml_node_struct* n, xpath_allocator* alloc)
08755         {
08756             assert(n);
08757 
08758             xml_node_type type = PUGI__NODETYPE(n);
08759 
08760             switch (_test)
08761             {
08762             case nodetest_name:
08763                 if (type == node_element && n->name && strequal(n->name, _data.nodetest))
08764                 {
08765                     ns.push_back(xml_node(n), alloc);
08766                     return true;
08767                 }
08768                 break;
08769                 
08770             case nodetest_type_node:
08771                 ns.push_back(xml_node(n), alloc);
08772                 return true;
08773                 
08774             case nodetest_type_comment:
08775                 if (type == node_comment)
08776                 {
08777                     ns.push_back(xml_node(n), alloc);
08778                     return true;
08779                 }
08780                 break;
08781                 
08782             case nodetest_type_text:
08783                 if (type == node_pcdata || type == node_cdata)
08784                 {
08785                     ns.push_back(xml_node(n), alloc);
08786                     return true;
08787                 }
08788                 break;
08789                 
08790             case nodetest_type_pi:
08791                 if (type == node_pi)
08792                 {
08793                     ns.push_back(xml_node(n), alloc);
08794                     return true;
08795                 }
08796                 break;
08797                                     
08798             case nodetest_pi:
08799                 if (type == node_pi && n->name && strequal(n->name, _data.nodetest))
08800                 {
08801                     ns.push_back(xml_node(n), alloc);
08802                     return true;
08803                 }
08804                 break;
08805                 
08806             case nodetest_all:
08807                 if (type == node_element)
08808                 {
08809                     ns.push_back(xml_node(n), alloc);
08810                     return true;
08811                 }
08812                 break;
08813                 
08814             case nodetest_all_in_namespace:
08815                 if (type == node_element && n->name && starts_with(n->name, _data.nodetest))
08816                 {
08817                     ns.push_back(xml_node(n), alloc);
08818                     return true;
08819                 }
08820                 break;
08821 
08822             default:
08823                 assert(!"Unknown axis");
08824             }
08825 
08826             return false;
08827         }
08828 
08829         template <class T> void step_fill(xpath_node_set_raw& ns, xml_node_struct* n, xpath_allocator* alloc, bool once, T)
08830         {
08831             const axis_t axis = T::axis;
08832 
08833             switch (axis)
08834             {
08835             case axis_attribute:
08836             {
08837                 for (xml_attribute_struct* a = n->first_attribute; a; a = a->next_attribute)
08838                     if (step_push(ns, a, n, alloc) & once)
08839                         return;
08840                 
08841                 break;
08842             }
08843             
08844             case axis_child:
08845             {
08846                 for (xml_node_struct* c = n->first_child; c; c = c->next_sibling)
08847                     if (step_push(ns, c, alloc) & once)
08848                         return;
08849                     
08850                 break;
08851             }
08852             
08853             case axis_descendant:
08854             case axis_descendant_or_self:
08855             {
08856                 if (axis == axis_descendant_or_self)
08857                     if (step_push(ns, n, alloc) & once)
08858                         return;
08859                     
08860                 xml_node_struct* cur = n->first_child;
08861                 
08862                 while (cur)
08863                 {
08864                     if (step_push(ns, cur, alloc) & once)
08865                         return;
08866                     
08867                     if (cur->first_child)
08868                         cur = cur->first_child;
08869                     else
08870                     {
08871                         while (!cur->next_sibling)
08872                         {
08873                             cur = cur->parent;
08874 
08875                             if (cur == n) return;
08876                         }
08877                     
08878                         cur = cur->next_sibling;
08879                     }
08880                 }
08881                 
08882                 break;
08883             }
08884             
08885             case axis_following_sibling:
08886             {
08887                 for (xml_node_struct* c = n->next_sibling; c; c = c->next_sibling)
08888                     if (step_push(ns, c, alloc) & once)
08889                         return;
08890                 
08891                 break;
08892             }
08893             
08894             case axis_preceding_sibling:
08895             {
08896                 for (xml_node_struct* c = n->prev_sibling_c; c->next_sibling; c = c->prev_sibling_c)
08897                     if (step_push(ns, c, alloc) & once)
08898                         return;
08899                 
08900                 break;
08901             }
08902             
08903             case axis_following:
08904             {
08905                 xml_node_struct* cur = n;
08906 
08907                 // exit from this node so that we don't include descendants
08908                 while (!cur->next_sibling)
08909                 {
08910                     cur = cur->parent;
08911 
08912                     if (!cur) return;
08913                 }
08914 
08915                 cur = cur->next_sibling;
08916 
08917                 while (cur)
08918                 {
08919                     if (step_push(ns, cur, alloc) & once)
08920                         return;
08921 
08922                     if (cur->first_child)
08923                         cur = cur->first_child;
08924                     else
08925                     {
08926                         while (!cur->next_sibling)
08927                         {
08928                             cur = cur->parent;
08929 
08930                             if (!cur) return;
08931                         }
08932 
08933                         cur = cur->next_sibling;
08934                     }
08935                 }
08936 
08937                 break;
08938             }
08939 
08940             case axis_preceding:
08941             {
08942                 xml_node_struct* cur = n;
08943 
08944                 // exit from this node so that we don't include descendants
08945                 while (!cur->prev_sibling_c->next_sibling)
08946                 {
08947                     cur = cur->parent;
08948 
08949                     if (!cur) return;
08950                 }
08951 
08952                 cur = cur->prev_sibling_c;
08953 
08954                 while (cur)
08955                 {
08956                     if (cur->first_child)
08957                         cur = cur->first_child->prev_sibling_c;
08958                     else
08959                     {
08960                         // leaf node, can't be ancestor
08961                         if (step_push(ns, cur, alloc) & once)
08962                             return;
08963 
08964                         while (!cur->prev_sibling_c->next_sibling)
08965                         {
08966                             cur = cur->parent;
08967 
08968                             if (!cur) return;
08969 
08970                             if (!node_is_ancestor(cur, n))
08971                                 if (step_push(ns, cur, alloc) & once)
08972                                     return;
08973                         }
08974 
08975                         cur = cur->prev_sibling_c;
08976                     }
08977                 }
08978 
08979                 break;
08980             }
08981             
08982             case axis_ancestor:
08983             case axis_ancestor_or_self:
08984             {
08985                 if (axis == axis_ancestor_or_self)
08986                     if (step_push(ns, n, alloc) & once)
08987                         return;
08988 
08989                 xml_node_struct* cur = n->parent;
08990                 
08991                 while (cur)
08992                 {
08993                     if (step_push(ns, cur, alloc) & once)
08994                         return;
08995                     
08996                     cur = cur->parent;
08997                 }
08998                 
08999                 break;
09000             }
09001 
09002             case axis_self:
09003             {
09004                 step_push(ns, n, alloc);
09005 
09006                 break;
09007             }
09008 
09009             case axis_parent:
09010             {
09011                 if (n->parent)
09012                     step_push(ns, n->parent, alloc);
09013 
09014                 break;
09015             }
09016                 
09017             default:
09018                 assert(!"Unimplemented axis");
09019             }
09020         }
09021         
09022         template <class T> void step_fill(xpath_node_set_raw& ns, xml_attribute_struct* a, xml_node_struct* p, xpath_allocator* alloc, bool once, T v)
09023         {
09024             const axis_t axis = T::axis;
09025 
09026             switch (axis)
09027             {
09028             case axis_ancestor:
09029             case axis_ancestor_or_self:
09030             {
09031                 if (axis == axis_ancestor_or_self && _test == nodetest_type_node) // reject attributes based on principal node type test
09032                     if (step_push(ns, a, p, alloc) & once)
09033                         return;
09034 
09035                 xml_node_struct* cur = p;
09036                 
09037                 while (cur)
09038                 {
09039                     if (step_push(ns, cur, alloc) & once)
09040                         return;
09041                     
09042                     cur = cur->parent;
09043                 }
09044                 
09045                 break;
09046             }
09047 
09048             case axis_descendant_or_self:
09049             case axis_self:
09050             {
09051                 if (_test == nodetest_type_node) // reject attributes based on principal node type test
09052                     step_push(ns, a, p, alloc);
09053 
09054                 break;
09055             }
09056 
09057             case axis_following:
09058             {
09059                 xml_node_struct* cur = p;
09060                 
09061                 while (cur)
09062                 {
09063                     if (cur->first_child)
09064                         cur = cur->first_child;
09065                     else
09066                     {
09067                         while (!cur->next_sibling)
09068                         {
09069                             cur = cur->parent;
09070 
09071                             if (!cur) return;
09072                         }
09073 
09074                         cur = cur->next_sibling;
09075                     }
09076 
09077                     if (step_push(ns, cur, alloc) & once)
09078                         return;
09079                 }
09080 
09081                 break;
09082             }
09083 
09084             case axis_parent:
09085             {
09086                 step_push(ns, p, alloc);
09087 
09088                 break;
09089             }
09090 
09091             case axis_preceding:
09092             {
09093                 // preceding:: axis does not include attribute nodes and attribute ancestors (they are the same as parent's ancestors), so we can reuse node preceding
09094                 step_fill(ns, p, alloc, once, v);
09095                 break;
09096             }
09097             
09098             default:
09099                 assert(!"Unimplemented axis");
09100             }
09101         }
09102 
09103         template <class T> void step_fill(xpath_node_set_raw& ns, const xpath_node& xn, xpath_allocator* alloc, bool once, T v)
09104         {
09105             const axis_t axis = T::axis;
09106             const bool axis_has_attributes = (axis == axis_ancestor || axis == axis_ancestor_or_self || axis == axis_descendant_or_self || axis == axis_following || axis == axis_parent || axis == axis_preceding || axis == axis_self);
09107 
09108             if (xn.node())
09109                 step_fill(ns, xn.node().internal_object(), alloc, once, v);
09110             else if (axis_has_attributes && xn.attribute() && xn.parent())
09111                 step_fill(ns, xn.attribute().internal_object(), xn.parent().internal_object(), alloc, once, v);
09112         }
09113 
09114         template <class T> xpath_node_set_raw step_do(const xpath_context& c, const xpath_stack& stack, nodeset_eval_t eval, T v)
09115         {
09116             const axis_t axis = T::axis;
09117             const bool axis_reverse = (axis == axis_ancestor || axis == axis_ancestor_or_self || axis == axis_preceding || axis == axis_preceding_sibling);
09118             const xpath_node_set::type_t axis_type = axis_reverse ? xpath_node_set::type_sorted_reverse : xpath_node_set::type_sorted;
09119 
09120             bool once =
09121                 (axis == axis_attribute && _test == nodetest_name) ||
09122                 (!_right && eval_once(axis_type, eval)) ||
09123                 (_right && !_right->_next && _right->_test == predicate_constant_one);
09124 
09125             xpath_node_set_raw ns;
09126             ns.set_type(axis_type);
09127 
09128             if (_left)
09129             {
09130                 xpath_node_set_raw s = _left->eval_node_set(c, stack, nodeset_eval_all);
09131 
09132                 // self axis preserves the original order
09133                 if (axis == axis_self) ns.set_type(s.type());
09134 
09135                 for (const xpath_node* it = s.begin(); it != s.end(); ++it)
09136                 {
09137                     size_t size = ns.size();
09138 
09139                     // in general, all axes generate elements in a particular order, but there is no order guarantee if axis is applied to two nodes
09140                     if (axis != axis_self && size != 0) ns.set_type(xpath_node_set::type_unsorted);
09141                     
09142                     step_fill(ns, *it, stack.result, once, v);
09143                     if (_right) apply_predicates(ns, size, stack, eval);
09144                 }
09145             }
09146             else
09147             {
09148                 step_fill(ns, c.n, stack.result, once, v);
09149                 if (_right) apply_predicates(ns, 0, stack, eval);
09150             }
09151 
09152             // child, attribute and self axes always generate unique set of nodes
09153             // for other axis, if the set stayed sorted, it stayed unique because the traversal algorithms do not visit the same node twice
09154             if (axis != axis_child && axis != axis_attribute && axis != axis_self && ns.type() == xpath_node_set::type_unsorted)
09155                 ns.remove_duplicates();
09156 
09157             return ns;
09158         }
09159         
09160     public:
09161         xpath_ast_node(ast_type_t type, xpath_value_type rettype_, const char_t* value):
09162             _type(static_cast<char>(type)), _rettype(static_cast<char>(rettype_)), _axis(0), _test(0), _left(0), _right(0), _next(0)
09163         {
09164             assert(type == ast_string_constant);
09165             _data.string = value;
09166         }
09167 
09168         xpath_ast_node(ast_type_t type, xpath_value_type rettype_, double value):
09169             _type(static_cast<char>(type)), _rettype(static_cast<char>(rettype_)), _axis(0), _test(0), _left(0), _right(0), _next(0)
09170         {
09171             assert(type == ast_number_constant);
09172             _data.number = value;
09173         }
09174         
09175         xpath_ast_node(ast_type_t type, xpath_value_type rettype_, xpath_variable* value):
09176             _type(static_cast<char>(type)), _rettype(static_cast<char>(rettype_)), _axis(0), _test(0), _left(0), _right(0), _next(0)
09177         {
09178             assert(type == ast_variable);
09179             _data.variable = value;
09180         }
09181         
09182         xpath_ast_node(ast_type_t type, xpath_value_type rettype_, xpath_ast_node* left = 0, xpath_ast_node* right = 0):
09183             _type(static_cast<char>(type)), _rettype(static_cast<char>(rettype_)), _axis(0), _test(0), _left(left), _right(right), _next(0)
09184         {
09185         }
09186 
09187         xpath_ast_node(ast_type_t type, xpath_ast_node* left, axis_t axis, nodetest_t test, const char_t* contents):
09188             _type(static_cast<char>(type)), _rettype(xpath_type_node_set), _axis(static_cast<char>(axis)), _test(static_cast<char>(test)), _left(left), _right(0), _next(0)
09189         {
09190             assert(type == ast_step);
09191             _data.nodetest = contents;
09192         }
09193 
09194         xpath_ast_node(ast_type_t type, xpath_ast_node* left, xpath_ast_node* right, predicate_t test):
09195             _type(static_cast<char>(type)), _rettype(xpath_type_node_set), _axis(0), _test(static_cast<char>(test)), _left(left), _right(right), _next(0)
09196         {
09197             assert(type == ast_filter || type == ast_predicate);
09198         }
09199 
09200         void set_next(xpath_ast_node* value)
09201         {
09202             _next = value;
09203         }
09204 
09205         void set_right(xpath_ast_node* value)
09206         {
09207             _right = value;
09208         }
09209 
09210         bool eval_boolean(const xpath_context& c, const xpath_stack& stack)
09211         {
09212             switch (_type)
09213             {
09214             case ast_op_or:
09215                 return _left->eval_boolean(c, stack) || _right->eval_boolean(c, stack);
09216                 
09217             case ast_op_and:
09218                 return _left->eval_boolean(c, stack) && _right->eval_boolean(c, stack);
09219                 
09220             case ast_op_equal:
09221                 return compare_eq(_left, _right, c, stack, equal_to());
09222 
09223             case ast_op_not_equal:
09224                 return compare_eq(_left, _right, c, stack, not_equal_to());
09225     
09226             case ast_op_less:
09227                 return compare_rel(_left, _right, c, stack, less());
09228             
09229             case ast_op_greater:
09230                 return compare_rel(_right, _left, c, stack, less());
09231 
09232             case ast_op_less_or_equal:
09233                 return compare_rel(_left, _right, c, stack, less_equal());
09234             
09235             case ast_op_greater_or_equal:
09236                 return compare_rel(_right, _left, c, stack, less_equal());
09237 
09238             case ast_func_starts_with:
09239             {
09240                 xpath_allocator_capture cr(stack.result);
09241 
09242                 xpath_string lr = _left->eval_string(c, stack);
09243                 xpath_string rr = _right->eval_string(c, stack);
09244 
09245                 return starts_with(lr.c_str(), rr.c_str());
09246             }
09247 
09248             case ast_func_contains:
09249             {
09250                 xpath_allocator_capture cr(stack.result);
09251 
09252                 xpath_string lr = _left->eval_string(c, stack);
09253                 xpath_string rr = _right->eval_string(c, stack);
09254 
09255                 return find_substring(lr.c_str(), rr.c_str()) != 0;
09256             }
09257 
09258             case ast_func_boolean:
09259                 return _left->eval_boolean(c, stack);
09260                 
09261             case ast_func_not:
09262                 return !_left->eval_boolean(c, stack);
09263                 
09264             case ast_func_true:
09265                 return true;
09266                 
09267             case ast_func_false:
09268                 return false;
09269 
09270             case ast_func_lang:
09271             {
09272                 if (c.n.attribute()) return false;
09273                 
09274                 xpath_allocator_capture cr(stack.result);
09275 
09276                 xpath_string lang = _left->eval_string(c, stack);
09277                 
09278                 for (xml_node n = c.n.node(); n; n = n.parent())
09279                 {
09280                     xml_attribute a = n.attribute(PUGIXML_TEXT("xml:lang"));
09281                     
09282                     if (a)
09283                     {
09284                         const char_t* value = a.value();
09285                         
09286                         // strnicmp / strncasecmp is not portable
09287                         for (const char_t* lit = lang.c_str(); *lit; ++lit)
09288                         {
09289                             if (tolower_ascii(*lit) != tolower_ascii(*value)) return false;
09290                             ++value;
09291                         }
09292                         
09293                         return *value == 0 || *value == '-';
09294                     }
09295                 }
09296                 
09297                 return false;
09298             }
09299 
09300             case ast_opt_compare_attribute:
09301             {
09302                 const char_t* value = (_right->_type == ast_string_constant) ? _right->_data.string : _right->_data.variable->get_string();
09303 
09304                 xml_attribute attr = c.n.node().attribute(_left->_data.nodetest);
09305 
09306                 return attr && strequal(attr.value(), value) && is_xpath_attribute(attr.name());
09307             }
09308 
09309             case ast_variable:
09310             {
09311                 assert(_rettype == _data.variable->type());
09312 
09313                 if (_rettype == xpath_type_boolean)
09314                     return _data.variable->get_boolean();
09315 
09316                 // fallthrough to type conversion
09317             }
09318 
09319             default:
09320             {
09321                 switch (_rettype)
09322                 {
09323                 case xpath_type_number:
09324                     return convert_number_to_boolean(eval_number(c, stack));
09325                     
09326                 case xpath_type_string:
09327                 {
09328                     xpath_allocator_capture cr(stack.result);
09329 
09330                     return !eval_string(c, stack).empty();
09331                 }
09332                     
09333                 case xpath_type_node_set:               
09334                 {
09335                     xpath_allocator_capture cr(stack.result);
09336 
09337                     return !eval_node_set(c, stack, nodeset_eval_any).empty();
09338                 }
09339 
09340                 default:
09341                     assert(!"Wrong expression for return type boolean");
09342                     return false;
09343                 }
09344             }
09345             }
09346         }
09347 
09348         double eval_number(const xpath_context& c, const xpath_stack& stack)
09349         {
09350             switch (_type)
09351             {
09352             case ast_op_add:
09353                 return _left->eval_number(c, stack) + _right->eval_number(c, stack);
09354                 
09355             case ast_op_subtract:
09356                 return _left->eval_number(c, stack) - _right->eval_number(c, stack);
09357 
09358             case ast_op_multiply:
09359                 return _left->eval_number(c, stack) * _right->eval_number(c, stack);
09360 
09361             case ast_op_divide:
09362                 return _left->eval_number(c, stack) / _right->eval_number(c, stack);
09363 
09364             case ast_op_mod:
09365                 return fmod(_left->eval_number(c, stack), _right->eval_number(c, stack));
09366 
09367             case ast_op_negate:
09368                 return -_left->eval_number(c, stack);
09369 
09370             case ast_number_constant:
09371                 return _data.number;
09372 
09373             case ast_func_last:
09374                 return static_cast<double>(c.size);
09375             
09376             case ast_func_position:
09377                 return static_cast<double>(c.position);
09378 
09379             case ast_func_count:
09380             {
09381                 xpath_allocator_capture cr(stack.result);
09382 
09383                 return static_cast<double>(_left->eval_node_set(c, stack, nodeset_eval_all).size());
09384             }
09385             
09386             case ast_func_string_length_0:
09387             {
09388                 xpath_allocator_capture cr(stack.result);
09389 
09390                 return static_cast<double>(string_value(c.n, stack.result).length());
09391             }
09392             
09393             case ast_func_string_length_1:
09394             {
09395                 xpath_allocator_capture cr(stack.result);
09396 
09397                 return static_cast<double>(_left->eval_string(c, stack).length());
09398             }
09399             
09400             case ast_func_number_0:
09401             {
09402                 xpath_allocator_capture cr(stack.result);
09403 
09404                 return convert_string_to_number(string_value(c.n, stack.result).c_str());
09405             }
09406             
09407             case ast_func_number_1:
09408                 return _left->eval_number(c, stack);
09409 
09410             case ast_func_sum:
09411             {
09412                 xpath_allocator_capture cr(stack.result);
09413 
09414                 double r = 0;
09415                 
09416                 xpath_node_set_raw ns = _left->eval_node_set(c, stack, nodeset_eval_all);
09417                 
09418                 for (const xpath_node* it = ns.begin(); it != ns.end(); ++it)
09419                 {
09420                     xpath_allocator_capture cri(stack.result);
09421 
09422                     r += convert_string_to_number(string_value(*it, stack.result).c_str());
09423                 }
09424             
09425                 return r;
09426             }
09427 
09428             case ast_func_floor:
09429             {
09430                 double r = _left->eval_number(c, stack);
09431                 
09432                 return r == r ? floor(r) : r;
09433             }
09434 
09435             case ast_func_ceiling:
09436             {
09437                 double r = _left->eval_number(c, stack);
09438                 
09439                 return r == r ? ceil(r) : r;
09440             }
09441 
09442             case ast_func_round:
09443                 return round_nearest_nzero(_left->eval_number(c, stack));
09444             
09445             case ast_variable:
09446             {
09447                 assert(_rettype == _data.variable->type());
09448 
09449                 if (_rettype == xpath_type_number)
09450                     return _data.variable->get_number();
09451 
09452                 // fallthrough to type conversion
09453             }
09454 
09455             default:
09456             {
09457                 switch (_rettype)
09458                 {
09459                 case xpath_type_boolean:
09460                     return eval_boolean(c, stack) ? 1 : 0;
09461                     
09462                 case xpath_type_string:
09463                 {
09464                     xpath_allocator_capture cr(stack.result);
09465 
09466                     return convert_string_to_number(eval_string(c, stack).c_str());
09467                 }
09468                     
09469                 case xpath_type_node_set:
09470                 {
09471                     xpath_allocator_capture cr(stack.result);
09472 
09473                     return convert_string_to_number(eval_string(c, stack).c_str());
09474                 }
09475                     
09476                 default:
09477                     assert(!"Wrong expression for return type number");
09478                     return 0;
09479                 }
09480                 
09481             }
09482             }
09483         }
09484         
09485         xpath_string eval_string_concat(const xpath_context& c, const xpath_stack& stack)
09486         {
09487             assert(_type == ast_func_concat);
09488 
09489             xpath_allocator_capture ct(stack.temp);
09490 
09491             // count the string number
09492             size_t count = 1;
09493             for (xpath_ast_node* nc = _right; nc; nc = nc->_next) count++;
09494 
09495             // gather all strings
09496             xpath_string static_buffer[4];
09497             xpath_string* buffer = static_buffer;
09498 
09499             // allocate on-heap for large concats
09500             if (count > sizeof(static_buffer) / sizeof(static_buffer[0]))
09501             {
09502                 buffer = static_cast<xpath_string*>(stack.temp->allocate(count * sizeof(xpath_string)));
09503                 assert(buffer);
09504             }
09505 
09506             // evaluate all strings to temporary stack
09507             xpath_stack swapped_stack = {stack.temp, stack.result};
09508 
09509             buffer[0] = _left->eval_string(c, swapped_stack);
09510 
09511             size_t pos = 1;
09512             for (xpath_ast_node* n = _right; n; n = n->_next, ++pos) buffer[pos] = n->eval_string(c, swapped_stack);
09513             assert(pos == count);
09514 
09515             // get total length
09516             size_t length = 0;
09517             for (size_t i = 0; i < count; ++i) length += buffer[i].length();
09518 
09519             // create final string
09520             char_t* result = static_cast<char_t*>(stack.result->allocate((length + 1) * sizeof(char_t)));
09521             assert(result);
09522 
09523             char_t* ri = result;
09524 
09525             for (size_t j = 0; j < count; ++j)
09526                 for (const char_t* bi = buffer[j].c_str(); *bi; ++bi)
09527                     *ri++ = *bi;
09528 
09529             *ri = 0;
09530 
09531             return xpath_string::from_heap_preallocated(result, ri);
09532         }
09533 
09534         xpath_string eval_string(const xpath_context& c, const xpath_stack& stack)
09535         {
09536             switch (_type)
09537             {
09538             case ast_string_constant:
09539                 return xpath_string::from_const(_data.string);
09540             
09541             case ast_func_local_name_0:
09542             {
09543                 xpath_node na = c.n;
09544                 
09545                 return xpath_string::from_const(local_name(na));
09546             }
09547 
09548             case ast_func_local_name_1:
09549             {
09550                 xpath_allocator_capture cr(stack.result);
09551 
09552                 xpath_node_set_raw ns = _left->eval_node_set(c, stack, nodeset_eval_first);
09553                 xpath_node na = ns.first();
09554                 
09555                 return xpath_string::from_const(local_name(na));
09556             }
09557 
09558             case ast_func_name_0:
09559             {
09560                 xpath_node na = c.n;
09561                 
09562                 return xpath_string::from_const(qualified_name(na));
09563             }
09564 
09565             case ast_func_name_1:
09566             {
09567                 xpath_allocator_capture cr(stack.result);
09568 
09569                 xpath_node_set_raw ns = _left->eval_node_set(c, stack, nodeset_eval_first);
09570                 xpath_node na = ns.first();
09571                 
09572                 return xpath_string::from_const(qualified_name(na));
09573             }
09574 
09575             case ast_func_namespace_uri_0:
09576             {
09577                 xpath_node na = c.n;
09578                 
09579                 return xpath_string::from_const(namespace_uri(na));
09580             }
09581 
09582             case ast_func_namespace_uri_1:
09583             {
09584                 xpath_allocator_capture cr(stack.result);
09585 
09586                 xpath_node_set_raw ns = _left->eval_node_set(c, stack, nodeset_eval_first);
09587                 xpath_node na = ns.first();
09588                 
09589                 return xpath_string::from_const(namespace_uri(na));
09590             }
09591 
09592             case ast_func_string_0:
09593                 return string_value(c.n, stack.result);
09594 
09595             case ast_func_string_1:
09596                 return _left->eval_string(c, stack);
09597 
09598             case ast_func_concat:
09599                 return eval_string_concat(c, stack);
09600 
09601             case ast_func_substring_before:
09602             {
09603                 xpath_allocator_capture cr(stack.temp);
09604 
09605                 xpath_stack swapped_stack = {stack.temp, stack.result};
09606 
09607                 xpath_string s = _left->eval_string(c, swapped_stack);
09608                 xpath_string p = _right->eval_string(c, swapped_stack);
09609 
09610                 const char_t* pos = find_substring(s.c_str(), p.c_str());
09611                 
09612                 return pos ? xpath_string::from_heap(s.c_str(), pos, stack.result) : xpath_string();
09613             }
09614             
09615             case ast_func_substring_after:
09616             {
09617                 xpath_allocator_capture cr(stack.temp);
09618 
09619                 xpath_stack swapped_stack = {stack.temp, stack.result};
09620 
09621                 xpath_string s = _left->eval_string(c, swapped_stack);
09622                 xpath_string p = _right->eval_string(c, swapped_stack);
09623                 
09624                 const char_t* pos = find_substring(s.c_str(), p.c_str());
09625                 if (!pos) return xpath_string();
09626 
09627                 const char_t* rbegin = pos + p.length();
09628                 const char_t* rend = s.c_str() + s.length();
09629 
09630                 return s.uses_heap() ? xpath_string::from_heap(rbegin, rend, stack.result) : xpath_string::from_const(rbegin);
09631             }
09632 
09633             case ast_func_substring_2:
09634             {
09635                 xpath_allocator_capture cr(stack.temp);
09636 
09637                 xpath_stack swapped_stack = {stack.temp, stack.result};
09638 
09639                 xpath_string s = _left->eval_string(c, swapped_stack);
09640                 size_t s_length = s.length();
09641 
09642                 double first = round_nearest(_right->eval_number(c, stack));
09643                 
09644                 if (is_nan(first)) return xpath_string(); // NaN
09645                 else if (first >= s_length + 1) return xpath_string();
09646                 
09647                 size_t pos = first < 1 ? 1 : static_cast<size_t>(first);
09648                 assert(1 <= pos && pos <= s_length + 1);
09649 
09650                 const char_t* rbegin = s.c_str() + (pos - 1);
09651                 const char_t* rend = s.c_str() + s.length();
09652                 
09653                 return s.uses_heap() ? xpath_string::from_heap(rbegin, rend, stack.result) : xpath_string::from_const(rbegin);
09654             }
09655             
09656             case ast_func_substring_3:
09657             {
09658                 xpath_allocator_capture cr(stack.temp);
09659 
09660                 xpath_stack swapped_stack = {stack.temp, stack.result};
09661 
09662                 xpath_string s = _left->eval_string(c, swapped_stack);
09663                 size_t s_length = s.length();
09664 
09665                 double first = round_nearest(_right->eval_number(c, stack));
09666                 double last = first + round_nearest(_right->_next->eval_number(c, stack));
09667                 
09668                 if (is_nan(first) || is_nan(last)) return xpath_string();
09669                 else if (first >= s_length + 1) return xpath_string();
09670                 else if (first >= last) return xpath_string();
09671                 else if (last < 1) return xpath_string();
09672                 
09673                 size_t pos = first < 1 ? 1 : static_cast<size_t>(first);
09674                 size_t end = last >= s_length + 1 ? s_length + 1 : static_cast<size_t>(last);
09675 
09676                 assert(1 <= pos && pos <= end && end <= s_length + 1);
09677                 const char_t* rbegin = s.c_str() + (pos - 1);
09678                 const char_t* rend = s.c_str() + (end - 1);
09679 
09680                 return (end == s_length + 1 && !s.uses_heap()) ? xpath_string::from_const(rbegin) : xpath_string::from_heap(rbegin, rend, stack.result);
09681             }
09682 
09683             case ast_func_normalize_space_0:
09684             {
09685                 xpath_string s = string_value(c.n, stack.result);
09686 
09687                 char_t* begin = s.data(stack.result);
09688                 char_t* end = normalize_space(begin);
09689 
09690                 return xpath_string::from_heap_preallocated(begin, end);
09691             }
09692 
09693             case ast_func_normalize_space_1:
09694             {
09695                 xpath_string s = _left->eval_string(c, stack);
09696 
09697                 char_t* begin = s.data(stack.result);
09698                 char_t* end = normalize_space(begin);
09699             
09700                 return xpath_string::from_heap_preallocated(begin, end);
09701             }
09702 
09703             case ast_func_translate:
09704             {
09705                 xpath_allocator_capture cr(stack.temp);
09706 
09707                 xpath_stack swapped_stack = {stack.temp, stack.result};
09708 
09709                 xpath_string s = _left->eval_string(c, stack);
09710                 xpath_string from = _right->eval_string(c, swapped_stack);
09711                 xpath_string to = _right->_next->eval_string(c, swapped_stack);
09712 
09713                 char_t* begin = s.data(stack.result);
09714                 char_t* end = translate(begin, from.c_str(), to.c_str(), to.length());
09715 
09716                 return xpath_string::from_heap_preallocated(begin, end);
09717             }
09718 
09719             case ast_opt_translate_table:
09720             {
09721                 xpath_string s = _left->eval_string(c, stack);
09722 
09723                 char_t* begin = s.data(stack.result);
09724                 char_t* end = translate_table(begin, _data.table);
09725 
09726                 return xpath_string::from_heap_preallocated(begin, end);
09727             }
09728 
09729             case ast_variable:
09730             {
09731                 assert(_rettype == _data.variable->type());
09732 
09733                 if (_rettype == xpath_type_string)
09734                     return xpath_string::from_const(_data.variable->get_string());
09735 
09736                 // fallthrough to type conversion
09737             }
09738 
09739             default:
09740             {
09741                 switch (_rettype)
09742                 {
09743                 case xpath_type_boolean:
09744                     return xpath_string::from_const(eval_boolean(c, stack) ? PUGIXML_TEXT("true") : PUGIXML_TEXT("false"));
09745                     
09746                 case xpath_type_number:
09747                     return convert_number_to_string(eval_number(c, stack), stack.result);
09748                     
09749                 case xpath_type_node_set:
09750                 {
09751                     xpath_allocator_capture cr(stack.temp);
09752 
09753                     xpath_stack swapped_stack = {stack.temp, stack.result};
09754 
09755                     xpath_node_set_raw ns = eval_node_set(c, swapped_stack, nodeset_eval_first);
09756                     return ns.empty() ? xpath_string() : string_value(ns.first(), stack.result);
09757                 }
09758                 
09759                 default:
09760                     assert(!"Wrong expression for return type string");
09761                     return xpath_string();
09762                 }
09763             }
09764             }
09765         }
09766 
09767         xpath_node_set_raw eval_node_set(const xpath_context& c, const xpath_stack& stack, nodeset_eval_t eval)
09768         {
09769             switch (_type)
09770             {
09771             case ast_op_union:
09772             {
09773                 xpath_allocator_capture cr(stack.temp);
09774 
09775                 xpath_stack swapped_stack = {stack.temp, stack.result};
09776 
09777                 xpath_node_set_raw ls = _left->eval_node_set(c, swapped_stack, eval);
09778                 xpath_node_set_raw rs = _right->eval_node_set(c, stack, eval);
09779 
09780                 // we can optimize merging two sorted sets, but this is a very rare operation, so don't bother
09781                 rs.set_type(xpath_node_set::type_unsorted);
09782 
09783                 rs.append(ls.begin(), ls.end(), stack.result);
09784                 rs.remove_duplicates();
09785 
09786                 return rs;
09787             }
09788 
09789             case ast_filter:
09790             {
09791                 xpath_node_set_raw set = _left->eval_node_set(c, stack, _test == predicate_constant_one ? nodeset_eval_first : nodeset_eval_all);
09792 
09793                 // either expression is a number or it contains position() call; sort by document order
09794                 if (_test != predicate_posinv) set.sort_do();
09795 
09796                 bool once = eval_once(set.type(), eval);
09797 
09798                 apply_predicate(set, 0, stack, once);
09799             
09800                 return set;
09801             }
09802             
09803             case ast_func_id:
09804                 return xpath_node_set_raw();
09805             
09806             case ast_step:
09807             {
09808                 switch (_axis)
09809                 {
09810                 case axis_ancestor:
09811                     return step_do(c, stack, eval, axis_to_type<axis_ancestor>());
09812                     
09813                 case axis_ancestor_or_self:
09814                     return step_do(c, stack, eval, axis_to_type<axis_ancestor_or_self>());
09815 
09816                 case axis_attribute:
09817                     return step_do(c, stack, eval, axis_to_type<axis_attribute>());
09818 
09819                 case axis_child:
09820                     return step_do(c, stack, eval, axis_to_type<axis_child>());
09821                 
09822                 case axis_descendant:
09823                     return step_do(c, stack, eval, axis_to_type<axis_descendant>());
09824 
09825                 case axis_descendant_or_self:
09826                     return step_do(c, stack, eval, axis_to_type<axis_descendant_or_self>());
09827 
09828                 case axis_following:
09829                     return step_do(c, stack, eval, axis_to_type<axis_following>());
09830                 
09831                 case axis_following_sibling:
09832                     return step_do(c, stack, eval, axis_to_type<axis_following_sibling>());
09833                 
09834                 case axis_namespace:
09835                     // namespaced axis is not supported
09836                     return xpath_node_set_raw();
09837                 
09838                 case axis_parent:
09839                     return step_do(c, stack, eval, axis_to_type<axis_parent>());
09840                 
09841                 case axis_preceding:
