09842                     return step_do(c, stack, eval, axis_to_type<axis_preceding>());
09843 
09844                 case axis_preceding_sibling:
09845                     return step_do(c, stack, eval, axis_to_type<axis_preceding_sibling>());
09846                 
09847                 case axis_self:
09848                     return step_do(c, stack, eval, axis_to_type<axis_self>());
09849 
09850                 default:
09851                     assert(!"Unknown axis");
09852                     return xpath_node_set_raw();
09853                 }
09854             }
09855 
09856             case ast_step_root:
09857             {
09858                 assert(!_right); // root step can't have any predicates
09859 
09860                 xpath_node_set_raw ns;
09861 
09862                 ns.set_type(xpath_node_set::type_sorted);
09863 
09864                 if (c.n.node()) ns.push_back(c.n.node().root(), stack.result);
09865                 else if (c.n.attribute()) ns.push_back(c.n.parent().root(), stack.result);
09866 
09867                 return ns;
09868             }
09869 
09870             case ast_variable:
09871             {
09872                 assert(_rettype == _data.variable->type());
09873 
09874                 if (_rettype == xpath_type_node_set)
09875                 {
09876                     const xpath_node_set& s = _data.variable->get_node_set();
09877 
09878                     xpath_node_set_raw ns;
09879 
09880                     ns.set_type(s.type());
09881                     ns.append(s.begin(), s.end(), stack.result);
09882 
09883                     return ns;
09884                 }
09885 
09886                 // fallthrough to type conversion
09887             }
09888 
09889             default:
09890                 assert(!"Wrong expression for return type node set");
09891                 return xpath_node_set_raw();
09892             }
09893         }
09894 
09895         void optimize(xpath_allocator* alloc)
09896         {
09897             if (_left) _left->optimize(alloc);
09898             if (_right) _right->optimize(alloc);
09899             if (_next) _next->optimize(alloc);
09900 
09901             // Rewrite [position()=expr] with [expr]
09902             // Note that this step has to go before classification to recognize [position()=1]
09903             if ((_type == ast_filter || _type == ast_predicate) &&
09904                 _right->_type == ast_op_equal && _right->_left->_type == ast_func_position && _right->_right->_rettype == xpath_type_number)
09905             {
09906                 _right = _right->_right;
09907             }
09908 
09909             // Classify filter/predicate ops to perform various optimizations during evaluation
09910             if (_type == ast_filter || _type == ast_predicate)
09911             {
09912                 assert(_test == predicate_default);
09913 
09914                 if (_right->_type == ast_number_constant && _right->_data.number == 1.0)
09915                     _test = predicate_constant_one;
09916                 else if (_right->_rettype == xpath_type_number && (_right->_type == ast_number_constant || _right->_type == ast_variable || _right->_type == ast_func_last))
09917                     _test = predicate_constant;
09918                 else if (_right->_rettype != xpath_type_number && _right->is_posinv_expr())
09919                     _test = predicate_posinv;
09920             }
09921 
09922             // Rewrite descendant-or-self::node()/child::foo with descendant::foo
09923             // The former is a full form of //foo, the latter is much faster since it executes the node test immediately
09924             // Do a similar kind of rewrite for self/descendant/descendant-or-self axes
09925             // Note that we only rewrite positionally invariant steps (//foo[1] != /descendant::foo[1])
09926             if (_type == ast_step && (_axis == axis_child || _axis == axis_self || _axis == axis_descendant || _axis == axis_descendant_or_self) && _left &&
09927                 _left->_type == ast_step && _left->_axis == axis_descendant_or_self && _left->_test == nodetest_type_node && !_left->_right &&
09928                 is_posinv_step())
09929             {
09930                 if (_axis == axis_child || _axis == axis_descendant)
09931                     _axis = axis_descendant;
09932                 else
09933                     _axis = axis_descendant_or_self;
09934 
09935                 _left = _left->_left;
09936             }
09937 
09938             // Use optimized lookup table implementation for translate() with constant arguments
09939             if (_type == ast_func_translate && _right->_type == ast_string_constant && _right->_next->_type == ast_string_constant)
09940             {
09941                 unsigned char* table = translate_table_generate(alloc, _right->_data.string, _right->_next->_data.string);
09942 
09943                 if (table)
09944                 {
09945                     _type = ast_opt_translate_table;
09946                     _data.table = table;
09947                 }
09948             }
09949 
09950             // Use optimized path for @attr = 'value' or @attr = $value
09951             if (_type == ast_op_equal &&
09952                 _left->_type == ast_step && _left->_axis == axis_attribute && _left->_test == nodetest_name && !_left->_left && !_left->_right &&
09953                 (_right->_type == ast_string_constant || (_right->_type == ast_variable && _right->_rettype == xpath_type_string)))
09954             {
09955                 _type = ast_opt_compare_attribute;
09956             }
09957         }
09958         
09959         bool is_posinv_expr() const
09960         {
09961             switch (_type)
09962             {
09963             case ast_func_position:
09964             case ast_func_last:
09965                 return false;
09966 
09967             case ast_string_constant:
09968             case ast_number_constant:
09969             case ast_variable:
09970                 return true;
09971 
09972             case ast_step:
09973             case ast_step_root:
09974                 return true;
09975 
09976             case ast_predicate:
09977             case ast_filter:
09978                 return true;
09979 
09980             default:
09981                 if (_left && !_left->is_posinv_expr()) return false;
09982                 
09983                 for (xpath_ast_node* n = _right; n; n = n->_next)
09984                     if (!n->is_posinv_expr()) return false;
09985                     
09986                 return true;
09987             }
09988         }
09989 
09990         bool is_posinv_step() const
09991         {
09992             assert(_type == ast_step);
09993 
09994             for (xpath_ast_node* n = _right; n; n = n->_next)
09995             {
09996                 assert(n->_type == ast_predicate);
09997 
09998                 if (n->_test != predicate_posinv)
09999                     return false;
10000             }
10001 
10002             return true;
10003         }
10004 
10005         xpath_value_type rettype() const
10006         {
10007             return static_cast<xpath_value_type>(_rettype);
10008         }
10009     };
10010 
10011     struct xpath_parser
10012     {
10013         xpath_allocator* _alloc;
10014         xpath_lexer _lexer;
10015 
10016         const char_t* _query;
10017         xpath_variable_set* _variables;
10018 
10019         xpath_parse_result* _result;
10020 
10021         char_t _scratch[32];
10022 
10023     #ifdef PUGIXML_NO_EXCEPTIONS
10024         jmp_buf _error_handler;
10025     #endif
10026 
10027         void throw_error(const char* message)
10028         {
10029             _result->error = message;
10030             _result->offset = _lexer.current_pos() - _query;
10031 
10032         #ifdef PUGIXML_NO_EXCEPTIONS
10033             longjmp(_error_handler, 1);
10034         #else
10035             throw xpath_exception(*_result);
10036         #endif
10037         }
10038 
10039         void throw_error_oom()
10040         {
10041         #ifdef PUGIXML_NO_EXCEPTIONS
10042             throw_error("Out of memory");
10043         #else
10044             throw std::bad_alloc();
10045         #endif
10046         }
10047 
10048         void* alloc_node()
10049         {
10050             void* result = _alloc->allocate_nothrow(sizeof(xpath_ast_node));
10051 
10052             if (!result) throw_error_oom();
10053 
10054             return result;
10055         }
10056 
10057         const char_t* alloc_string(const xpath_lexer_string& value)
10058         {
10059             if (value.begin)
10060             {
10061                 size_t length = static_cast<size_t>(value.end - value.begin);
10062 
10063                 char_t* c = static_cast<char_t*>(_alloc->allocate_nothrow((length + 1) * sizeof(char_t)));
10064                 if (!c) throw_error_oom();
10065                 assert(c); // workaround for clang static analysis
10066 
10067                 memcpy(c, value.begin, length * sizeof(char_t));
10068                 c[length] = 0;
10069 
10070                 return c;
10071             }
10072             else return 0;
10073         }
10074 
10075         xpath_ast_node* parse_function_helper(ast_type_t type0, ast_type_t type1, size_t argc, xpath_ast_node* args[2])
10076         {
10077             assert(argc <= 1);
10078 
10079             if (argc == 1 && args[0]->rettype() != xpath_type_node_set) throw_error("Function has to be applied to node set");
10080 
10081             return new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(argc == 0 ? type0 : type1, xpath_type_string, args[0]);
10082         }
10083 
10084         xpath_ast_node* parse_function(const xpath_lexer_string& name, size_t argc, xpath_ast_node* args[2])
10085         {
10086             switch (name.begin[0])
10087             {
10088             case 'b':
10089                 if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("boolean") && argc == 1)
10090                     return new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(ast_func_boolean, xpath_type_boolean, args[0]);
10091                     
10092                 break;
10093             
10094             case 'c':
10095                 if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("count") && argc == 1)
10096                 {
10097                     if (args[0]->rettype() != xpath_type_node_set) throw_error("Function has to be applied to node set");
10098                     return new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(ast_func_count, xpath_type_number, args[0]);
10099                 }
10100                 else if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("contains") && argc == 2)
10101                     return new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(ast_func_contains, xpath_type_boolean, args[0], args[1]);
10102                 else if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("concat") && argc >= 2)
10103                     return new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(ast_func_concat, xpath_type_string, args[0], args[1]);
10104                 else if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("ceiling") && argc == 1)
10105                     return new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(ast_func_ceiling, xpath_type_number, args[0]);
10106                     
10107                 break;
10108             
10109             case 'f':
10110                 if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("false") && argc == 0)
10111                     return new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(ast_func_false, xpath_type_boolean);
10112                 else if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("floor") && argc == 1)
10113                     return new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(ast_func_floor, xpath_type_number, args[0]);
10114                     
10115                 break;
10116             
10117             case 'i':
10118                 if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("id") && argc == 1)
10119                     return new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(ast_func_id, xpath_type_node_set, args[0]);
10120                     
10121                 break;
10122             
10123             case 'l':
10124                 if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("last") && argc == 0)
10125                     return new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(ast_func_last, xpath_type_number);
10126                 else if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("lang") && argc == 1)
10127                     return new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(ast_func_lang, xpath_type_boolean, args[0]);
10128                 else if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("local-name") && argc <= 1)
10129                     return parse_function_helper(ast_func_local_name_0, ast_func_local_name_1, argc, args);
10130             
10131                 break;
10132             
10133             case 'n':
10134                 if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("name") && argc <= 1)
10135                     return parse_function_helper(ast_func_name_0, ast_func_name_1, argc, args);
10136                 else if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("namespace-uri") && argc <= 1)
10137                     return parse_function_helper(ast_func_namespace_uri_0, ast_func_namespace_uri_1, argc, args);
10138                 else if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("normalize-space") && argc <= 1)
10139                     return new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(argc == 0 ? ast_func_normalize_space_0 : ast_func_normalize_space_1, xpath_type_string, args[0], args[1]);
10140                 else if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("not") && argc == 1)
10141                     return new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(ast_func_not, xpath_type_boolean, args[0]);
10142                 else if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("number") && argc <= 1)
10143                     return new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(argc == 0 ? ast_func_number_0 : ast_func_number_1, xpath_type_number, args[0]);
10144             
10145                 break;
10146             
10147             case 'p':
10148                 if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("position") && argc == 0)
10149                     return new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(ast_func_position, xpath_type_number);
10150                 
10151                 break;
10152             
10153             case 'r':
10154                 if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("round") && argc == 1)
10155                     return new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(ast_func_round, xpath_type_number, args[0]);
10156 
10157                 break;
10158             
10159             case 's':
10160                 if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("string") && argc <= 1)
10161                     return new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(argc == 0 ? ast_func_string_0 : ast_func_string_1, xpath_type_string, args[0]);
10162                 else if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("string-length") && argc <= 1)
10163                     return new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(argc == 0 ? ast_func_string_length_0 : ast_func_string_length_1, xpath_type_number, args[0]);
10164                 else if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("starts-with") && argc == 2)
10165                     return new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(ast_func_starts_with, xpath_type_boolean, args[0], args[1]);
10166                 else if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("substring-before") && argc == 2)
10167                     return new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(ast_func_substring_before, xpath_type_string, args[0], args[1]);
10168                 else if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("substring-after") && argc == 2)
10169                     return new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(ast_func_substring_after, xpath_type_string, args[0], args[1]);
10170                 else if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("substring") && (argc == 2 || argc == 3))
10171                     return new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(argc == 2 ? ast_func_substring_2 : ast_func_substring_3, xpath_type_string, args[0], args[1]);
10172                 else if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("sum") && argc == 1)
10173                 {
10174                     if (args[0]->rettype() != xpath_type_node_set) throw_error("Function has to be applied to node set");
10175                     return new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(ast_func_sum, xpath_type_number, args[0]);
10176                 }
10177 
10178                 break;
10179             
10180             case 't':
10181                 if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("translate") && argc == 3)
10182                     return new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(ast_func_translate, xpath_type_string, args[0], args[1]);
10183                 else if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("true") && argc == 0)
10184                     return new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(ast_func_true, xpath_type_boolean);
10185                     
10186                 break;
10187 
10188             default:
10189                 break;
10190             }
10191 
10192             throw_error("Unrecognized function or wrong parameter count");
10193 
10194             return 0;
10195         }
10196 
10197         axis_t parse_axis_name(const xpath_lexer_string& name, bool& specified)
10198         {
10199             specified = true;
10200 
10201             switch (name.begin[0])
10202             {
10203             case 'a':
10204                 if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("ancestor"))
10205                     return axis_ancestor;
10206                 else if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("ancestor-or-self"))
10207                     return axis_ancestor_or_self;
10208                 else if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("attribute"))
10209                     return axis_attribute;
10210                 
10211                 break;
10212             
10213             case 'c':
10214                 if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("child"))
10215                     return axis_child;
10216                 
10217                 break;
10218             
10219             case 'd':
10220                 if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("descendant"))
10221                     return axis_descendant;
10222                 else if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("descendant-or-self"))
10223                     return axis_descendant_or_self;
10224                 
10225                 break;
10226             
10227             case 'f':
10228                 if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("following"))
10229                     return axis_following;
10230                 else if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("following-sibling"))
10231                     return axis_following_sibling;
10232                 
10233                 break;
10234             
10235             case 'n':
10236                 if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("namespace"))
10237                     return axis_namespace;
10238                 
10239                 break;
10240             
10241             case 'p':
10242                 if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("parent"))
10243                     return axis_parent;
10244                 else if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("preceding"))
10245                     return axis_preceding;
10246                 else if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("preceding-sibling"))
10247                     return axis_preceding_sibling;
10248                 
10249                 break;
10250             
10251             case 's':
10252                 if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("self"))
10253                     return axis_self;
10254                 
10255                 break;
10256 
10257             default:
10258                 break;
10259             }
10260 
10261             specified = false;
10262             return axis_child;
10263         }
10264 
10265         nodetest_t parse_node_test_type(const xpath_lexer_string& name)
10266         {
10267             switch (name.begin[0])
10268             {
10269             case 'c':
10270                 if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("comment"))
10271                     return nodetest_type_comment;
10272 
10273                 break;
10274 
10275             case 'n':
10276                 if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("node"))
10277                     return nodetest_type_node;
10278 
10279                 break;
10280 
10281             case 'p':
10282                 if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("processing-instruction"))
10283                     return nodetest_type_pi;
10284 
10285                 break;
10286 
10287             case 't':
10288                 if (name == PUGIXML_TEXT("text"))
10289                     return nodetest_type_text;
10290 
10291                 break;
10292             
10293             default:
10294                 break;
10295             }
10296 
10297             return nodetest_none;
10298         }
10299 
10300         // PrimaryExpr ::= VariableReference | '(' Expr ')' | Literal | Number | FunctionCall
10301         xpath_ast_node* parse_primary_expression()
10302         {
10303             switch (_lexer.current())
10304             {
10305             case lex_var_ref:
10306             {
10307                 xpath_lexer_string name = _lexer.contents();
10308 
10309                 if (!_variables)
10310                     throw_error("Unknown variable: variable set is not provided");
10311 
10312                 xpath_variable* var = get_variable_scratch(_scratch, _variables, name.begin, name.end);
10313 
10314                 if (!var)
10315                     throw_error("Unknown variable: variable set does not contain the given name");
10316 
10317                 _lexer.next();
10318 
10319                 return new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(ast_variable, var->type(), var);
10320             }
10321 
10322             case lex_open_brace:
10323             {
10324                 _lexer.next();
10325 
10326                 xpath_ast_node* n = parse_expression();
10327 
10328                 if (_lexer.current() != lex_close_brace)
10329                     throw_error("Unmatched braces");
10330 
10331                 _lexer.next();
10332 
10333                 return n;
10334             }
10335 
10336             case lex_quoted_string:
10337             {
10338                 const char_t* value = alloc_string(_lexer.contents());
10339 
10340                 xpath_ast_node* n = new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(ast_string_constant, xpath_type_string, value);
10341                 _lexer.next();
10342 
10343                 return n;
10344             }
10345 
10346             case lex_number:
10347             {
10348                 double value = 0;
10349 
10350                 if (!convert_string_to_number_scratch(_scratch, _lexer.contents().begin, _lexer.contents().end, &value))
10351                     throw_error_oom();
10352 
10353                 xpath_ast_node* n = new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(ast_number_constant, xpath_type_number, value);
10354                 _lexer.next();
10355 
10356                 return n;
10357             }
10358 
10359             case lex_string:
10360             {
10361                 xpath_ast_node* args[2] = {0};
10362                 size_t argc = 0;
10363                 
10364                 xpath_lexer_string function = _lexer.contents();
10365                 _lexer.next();
10366                 
10367                 xpath_ast_node* last_arg = 0;
10368                 
10369                 if (_lexer.current() != lex_open_brace)
10370                     throw_error("Unrecognized function call");
10371                 _lexer.next();
10372 
10373                 if (_lexer.current() != lex_close_brace)
10374                     args[argc++] = parse_expression();
10375 
10376                 while (_lexer.current() != lex_close_brace)
10377                 {
10378                     if (_lexer.current() != lex_comma)
10379                         throw_error("No comma between function arguments");
10380                     _lexer.next();
10381                     
10382                     xpath_ast_node* n = parse_expression();
10383                     
10384                     if (argc < 2) args[argc] = n;
10385                     else last_arg->set_next(n);
10386 
10387                     argc++;
10388                     last_arg = n;
10389                 }
10390                 
10391                 _lexer.next();
10392 
10393                 return parse_function(function, argc, args);
10394             }
10395 
10396             default:
10397                 throw_error("Unrecognizable primary expression");
10398 
10399                 return 0;
10400             }
10401         }
10402         
10403         // FilterExpr ::= PrimaryExpr | FilterExpr Predicate
10404         // Predicate ::= '[' PredicateExpr ']'
10405         // PredicateExpr ::= Expr
10406         xpath_ast_node* parse_filter_expression()
10407         {
10408             xpath_ast_node* n = parse_primary_expression();
10409 
10410             while (_lexer.current() == lex_open_square_brace)
10411             {
10412                 _lexer.next();
10413 
10414                 xpath_ast_node* expr = parse_expression();
10415 
10416                 if (n->rettype() != xpath_type_node_set) throw_error("Predicate has to be applied to node set");
10417 
10418                 n = new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(ast_filter, n, expr, predicate_default);
10419 
10420                 if (_lexer.current() != lex_close_square_brace)
10421                     throw_error("Unmatched square brace");
10422             
10423                 _lexer.next();
10424             }
10425             
10426             return n;
10427         }
10428         
10429         // Step ::= AxisSpecifier NodeTest Predicate* | AbbreviatedStep
10430         // AxisSpecifier ::= AxisName '::' | '@'?
10431         // NodeTest ::= NameTest | NodeType '(' ')' | 'processing-instruction' '(' Literal ')'
10432         // NameTest ::= '*' | NCName ':' '*' | QName
10433         // AbbreviatedStep ::= '.' | '..'
10434         xpath_ast_node* parse_step(xpath_ast_node* set)
10435         {
10436             if (set && set->rettype() != xpath_type_node_set)
10437                 throw_error("Step has to be applied to node set");
10438 
10439             bool axis_specified = false;
10440             axis_t axis = axis_child; // implied child axis
10441 
10442             if (_lexer.current() == lex_axis_attribute)
10443             {
10444                 axis = axis_attribute;
10445                 axis_specified = true;
10446                 
10447                 _lexer.next();
10448             }
10449             else if (_lexer.current() == lex_dot)
10450             {
10451                 _lexer.next();
10452                 
10453                 return new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(ast_step, set, axis_self, nodetest_type_node, 0);
10454             }
10455             else if (_lexer.current() == lex_double_dot)
10456             {
10457                 _lexer.next();
10458                 
10459                 return new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(ast_step, set, axis_parent, nodetest_type_node, 0);
10460             }
10461         
10462             nodetest_t nt_type = nodetest_none;
10463             xpath_lexer_string nt_name;
10464             
10465             if (_lexer.current() == lex_string)
10466             {
10467                 // node name test
10468                 nt_name = _lexer.contents();
10469                 _lexer.next();
10470 
10471                 // was it an axis name?
10472                 if (_lexer.current() == lex_double_colon)
10473                 {
10474                     // parse axis name
10475                     if (axis_specified) throw_error("Two axis specifiers in one step");
10476 
10477                     axis = parse_axis_name(nt_name, axis_specified);
10478 
10479                     if (!axis_specified) throw_error("Unknown axis");
10480 
10481                     // read actual node test
10482                     _lexer.next();
10483 
10484                     if (_lexer.current() == lex_multiply)
10485                     {
10486                         nt_type = nodetest_all;
10487                         nt_name = xpath_lexer_string();
10488                         _lexer.next();
10489                     }
10490                     else if (_lexer.current() == lex_string)
10491                     {
10492                         nt_name = _lexer.contents();
10493                         _lexer.next();
10494                     }
10495                     else throw_error("Unrecognized node test");
10496                 }
10497                 
10498                 if (nt_type == nodetest_none)
10499                 {
10500                     // node type test or processing-instruction
10501                     if (_lexer.current() == lex_open_brace)
10502                     {
10503                         _lexer.next();
10504                         
10505                         if (_lexer.current() == lex_close_brace)
10506                         {
10507                             _lexer.next();
10508 
10509                             nt_type = parse_node_test_type(nt_name);
10510 
10511                             if (nt_type == nodetest_none) throw_error("Unrecognized node type");
10512                             
10513                             nt_name = xpath_lexer_string();
10514                         }
10515                         else if (nt_name == PUGIXML_TEXT("processing-instruction"))
10516                         {
10517                             if (_lexer.current() != lex_quoted_string)
10518                                 throw_error("Only literals are allowed as arguments to processing-instruction()");
10519                         
10520                             nt_type = nodetest_pi;
10521                             nt_name = _lexer.contents();
10522                             _lexer.next();
10523                             
10524                             if (_lexer.current() != lex_close_brace)
10525                                 throw_error("Unmatched brace near processing-instruction()");
10526                             _lexer.next();
10527                         }
10528                         else
10529                             throw_error("Unmatched brace near node type test");
10530 
10531                     }
10532                     // QName or NCName:*
10533                     else
10534                     {
10535                         if (nt_name.end - nt_name.begin > 2 && nt_name.end[-2] == ':' && nt_name.end[-1] == '*') // NCName:*
10536                         {
10537                             nt_name.end--; // erase *
10538                             
10539                             nt_type = nodetest_all_in_namespace;
10540                         }
10541                         else nt_type = nodetest_name;
10542                     }
10543                 }
10544             }
10545             else if (_lexer.current() == lex_multiply)
10546             {
10547                 nt_type = nodetest_all;
10548                 _lexer.next();
10549             }
10550             else throw_error("Unrecognized node test");
10551             
10552             xpath_ast_node* n = new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(ast_step, set, axis, nt_type, alloc_string(nt_name));
10553             
10554             xpath_ast_node* last = 0;
10555             
10556             while (_lexer.current() == lex_open_square_brace)
10557             {
10558                 _lexer.next();
10559                 
10560                 xpath_ast_node* expr = parse_expression();
10561 
10562                 xpath_ast_node* pred = new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(ast_predicate, 0, expr, predicate_default);
10563                 
10564                 if (_lexer.current() != lex_close_square_brace)
10565                     throw_error("Unmatched square brace");
10566                 _lexer.next();
10567                 
10568                 if (last) last->set_next(pred);
10569                 else n->set_right(pred);
10570                 
10571                 last = pred;
10572             }
10573 
10574             return n;
10575         }
10576         
10577         // RelativeLocationPath ::= Step | RelativeLocationPath '/' Step | RelativeLocationPath '//' Step
10578         xpath_ast_node* parse_relative_location_path(xpath_ast_node* set)
10579         {
10580             xpath_ast_node* n = parse_step(set);
10581             
10582             while (_lexer.current() == lex_slash || _lexer.current() == lex_double_slash)
10583             {
10584                 lexeme_t l = _lexer.current();
10585                 _lexer.next();
10586 
10587                 if (l == lex_double_slash)
10588                     n = new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(ast_step, n, axis_descendant_or_self, nodetest_type_node, 0);
10589                 
10590                 n = parse_step(n);
10591             }
10592             
10593             return n;
10594         }
10595         
10596         // LocationPath ::= RelativeLocationPath | AbsoluteLocationPath
10597         // AbsoluteLocationPath ::= '/' RelativeLocationPath? | '//' RelativeLocationPath
10598         xpath_ast_node* parse_location_path()
10599         {
10600             if (_lexer.current() == lex_slash)
10601             {
10602                 _lexer.next();
10603                 
10604                 xpath_ast_node* n = new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(ast_step_root, xpath_type_node_set);
10605 
10606                 // relative location path can start from axis_attribute, dot, double_dot, multiply and string lexemes; any other lexeme means standalone root path
10607                 lexeme_t l = _lexer.current();
10608 
10609                 if (l == lex_string || l == lex_axis_attribute || l == lex_dot || l == lex_double_dot || l == lex_multiply)
10610                     return parse_relative_location_path(n);
10611                 else
10612                     return n;
10613             }
10614             else if (_lexer.current() == lex_double_slash)
10615             {
10616                 _lexer.next();
10617                 
10618                 xpath_ast_node* n = new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(ast_step_root, xpath_type_node_set);
10619                 n = new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(ast_step, n, axis_descendant_or_self, nodetest_type_node, 0);
10620                 
10621                 return parse_relative_location_path(n);
10622             }
10623 
10624             // else clause moved outside of if because of bogus warning 'control may reach end of non-void function being inlined' in gcc 4.0.1
10625             return parse_relative_location_path(0);
10626         }
10627         
10628         // PathExpr ::= LocationPath
10629         //              | FilterExpr
10630         //              | FilterExpr '/' RelativeLocationPath
10631         //              | FilterExpr '//' RelativeLocationPath
10632         // UnionExpr ::= PathExpr | UnionExpr '|' PathExpr
10633         // UnaryExpr ::= UnionExpr | '-' UnaryExpr
10634         xpath_ast_node* parse_path_or_unary_expression()
10635         {
10636             // Clarification.
10637             // PathExpr begins with either LocationPath or FilterExpr.
10638             // FilterExpr begins with PrimaryExpr
10639             // PrimaryExpr begins with '$' in case of it being a variable reference,
10640             // '(' in case of it being an expression, string literal, number constant or
10641             // function call.
10642 
10643             if (_lexer.current() == lex_var_ref || _lexer.current() == lex_open_brace || 
10644                 _lexer.current() == lex_quoted_string || _lexer.current() == lex_number ||
10645                 _lexer.current() == lex_string)
10646             {
10647                 if (_lexer.current() == lex_string)
10648                 {
10649                     // This is either a function call, or not - if not, we shall proceed with location path
10650                     const char_t* state = _lexer.state();
10651                     
10652                     while (PUGI__IS_CHARTYPE(*state, ct_space)) ++state;
10653                     
10654                     if (*state != '(') return parse_location_path();
10655 
10656                     // This looks like a function call; however this still can be a node-test. Check it.
10657                     if (parse_node_test_type(_lexer.contents()) != nodetest_none) return parse_location_path();
10658                 }
10659                 
10660                 xpath_ast_node* n = parse_filter_expression();
10661 
10662                 if (_lexer.current() == lex_slash || _lexer.current() == lex_double_slash)
10663                 {
10664                     lexeme_t l = _lexer.current();
10665                     _lexer.next();
10666                     
10667                     if (l == lex_double_slash)
10668                     {
10669                         if (n->rettype() != xpath_type_node_set) throw_error("Step has to be applied to node set");
10670 
10671                         n = new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(ast_step, n, axis_descendant_or_self, nodetest_type_node, 0);
10672                     }
10673     
10674                     // select from location path
10675                     return parse_relative_location_path(n);
10676                 }
10677 
10678                 return n;
10679             }
10680             else if (_lexer.current() == lex_minus)
10681             {
10682                 _lexer.next();
10683 
10684                 // precedence 7+ - only parses union expressions
10685                 xpath_ast_node* expr = parse_expression_rec(parse_path_or_unary_expression(), 7);
10686 
10687                 return new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(ast_op_negate, xpath_type_number, expr);
10688             }
10689             else
10690                 return parse_location_path();
10691         }
10692 
10693         struct binary_op_t
10694         {
10695             ast_type_t asttype;
10696             xpath_value_type rettype;
10697             int precedence;
10698 
10699             binary_op_t(): asttype(ast_unknown), rettype(xpath_type_none), precedence(0)
10700             {
10701             }
10702 
10703             binary_op_t(ast_type_t asttype_, xpath_value_type rettype_, int precedence_): asttype(asttype_), rettype(rettype_), precedence(precedence_)
10704             {
10705             }
10706 
10707             static binary_op_t parse(xpath_lexer& lexer)
10708             {
10709                 switch (lexer.current())
10710                 {
10711                 case lex_string:
10712                     if (lexer.contents() == PUGIXML_TEXT("or"))
10713                         return binary_op_t(ast_op_or, xpath_type_boolean, 1);
10714                     else if (lexer.contents() == PUGIXML_TEXT("and"))
10715                         return binary_op_t(ast_op_and, xpath_type_boolean, 2);
10716                     else if (lexer.contents() == PUGIXML_TEXT("div"))
10717                         return binary_op_t(ast_op_divide, xpath_type_number, 6);
10718                     else if (lexer.contents() == PUGIXML_TEXT("mod"))
10719                         return binary_op_t(ast_op_mod, xpath_type_number, 6);
10720                     else
10721                         return binary_op_t();
10722 
10723                 case lex_equal:
10724                     return binary_op_t(ast_op_equal, xpath_type_boolean, 3);
10725 
10726                 case lex_not_equal:
10727                     return binary_op_t(ast_op_not_equal, xpath_type_boolean, 3);
10728 
10729                 case lex_less:
10730                     return binary_op_t(ast_op_less, xpath_type_boolean, 4);
10731 
10732                 case lex_greater:
10733                     return binary_op_t(ast_op_greater, xpath_type_boolean, 4);
10734 
10735                 case lex_less_or_equal:
10736                     return binary_op_t(ast_op_less_or_equal, xpath_type_boolean, 4);
10737 
10738                 case lex_greater_or_equal:
10739                     return binary_op_t(ast_op_greater_or_equal, xpath_type_boolean, 4);
10740 
10741                 case lex_plus:
10742                     return binary_op_t(ast_op_add, xpath_type_number, 5);
10743 
10744                 case lex_minus:
10745                     return binary_op_t(ast_op_subtract, xpath_type_number, 5);
10746 
10747                 case lex_multiply:
10748                     return binary_op_t(ast_op_multiply, xpath_type_number, 6);
10749 
10750                 case lex_union:
10751                     return binary_op_t(ast_op_union, xpath_type_node_set, 7);
10752 
10753                 default:
10754                     return binary_op_t();
10755                 }
10756             }
10757         };
10758 
10759         xpath_ast_node* parse_expression_rec(xpath_ast_node* lhs, int limit)
10760         {
10761             binary_op_t op = binary_op_t::parse(_lexer);
10762 
10763             while (op.asttype != ast_unknown && op.precedence >= limit)
10764             {
10765                 _lexer.next();
10766 
10767                 xpath_ast_node* rhs = parse_path_or_unary_expression();
10768 
10769                 binary_op_t nextop = binary_op_t::parse(_lexer);
10770 
10771                 while (nextop.asttype != ast_unknown && nextop.precedence > op.precedence)
10772                 {
10773                     rhs = parse_expression_rec(rhs, nextop.precedence);
10774 
10775                     nextop = binary_op_t::parse(_lexer);
10776                 }
10777 
10778                 if (op.asttype == ast_op_union && (lhs->rettype() != xpath_type_node_set || rhs->rettype() != xpath_type_node_set))
10779                     throw_error("Union operator has to be applied to node sets");
10780 
10781                 lhs = new (alloc_node()) xpath_ast_node(op.asttype, op.rettype, lhs, rhs);
10782 
10783                 op = binary_op_t::parse(_lexer);
10784             }
10785 
10786             return lhs;
10787         }
10788 
10789         // Expr ::= OrExpr
10790         // OrExpr ::= AndExpr | OrExpr 'or' AndExpr
10791         // AndExpr ::= EqualityExpr | AndExpr 'and' EqualityExpr
10792         // EqualityExpr ::= RelationalExpr
10793         //                  | EqualityExpr '=' RelationalExpr
10794         //                  | EqualityExpr '!=' RelationalExpr
10795         // RelationalExpr ::= AdditiveExpr
10796         //                    | RelationalExpr '<' AdditiveExpr
10797         //                    | RelationalExpr '>' AdditiveExpr
10798         //                    | RelationalExpr '<=' AdditiveExpr
10799         //                    | RelationalExpr '>=' AdditiveExpr
10800         // AdditiveExpr ::= MultiplicativeExpr
10801         //                  | AdditiveExpr '+' MultiplicativeExpr
10802         //                  | AdditiveExpr '-' MultiplicativeExpr
10803         // MultiplicativeExpr ::= UnaryExpr
10804         //                        | MultiplicativeExpr '*' UnaryExpr
10805         //                        | MultiplicativeExpr 'div' UnaryExpr
10806         //                        | MultiplicativeExpr 'mod' UnaryExpr
10807         xpath_ast_node* parse_expression()
10808         {
10809             return parse_expression_rec(parse_path_or_unary_expression(), 0);
10810         }
10811 
10812         xpath_parser(const char_t* query, xpath_variable_set* variables, xpath_allocator* alloc, xpath_parse_result* result): _alloc(alloc), _lexer(query), _query(query), _variables(variables), _result(result)
10813         {
10814         }
10815 
10816         xpath_ast_node* parse()
10817         {
10818             xpath_ast_node* result = parse_expression();
10819             
10820             if (_lexer.current() != lex_eof)
10821             {
10822                 // there are still unparsed tokens left, error
10823                 throw_error("Incorrect query");
10824             }
10825             
10826             return result;
10827         }
10828 
10829         static xpath_ast_node* parse(const char_t* query, xpath_variable_set* variables, xpath_allocator* alloc, xpath_parse_result* result)
10830         {
10831             xpath_parser parser(query, variables, alloc, result);
10832 
10833         #ifdef PUGIXML_NO_EXCEPTIONS
10834             int error = setjmp(parser._error_handler);
10835 
10836             return (error == 0) ? parser.parse() : 0;
10837         #else
10838             return parser.parse();
10839         #endif
10840         }
10841     };
10842 
10843     struct xpath_query_impl
10844     {
10845         static xpath_query_impl* create()
10846         {
10847             void* memory = xml_memory::allocate(sizeof(xpath_query_impl));
10848 
10849             return new (memory) xpath_query_impl();
10850         }
10851 
10852         static void destroy(void* ptr)
10853         {
10854             if (!ptr) return;
10855             
10856             // free all allocated pages
10857             static_cast<xpath_query_impl*>(ptr)->alloc.release();
10858 
10859             // free allocator memory (with the first page)
10860             xml_memory::deallocate(ptr);
10861         }
10862 
10863         xpath_query_impl(): root(0), alloc(&block)
10864         {
10865             block.next = 0;
10866             block.capacity = sizeof(block.data);
10867         }
10868 
10869         xpath_ast_node* root;
10870         xpath_allocator alloc;
10871         xpath_memory_block block;
10872     };
10873 
10874     PUGI__FN xpath_string evaluate_string_impl(xpath_query_impl* impl, const xpath_node& n, xpath_stack_data& sd)
10875     {
10876         if (!impl) return xpath_string();
10877 
10878     #ifdef PUGIXML_NO_EXCEPTIONS
10879         if (setjmp(sd.error_handler)) return xpath_string();
10880     #endif
10881 
10882         xpath_context c(n, 1, 1);
10883 
10884         return impl->root->eval_string(c, sd.stack);
10885     }
10886 
10887     PUGI__FN impl::xpath_ast_node* evaluate_node_set_prepare(xpath_query_impl* impl)
10888     {
10889         if (!impl) return 0;
10890 
10891         if (impl->root->rettype() != xpath_type_node_set)
10892         {
10893         #ifdef PUGIXML_NO_EXCEPTIONS
10894             return 0;
10895         #else
10896             xpath_parse_result res;
10897             res.error = "Expression does not evaluate to node set";
10898 
10899             throw xpath_exception(res);
10900         #endif
10901         }
10902 
10903         return impl->root;
10904     }

10988 
10989     PUGI__FN void xpath_node_set::_assign(const_iterator begin_, const_iterator end_)
10990     {
10991         assert(begin_ <= end_);
10992 
10993         size_t size_ = static_cast<size_t>(end_ - begin_);
10994 
10995         if (size_ <= 1)
10996         {
10997             // deallocate old buffer
10998             if (_begin != &_storage) impl::xml_memory::deallocate(_begin);
10999 
11000             // use internal buffer
11001             if (begin_ != end_) _storage = *begin_;
11002 
11003             _begin = &_storage;
11004             _end = &_storage + size_;
11005         }
11006         else
11007         {
11008             // make heap copy
11009             xpath_node* storage = static_cast<xpath_node*>(impl::xml_memory::allocate(size_ * sizeof(xpath_node)));
11010 
11011             if (!storage)
11012             {
11013             #ifdef PUGIXML_NO_EXCEPTIONS
11014                 return;
11015             #else
11016                 throw std::bad_alloc();
11017             #endif
11018             }
11019 
11020             memcpy(storage, begin_, size_ * sizeof(xpath_node));
11021             
11022             // deallocate old buffer
11023             if (_begin != &_storage) impl::xml_memory::deallocate(_begin);
11024 
11025             // finalize
11026             _begin = storage;
11027             _end = storage + size_;
11028         }
11029     }
11030

11119     PUGI__FN const char_t* xpath_variable::name() const
11120     {
11121         switch (_type)
11122         {
11123         case xpath_type_node_set:
11124             return static_cast<const impl::xpath_variable_node_set*>(this)->name;
11125 
11126         case xpath_type_number:
11127             return static_cast<const impl::xpath_variable_number*>(this)->name;
11128 
11129         case xpath_type_string:
11130             return static_cast<const impl::xpath_variable_string*>(this)->name;
11131 
11132         case xpath_type_boolean:
11133             return static_cast<const impl::xpath_variable_boolean*>(this)->name;
11134 
11135         default:
11136             assert(!"Invalid variable type");
11137             return 0;
11138         }
11139     }

11183     PUGI__FN bool xpath_variable::set(const char_t* value)
11184     {
11185         if (_type != xpath_type_string) return false;
11186 
11187         impl::xpath_variable_string* var = static_cast<impl::xpath_variable_string*>(this);
11188 
11189         // duplicate string
11190         size_t size = (impl::strlength(value) + 1) * sizeof(char_t);
11191 
11192         char_t* copy = static_cast<char_t*>(impl::xml_memory::allocate(size));
11193         if (!copy) return false;
11194 
11195         memcpy(copy, value, size);
11196 
11197         // replace old string
11198         if (var->value) impl::xml_memory::deallocate(var->value);
11199         var->value = copy;
11200 
11201         return true;
11202     }

11217     PUGI__FN xpath_variable_set::~xpath_variable_set()
11218     {
11219         for (size_t i = 0; i < sizeof(_data) / sizeof(_data[0]); ++i)
11220         {
11221             xpath_variable* var = _data[i];
11222 
11223             while (var)
11224             {
11225                 xpath_variable* next = var->_next;
11226 
11227                 impl::delete_xpath_variable(var->_type, var);
11228 
11229                 var = next;
11230             }
11231         }
11232     }
11233 
11234     PUGI__FN xpath_variable* xpath_variable_set::find(const char_t* name) const
11235     {
11236         const size_t hash_size = sizeof(_data) / sizeof(_data[0]);
11237         size_t hash = impl::hash_string(name) % hash_size;
11238 
11239         // look for existing variable
11240         for (xpath_variable* var = _data[hash]; var; var = var->_next)
11241             if (impl::strequal(var->name(), name))
11242                 return var;
11243 
11244         return 0;
11245     }
11246 
11247     PUGI__FN xpath_variable* xpath_variable_set::add(const char_t* name, xpath_value_type type)
11248     {
11249         const size_t hash_size = sizeof(_data) / sizeof(_data[0]);
11250         size_t hash = impl::hash_string(name) % hash_size;
11251 
11252         // look for existing variable
11253         for (xpath_variable* var = _data[hash]; var; var = var->_next)
11254             if (impl::strequal(var->name(), name))
11255                 return var->type() == type ? var : 0;
11256 
11257         // add new variable
11258         xpath_variable* result = impl::new_xpath_variable(type, name);
11259 
11260         if (result)
11261         {
11262             result->_type = type;
11263             result->_next = _data[hash];
11264 
11265             _data[hash] = result;
11266         }
11267 
11268         return result;
11269     }

11305     PUGI__FN xpath_query::xpath_query(const char_t* query, xpath_variable_set* variables): _impl(0)
11306     {
11307         impl::xpath_query_impl* qimpl = impl::xpath_query_impl::create();
11308 
11309         if (!qimpl)
11310         {
11311         #ifdef PUGIXML_NO_EXCEPTIONS
11312             _result.error = "Out of memory";
11313         #else
11314             throw std::bad_alloc();
11315         #endif
11316         }
11317         else
11318         {
11319             impl::buffer_holder impl_holder(qimpl, impl::xpath_query_impl::destroy);
11320 
11321             qimpl->root = impl::xpath_parser::parse(query, variables, &qimpl->alloc, &_result);
11322 
11323             if (qimpl->root)
11324             {
11325                 qimpl->root->optimize(&qimpl->alloc);
11326 
11327                 _impl = static_cast<impl::xpath_query_impl*>(impl_holder.release());
11328                 _result.error = 0;
11329             }
11330         }
11331     }
11332 
11333     PUGI__FN xpath_query::~xpath_query()
11334     {
11335         impl::xpath_query_impl::destroy(_impl);
11336     }

11340         if (!_impl) return xpath_type_none;
11341

11343     }

11345     PUGI__FN bool xpath_query::evaluate_boolean(const xpath_node& n) const
11346     {
11347         if (!_impl) return false;
11348         
11349         impl::xpath_context c(n, 1, 1);
11350         impl::xpath_stack_data sd;
11351 
11352     #ifdef PUGIXML_NO_EXCEPTIONS
11353         if (setjmp(sd.error_handler)) return false;
11354     #endif
11355         
11356         return static_cast<impl::xpath_query_impl*>(_impl)->root->eval_boolean(c, sd.stack);
11357     }

11360     {
11361         if (!_impl) return impl::gen_nan();
11362         
11363         impl::xpath_context c(n, 1, 1);
11364         impl::xpath_stack_data sd;
11365 
11366     #ifdef PUGIXML_NO_EXCEPTIONS
11367         if (setjmp(sd.error_handler)) return impl::gen_nan();
11368     #endif
11369 
11370         return static_cast<impl::xpath_query_impl*>(_impl)->root->eval_number(c, sd.stack);

11374     PUGI__FN string_t xpath_query::evaluate_string(const xpath_node& n) const
11375     {
11376         impl::xpath_stack_data sd;
11377 
11378         impl::xpath_string r = impl::evaluate_string_impl(static_cast<impl::xpath_query_impl*>(_impl), n, sd);
11379 
11380         return string_t(r.c_str(), r.length());

11384     PUGI__FN size_t xpath_query::evaluate_string(char_t* buffer, size_t capacity, const xpath_node& n) const
11385     {
11386         impl::xpath_stack_data sd;
11387 
11388         impl::xpath_string r = impl::evaluate_string_impl(static_cast<impl::xpath_query_impl*>(_impl), n, sd);
11389 
11390         size_t full_size = r.length() + 1;
11391         
11392         if (capacity > 0)
11393         {
11394             size_t size = (full_size < capacity) ? full_size : capacity;
11395             assert(size > 0);
11396 
11397             memcpy(buffer, r.c_str(), (size - 1) * sizeof(char_t));
11398             buffer[size - 1] = 0;
11399         }
11400         
11401         return full_size;
11402     }

11404     PUGI__FN xpath_node_set xpath_query::evaluate_node_set(const xpath_node& n) const
11405     {
11406         impl::xpath_ast_node* root = impl::evaluate_node_set_prepare(static_cast<impl::xpath_query_impl*>(_impl));
11407         if (!root) return xpath_node_set();
11408 
11409         impl::xpath_context c(n, 1, 1);
11410         impl::xpath_stack_data sd;
11411 
11412     #ifdef PUGIXML_NO_EXCEPTIONS
11413         if (setjmp(sd.error_handler)) return xpath_node_set();
11414     #endif
11415 
11416         impl::xpath_node_set_raw r = root->eval_node_set(c, sd.stack, impl::nodeset_eval_all);
11417 
11418         return xpath_node_set(r.begin(), r.end(), r.type());
11419     }

11421     PUGI__FN xpath_node xpath_query::evaluate_node(const xpath_node& n) const
11422     {
11423         impl::xpath_ast_node* root = impl::evaluate_node_set_prepare(static_cast<impl::xpath_query_impl*>(_impl));
11424         if (!root) return xpath_node();
11425 
11426         impl::xpath_context c(n, 1, 1);
11427         impl::xpath_stack_data sd;
11428 
11429     #ifdef PUGIXML_NO_EXCEPTIONS
11430         if (setjmp(sd.error_handler)) return xpath_node();
11431     #endif
11432 
11433         impl::xpath_node_set_raw r = root->eval_node_set(c, sd.stack, impl::nodeset_eval_first);
11434 
11435         return r.first();
11436     }
